Chapter 1200 A Bunch of Old Foxes!

Chapter 1200: A Bunch of Old Foxes
!【Fourth Update】
Heavenly Emperor Palace Base.
At this moment, Migudao Ancestor, Tianfan Dao Ancestor, Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, as well as the Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor from Black Wind Mountain had also arrived here, discussing this offensive operation with the three Palace Masters of the Heavenly Emperor Palace.
“This operation can be considered a failure. We didn’t expect the Forbidden Insect Race to have hidden three Lord-level Forbidden Insects!”
The Azure Dragon Palace Master sighed.
The Eternal Dao Ancestor said, “At present, the Forbidden Insect Race possesses nine Lord-level Forbidden Insects, equivalent to nine level-9 Half-Step Domain Ancestors. And this might not even be all of them—what if there are still Lord-level ones guarding the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest?”
Previously, if the Eternal Dao Ancestor had said this, the other Dao Ancestors probably wouldn’t have cared.
They would have thought that if there really were more Lord-level Forbidden Insects, then when they attacked the nest before, all of them should have come out.
“Zero Four Seven”
But now, they felt that the Eternal Dao Ancestor’s words made some sense.
Nine Lord-level Forbidden Insects might not be the full number. There might even be a tenth, or even an eleventh Lord-level Forbidden Insect.
Shenxu Dao Ancestor suddenly spoke: “We must be prepared. Quite a few Dao Ancestors’ corpses were seized by the Forbidden Insect Race this time. It’s possible they can use those corpses to cultivate a few more Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
Moreover, we must also be mentally prepared for one thing—the birth of an Insect King!”
“An Insect King is comparable to a Domain Ancestor. How could it be so easy to be born?”
Migudao Ancestor immediately refuted.
The Azure Dragon Palace Master glanced deeply at Shenxu Dao Ancestor and the Eternal Dao Ancestor, then said, “Eternal Dao Ancestor, Shenxu Dao Ancestor, do you know something?”
The Eternal Dao Ancestor replied, “We do know a bit. I’m just afraid you won’t believe it if we say it!”
“Speak. I believe you!”
said the Azure Dragon Palace Master.
“Then I’ll say it!”
The Eternal Dao Ancestor explained: “According to the secret records of our Black Wind Mountain, inside the Forbidden Insect nest there should be a Forbidden Insect Tree. On this tree are countless cocoons. As long as there is energy, these cocoons will give birth to Forbidden Insects.
Judging by the current scale of the Forbidden Insect Race, that tree must still have at least several Lord-level cocoons, as well as one Insect King-level cocoon! As for when that… Insect King-level cocoon will hatch, I do not know.”
“If this information is true, can we enter the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest and destroy the tree along with the Insect King-level cocoon?”
Tianfan Dao Ancestor proposed.
“No!”
The Eternal Dao Ancestor shook his head. “Not to mention whether we can destroy the tree, the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest suppresses us greatly. I’m afraid we wouldn’t even be able to use a fraction of our strength. Moreover, that is the lair of the Forbidden Insect Race. Once the Lord-level Forbidden Insects engage us in battle, we would likely perish without even a chance to escape! If anyone is willing to go, I have no objection!”
Tianfan Dao Ancestor fell silent, not daring to speak further.
He did not wish to seek death, so naturally he did not dare to enter the Forbidden Insect nest.
“What should we do next? With the forces our major factions have invested in the Dark Forbidden Domain, it’s not enough to eliminate the Forbidden Insect Race. If we let them continue to accumulate, sooner or later they will destroy our bases! Moreover, we cannot keep guarding here forever. Those Dao Ancestors also need to return to cultivate and improve their strength!”
The Azure Dragon Palace Master said worriedly.
“I have a suggestion!”
Shenxu Dao Ancestor said.
The other Half-Step Domain Ancestors looked at him.
Shenxu Dao Ancestor continued: “The reason Dao Ancestors frequently return to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm is simply to sacrifice Forbidden Insects in exchange for origin rewards and cultivation boosts from the realm.
But if we publicly collect the corpses of Forbidden Insects and provide cultivation resources and benefits according to the value of each corpse, then the Dao Ancestors won’t need to leave the base. They can cultivate here and at any time go out to fight the Forbidden Insect Race without needing to return to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm!”
“That is indeed a solution!”
Several Half-Step Domain Ancestors agreed one after another.
However, this method would only ensure sufficient Dao Ancestor combat strength in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm; it did not mean they could eliminate the Forbidden Insect Race.
The eight Half-Step Domain Ancestors discussed for a long time but still failed to come up with a concrete decision on how to eliminate the Forbidden Insect Race.
In the end, they concluded the meeting and continued with their current strategy.
After the meeting ended.
Migudao Ancestor, Tianfan Dao Ancestor, and Zhenyu Dao Ancestor left the Heavenly Emperor Palace base, but they did not part ways, instead chatting in the void of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Zhenyu Dao Ancestor was the first to express dissatisfaction: “The Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain must be hiding other Half-Step Domain Ancestors. If they sent all of them out, we could easily win this battle!”
“You expect the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain to go all out? How is that possible?” This novel is first published by ‘Dragon’

Migudao Ancestor sneered: “The Heavenly Emperor Palace may not be in a hurry to eliminate the Forbidden Insect Race. They might even be using the Forbidden Insects as a means to accelerate the birth of the Forbidden Realm... Only through the continuous sacrifice of Forbidden Insects can the Xuanxu Ancient Realm grow rapidly.
If they wiped out the Forbidden Insect Race all at once, it might not necessarily lead to the birth of the Forbidden Realm. But harvesting them wave after wave like cutting leeks is undoubtedly the best method.
Black Wind Mountain’s purpose is also not pure. They too want the Forbidden Realm to be born, while also using the Forbidden Insects to temper their Dao Ancestors.
Although many Dao Ancestors will die, it can also cultivate quite a number of strong individuals.
In short, neither of these two forces truly intends to eliminate the Forbidden Insect Race!”
“But our strength is too weak. We have no way to deal with the Forbidden Insect Race. Otherwise, we would spare no cost to destroy them!”
Tianfan Dao Ancestor sighed.
The three chatted for a while..., then each went their separate ways.
Migudao Ancestor watched Tianfan Dao Ancestor and Zhenyu Dao Ancestor leave and couldn’t help but sneer inwardly: “They’re also two old foxes!”
....Because the Forbidden Insect Race suffered heavy losses this time and seized many Dao Ancestors’ corpses, they also needed time to recover and cultivate more Forbidden Insects. Therefore, for a period of time, they would not attack the major bases in the Dao Mountain Domain.
Meanwhile, the various bases announced that Forbidden Insect corpses could be exchanged for cultivation resources. Many Dao Ancestors, having only killed a single Forbidden Insect, were too lazy to return to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm and thus chose to exchange them for resources instead.
Moreover, the major bases refined the dark forbidden power of the Dark Forbidden Domain into a gentler form and infused it into the bases, transforming each base into an optimal cultivation sanctuary. As a result, many Dao Ancestors were willing to cultivate here.
Ye Tian, however, returned to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm. After all, he had obtained quite a number of Forbidden Insect corpses this time. If he sacrificed them all, he might be able to reach the true limit of the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor level in one leap.
Additionally.
He had already gained deep insight into Forbidden Dao Techniques, and this time he had a chance to comprehend a true Forbidden Dao Technique.

Chapter 1201 Breakthrough, Supreme Dao Ancestor!

Chapter 1201: Breakthrough, Supreme Dao Ancestor
!【Fifth Update】
Forbidden Void Realm.
Ye Tian entered here to cultivate, allowing him to have a thousand times more time than others.
Very quickly.
One by one, the corpses of Forbidden Insects were taken out by him and then sacrificed to the origin of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm.
Soon after, the Xuanxu Ancient Realm bestowed origin power upon him, further increasing Ye Tian’s cultivation speed by a great margin.
However, before entering seclusion, he fused the two Forbidden talents he had copied. The Forbidden talent Dark Spear became even stronger than before, but the Forbidden talent that interested Ye Tian the most was—Stealth! The Forbidden talent Stealth was extremely practical. Once activated, he could perfectly blend into the void of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
With his current strength, if he used the Forbidden talent Stealth, even Invincible Dao Ancestors or Commander-level Forbidden Insects would find it difficult to sense his existence. Only Half-Step Domain Ancestors could truly detect him.
Stealth! Ye Tian’s body disappeared, perfectly merging into the void of the Forbidden Void Realm.
Immediately after, he walked through the Forbidden Void Realm, passing by many Dao Ancestors, even passing by his wife Xiao Yue, yet she did not notice him.
“A very good ability. Entering the Dark Forbidden Domain in the future will be much safer!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Next, he began to cultivate with all his strength. In the blink of an eye, 100 years passed in the outside world, while Ye Tian cultivated for an extremely long time in the Forbidden Void Realm. His physical strength, Forbidden Dao power, and soul power had all reached the limit of the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor. If he did not break through the bottleneck, he would no longer be able to improve.
Moreover, he was on the verge of comprehending a Forbidden Dao Technique.
Ye Tian decided that once he comprehended the Forbidden Dao Technique, he would immediately attempt to break through to the Supreme Dao Ancestor realm.
In another instant, 50 more years passed in the outside world, and Ye Tian finally comprehended his own Forbidden Dao Technique in the Forbidden Void Realm.
Forbidden Void Realm.
Ye Tian stood in the empty void and waved his hand. A black spear emitting terrifying Forbidden laws appeared.
Puff! The void was pierced by the black spear, its power many times stronger than an ordinary Forbidden spear.
Containing the unique Forbidden laws of the Dao Technique itself—this was a Forbidden Dao Technique.
And without a doubt, the Dao Technique Ye Tian used was already considered a Forbidden Dao Technique, surpassing Supreme Dao Techniques. However, it could only be regarded as the lowest level of Forbidden Dao Technique. In the eyes of Half-Step Domain Ancestors, such a technique might not even qualify.
But for Ye Tian, being able to create such a Forbidden Dao Technique was already remarkable.
“If others knew that I haven’t even created a single Supreme Technique, yet I’ve created a Forbidden Dao Technique that surpasses them, they would probably be dumbfounded!”
Ye Tian said with a smile.
However, he was now also capable of creating Supreme Techniques.
, but there was no need... it wouldn’t help his strength much. Only Forbidden Dao Techniques could allow his power to surge dramatically.
For example, even though he had not yet reached the Dao Ancestor realm, his combat power already surpassed that of ordinary Supreme Dao Ancestors, enough to rival Supreme Dao Ancestors like Lantian Dao Ancestor.
Once he stepped into the ranks of Supreme Dao Ancestors, his combat power would likely soar to the level of someone like Wind King.
“This Forbidden Dao Technique was comprehended based on the Forbidden talent: Dark Spear. I’ll name it Dark Extreme Dao Spear!”
Ye Tian named it.
Next, Ye Tian planned to break through to become a Supreme Dao Ancestor.
He left the Forbidden Void Realm, returned to the human territory, and began seclusion to break into the ranks of Supreme Dao Ancestors.
Time passed day by day.
On this day.
The void of the human territory surged with winds and clouds, and strands of Great Dao laws spread, as the origin of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm descended.
At this moment.
Many Supreme Dao Ancestors from various forces turned their gaze toward the human territory.
“The human race is about to give birth to a Supreme Dao Ancestor!”
“Is it Wanfa Dao Ancestor? His cultivation speed is terrifying—he’s becoming a Supreme Dao Ancestor so quickly!”
“I heard before that Wanfa Dao Ancestor’s combat power is extremely strong, even stronger than Young Master Gui. Once he breaks into the Supreme Dao Ancestor ranks, his strength will likely far exceed that of ordinary Supreme Dao Ancestors!”
....Boom!!!! At this moment, Ye Tian had already broken through the bottleneck and advanced into the ranks of Supreme Dao Ancestors. His body was transforming into a Supreme Dao Body. His Forbidden Dao power became purer and more powerful, far surpassing before, and even his soul became more refined, engraved with Forbidden origin laws.
At this moment, Ye Tian seemed to become the embodiment of the Forbidden Dao itself, able to mobilize the Forbidden laws of heaven and earth with every move.
“Very strong, far stronger than before. Even Wind King might not be my opponent!”
Ye Tian estimated.
More importantly, he had just advanced to the Supreme Dao Ancestor level. Whether it was his Forbidden Dao power or physical strength, both could still continue to improve rapidly. Only after reaching a certain level would the progress slow down; at the beginning, the improvement was extremely fast.
In addition, his Forbidden Dao Technique, Dark Extreme Dao Spear, had only just been created and was still at an entry level, not yet cultivated to a profound stage.
Therefore, once Ye Tian focused on cultivating Dark Extreme Dao Spear, his strength would surge again.
“I have fused several Forbidden talents: Dark Spear. Cultivating this Forbidden Dao Technique, Dark Extreme Dao Spear, is countless times easier for me than for Half-Step Domain Ancestors. At most, they can raise a Forbidden Dao Technique to minor mastery, but I can easily cultivate one to major mastery, even perfection, and even the ultimate level!”
Ye Tian said confidently.
Having just advanced to Supreme Dao Ancestor, one after another Supreme Dao Ancestors came to the human race to offer congratulations.
Some of these Supreme Dao Ancestors came from Eighth Heaven forces, while others came from Ninth Heaven forces.
Ye Tian received them all. Perhaps they were enemies before, but now all major forces were cooperating, making them allies. Naturally, Ye Tian would not ignore them.
Among them, many Supreme Dao Ancestors wanted to cooperate with Ye Tian to hunt Forbidden Insects, but Ye Tian declined them one by one.
He did not want to cooperate with these Supreme Dao Ancestors—it wouldn’t be cooperation, but rather protecting them.
Moreover, he could fully cooperate with the Supreme Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain, so why cooperate with them? On this day.
Ye Tian arrived at the Time King Small Realm and met the Eternal Dao Ancestor who had just returned from the Dark Forbidden Domain. The latter had come back specifically for Ye Tian to hold a Ten Kings Conferment Ceremony for him.
That’s right, Ye Tian had become a Supreme Dao Ancestor and one of the Ten Kings! To read the version without underlines, please download Shitou Novel

Chapter 1202 Conferment, Dark King!

Chapter 1202: Conferment, Dark King
!【Second Update】
Ye Tian became one of the Ten Kings. The Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor conferred the title upon him, but very few people knew about this matter. Those Heavenly Kings and True Ancestors were completely unaware.
Only the Ten Kings, Invincible Dao Ancestors, and Half-Step Domain Ancestors were qualified to participate in the Ten Kings Conferment Ceremony.
Ye Tian was brought from the Time King Small Realm to another small realm—the Black Wind Mountain Small Realm.
Strictly speaking, this was the true Black Wind Mountain. The one outside could at most be considered the outer mountain.
In the endless dark void, Ye Tian saw a massive black mountain. This was the real Black Wind Mountain. Even though he had become a Supreme Dao Ancestor, he still had no idea where this small realm was hidden.
Soon, Ye Tian saw Wind King, Fire King, Wood King, Metal King, Ice King, and Time King. However, they did not come in person, but appeared as incarnations stationed within Black Wind Mountain.
After all, if these six kings also left the Black Wind Mountain base, it would easily attract outside attention.
Besides these six kings, Ye Tian also saw many incarnations of Invincible Dao Ancestors, one of whom he recognized—Liuhuo Dao Ancestor.
At present, only six Invincible Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain were known to the outside world, yet ten Invincible Dao Ancestors participated in this conferment ceremony, which greatly surprised Ye Tian.
Soon, he learned their titles.
Bingfeng Dao Ancestor! Zhuoying Dao Ancestor! Longhuang Dao Ancestor! Feiyu Dao Ancestor! Yuding Dao Ancestor! Jinfu Dao Ancestor! … Liuhuo Dao Ancestor! Ten Invincible Dao Ancestors participated in Ye Tian’s conferment ceremony, leaving him somewhat stunned.
However, after learning that this was the custom of Black Wind Mountain, he quickly accepted it calmly.
Above the Invincible Dao Ancestors were the two Half-Step Domain Ancestors—Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor.
The conferment ceremony was very simple. First, the token was handed over, replacing the Great Heavenly King token with a Ten Kings token.
According to past rules, if Ye Tian wanted to become one of the Ten Kings after reaching the Supreme Dao Ancestor level, he would have to withstand the attacks of one of the Ten Kings for a long time or at least not fall into a disadvantage to inherit the title.
But now, four of the Ten Kings had fallen, and the previous Ten Kings obviously could not inherit the title again, so new Supreme Dao Ancestors had to take their place.
Therefore, Ye Tian could directly become the seventh of the Ten Kings of Black Wind Mountain.
“Ye Tian, Black Wind Mountain still has the titles of Earth King, Water King, Space King, and Dark King among the Ten Kings. Which title do you choose?”
the Eternal Dao Ancestor asked.
“I choose Dark King!”
Ye Tian thought for a moment before replying.
Immediately, the Eternal Dao Ancestor handed the Dark King token to Ye Tian. After Ye Tian completed the oath, he officially became the Dark King.
Suddenly.
The Eternal Dao Ancestor pointed a finger at Ye Tian’s forehead and transmitted something.
“Soul Impervious Technique!”
This was a secret technique that permanently sealed the origin memories of the soul. Once cultivated, no one could extract even a trace of memory from his soul. This was a supreme secret technique of Black Wind Mountain, granted only to the Ten Kings.
It was precisely because of this that outsiders never knew the secrets and true strength of Black Wind Mountain. Otherwise, its secrets would have long been exposed.
Afterward.
The Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor brought Ye Tian to the Black Wind Hall of Black Wind Mountain.
Here, the Eternal Dao Ancestor personally explained some of the secrets of Black Wind Mountain to Ye Tian. After all, at the level of the Ten Kings, Ye Tian was qualified to know these matters.
....“Dark King, you are now one of the Ten Kings and are qualified to know most of the secrets. However, some secrets, to be honest, cannot even be known by Invincible Dao Ancestors, so they cannot be told to you!”
the Eternal Dao Ancestor said.
“Eternal Dao Ancestor, I understand!”
Ye Tian nodded.
Then the Eternal Dao Ancestor continued: “First, you can know the general strength of Black Wind Mountain.
At present, Black Wind Mountain has sixty-two Supreme Dao Ancestors and twenty-one Invincible Dao Ancestors. This is our true strength, and there is no concealment from you.
As for how many Half-Step Domain Ancestors there are, you are not qualified to know yet.
However, Shenxu Dao Ancestor and I are the Half-Step Domain Ancestors who frequently act outside, so members of Black Wind Mountain at the level of Ten Kings and above are aware of us!”
Ye Tian was shocked.
Sixty-two Supreme Dao Ancestors and twenty-one Invincible Dao Ancestors—this number was astonishing.
“Do you think Black Wind Mountain is very powerful?”
the Eternal Dao Ancestor asked.
“Yes!”
Ye Tian nodded.
But suddenly, the Eternal Dao Ancestor sighed: “In fact, at its peak, Black Wind Mountain had hundreds of Supreme Dao Ancestors and more than fifty Invincible Dao Ancestors. Unfortunately, during the war when the Domain Realm shattered, you have no idea how tragic it was. Black Wind Mountain was forced to participate in that battle—not only because of the threat from the Vast Sea Domain Ancestor, but also for other reasons that cannot be disclosed.
In short, far more than just a few Ten Kings died in that battle.
Those Ninth Heaven forces also suffered heavy losses, but since their battlefield was more peripheral, their losses were not as severe as ours.
Black Wind Mountain was on the main battlefield connected to the Heavenly Emperor Palace, so the Heavenly Emperor Palace roughly knows some of our strength.
In addition, while in the Dark Forbidden Domain, Black Wind Mountain also encountered extremely terrifying events, resulting in further losses.”
Then, the Eternal Dao Ancestor revealed another shocking piece of information.
“.
In fact, Black Wind Mountain is strictly divided into three branches: Wind Mountain, Black Mountain, and the true headquarters, Black Wind Mountain. Each branch has its own Mountain Lord.
The branch in the Dao Mountain Domain belongs to Wind Mountain. Unfortunately, that battle broke out too suddenly, and the other two branches were not in the Vast Sea Domain Realm at the time, so we are currently unable to contact Black Mountain and the headquarters.
The strength of the three branches is roughly similar, and the headquarters is not much stronger than us. However, we are only a part separated from the headquarters, so the main Black Wind Mountain is more orthodox.
The Heavenly Emperor Palace’s plan is… to facilitate the birth of the Forbidden Realm. We know this, but the fundamental reason we do not stop it is… because we also want to use the Forbidden Realm as a coordinate to summon Black Mountain and the headquarters!”
“Black Mountain and the headquarters are also not having an easy time in the Divine Heaven Domain. They have powerful enemies. If they can come to the Dao Mountain Domain, it would be a good thing—they could develop peacefully.
Therefore, our goal is also to promote the birth of the Forbidden Realm. As long as the Heavenly Emperor Palace does not provoke us, we will not attack them!”
After finishing, the Eternal Dao Ancestor spoke.
Ye Tian asked curiously, “Eternal Dao Ancestor, is the Mountain Lord of Wind Mountain here?”
“Yes!”
The Eternal Dao Ancestor replied: “However, you are not qualified to meet the Wind Mountain Lord yet, unless you reach the Half-Step Domain Ancestor level. Do you understand? Also, if one day you reach the Invincible Dao Ancestor level, you can send a clone into the Forbidden Insect nest to explore. You might gain some benefits. There are definitely many good things inside the Forbidden Insect nest, but unfortunately, we Half-Step Domain Ancestors do not dare to take that risk!”
“Eternal Dao Ancestor, I understand!”
Ye Tian responded.
Next, Ye Tian received the equipment belonging to the Dark King from Black Wind Mountain—or rather, from Wind Mountain—as well as a large number of resources.
What interested Ye Tian the most was that he could freely enter Wind Mountain to observe the insights of various Half-Step Domain Ancestors regarding Forbidden Dao Techniques. Those insights were engraved on Forbidden stone tablets. By studying them carefully, one could always gain some understanding, which would be very helpful for creating Forbidden Dao Techniques.

Chapter 1203 Searching for Lord-Level!

Chapter 1203: Searching for Lord-Level
!【Third Update】
Ye Tian left Black Wind Mountain and returned to the human race.
This time, he had become the Dark King of Black Wind Mountain. His status there was now on par with the Wind King. He even came to know many secrets, and all kinds of precious classics were opened to him for free.
For example, the Great Dao Techniques in the Dao Technique library—he could cultivate them all freely.
Unfortunately, he was not very interested in Great Dao Techniques, as they were of little help to his strength now.
At the level of a Supreme Dao Ancestor, the greatest benefit Black Wind Mountain could provide him was backing. Future cultivation would rely more on himself.
In addition, Ye Tian could issue orders to many Heavenly Kings and True Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain, indirectly making them work for him.
Many resources also passed through his hands for management, giving him tremendous authority.
To a certain extent, even Half-Step Domain Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors did not hold as much power as the Ten Kings, because they did not directly manage affairs. The Ten Kings were the true rulers of Black Wind Mountain on the surface.
....“It’s a pity I can no longer enter the Forbidden Void Realm to cultivate!”
After becoming a Supreme Dao Ancestor, Ye Tian faced this issue and felt somewhat regretful.
Although he could send a clone into the Forbidden Void Realm, a clone could not cultivate. Thus, the Forbidden Void Realm could now only be used for his family to cultivate and to train the human race and the Nine Extremes Legion. Its value to him personally was no longer high.
At this moment, he also understood why Ouyang Jiuer was not very interested in the Forbidden Void Realm. For an individual, its value was limited.
However, for an entire force, the value of the Forbidden Void Realm was immense.
Thinking of Ouyang Jiuer, he realized that she had not appeared for a long time.
According to what he knew, Ouyang Jiuer was currently not at the human residence, clearly having gone elsewhere. Yet she had not gone to the Dark Forbidden Domain to hunt Forbidden Insects either.
Of course, her absence did not seem strange to him.
After all, with so many Half-Step Domain Ancestors stationed at the major bases in the Dark Forbidden Domain, Ouyang Jiuer might know some of them. If her identity were exposed, it would be troublesome.
Therefore, she was likely hiding somewhere and cultivating.
Based on his understanding of her, Ouyang Jiuer had probably already entered the ranks of Supreme Dao Ancestors.
Black Wind Mountain Base.
Ye Tian returned here, this time appearing as the Dark King.
Of course, he still came with a replicated body, while his true body remained under the identity of Ye Tian.
Many Heavenly Kings of Black Wind Mountain knew that the previous Dark King had fallen. Now that a new Dark King had appeared, they speculated that some Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor had broken through to become the Dark King, or perhaps a hidden Supreme Dao Ancestor from behind the scenes had taken the position.
For a short time, Ye Tian would hardly be exposed, but as time passed.
If a Heavenly King did not appear for a long time, others would eventually guess his identity and realize that he was the Nine Extremes Heavenly King.
Of course, Black Wind Mountain was no longer very strict about keeping identities secret, so even if it was guessed, it would not matter much.
After appearing as the Dark King, Ye Tian joined the other Ten Kings of Black Wind Mountain to hunt Forbidden Insects in the Dark Forbidden Domain. Gradually, he built up a reputation, and many forces came to know that Black Wind Mountain had gained a powerful top-tier Supreme Dao Ancestor—the Dark King! On this day.
Ye Tian prepared to execute a plan: to use the Forbidden talent—Stealth—to approach Lord-level Forbidden Insects and copy their Forbidden talents. This plan was naturally very risky, but by using a replicated body, even if he were killed, it would not matter.
Once he copied multiple Forbidden talents, especially Dark Spear, it would greatly enhance his strength.
Previously, he did not dare to do this because he lacked the Forbidden talent Stealth. Even if he forced his way in, he would be intercepted by Commander-level and numerous elite Forbidden Insects, with no chance to get close to Lord-level ones.
But now that he possessed the Forbidden talent Stealth, he could easily approach Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
Within the endless darkness of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Ye Tian’s figure completely merged into the void, passing through one Forbidden Insect after another, none of which noticed him at all.
The effect of the Forbidden talent Stealth was even better than Ouyang Jiuer’s Shadowless Divine Step. The Shadowless Divine Step could only make others ignore one’s presence from a distance, but not at close range. In contrast, the Forbidden talent Stealth made one undetectable even at close range.
Not far from the Forbidden Insect nest, Ye Tian encountered his first Lord-level Forbidden Insect. Coincidentally, this one possessed a Forbidden talent he had not yet copied....
Unfortunately, it only had one Forbidden talent—Dark Spear—and did not possess Stealth.
Clearly, that previous Commander-level Forbidden Insect with two Forbidden talents was an extremely special existence among its kind.
“Copy!”
With a single thought from Ye Tian.
Suddenly.
The Lord-level Forbidden Insect looked toward Ye Tian and immediately launched an attack.
With a puff! Ye Tian’s replicated body was instantly killed without any resistance.
However, this test allowed Ye Tian to measure the effect of the Forbidden talent Stealth. At a distance, even Lord-level Forbidden Insects could not sense him, but once he got slightly closer, they could detect him.
Once a replicated body was killed, it required ten thousand years before the ability could be used again.
Thus, Ye Tian personally accelerated time by a hundred thousand times, and in just over a month, the ability to create a replicated body could be used again.
After that, Ye Tian continued sending replicated bodies to search for Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
In this way, after repeated attempts, Ye Tian finally copied the Forbidden talents of nine Lord-level Forbidden Insects—nine instances of the Forbidden talent Dark Spear and two instances of the Forbidden talent Stealth! The second Stealth talent came from another Lord-level Forbidden Insect, which surprised him greatly.
After fusing these Forbidden talents, both of his talents became significantly stronger than before.
When comprehending Dark Extreme Dao Spear, Ye Tian clearly felt that his progress was much faster than before. The effect of the Forbidden talent Stealth had also improved considerably, although it still could not deceive Half-Step Domain Ancestors and Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
Time passed, and in the blink of an eye, several years went by.
On this day.
Ye Tian prepared to infiltrate the Forbidden Insect nest once again. As long as he did not approach Lord-level Forbidden Insects, he would not be detected. Thus, after entering the nest, he could spend more time investigating the situation there instead of being quickly killed like last time.

Chapter 1204 Dark Dull Gold Vein and Forbidden Stele..

Chapter 1204: Dark Dull Gold Vein and Forbidden Stele
!【Fourth Update】
Ye Tian activated the Forbidden talent Stealth and easily passed through the patrols of the Forbidden Insect Race, approaching their nest.
Here, there were still two Lord-level Forbidden Insects guarding the nest.
Ye Tian did not approach them. Instead, he moved toward the nest from another direction, making it less likely to be detected by the Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
The passage drew closer and closer.
“I’m in!”
Ye Tian let out a breath of relief.
At this moment, he had already entered a passage of the Forbidden Insect nest and slowly flew deeper inside.
Because he was in the state of the Forbidden talent Stealth, not a single Forbidden Insect noticed his presence.
Soon, Ye Tian smoothly entered the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest.
This time, he did not approach the Forbidden Insect Tree, as there was no need. After all, he had already been there once. Even if he went again, he could only confirm whether new Lord-level Forbidden Insects had been born, which was of little significance.
Therefore, he intended to explore other areas within the nest.
The interior of the Forbidden Insect nest was vast. The first time Ye Tian came, he had gone straight to the core area and had not explored elsewhere. This time, he discovered many interesting places.
Not long after flying, Ye Tian discovered a mineral vein.
This vein seemed to be connected to a vortex, with various substances continuously flowing out from the vortex and merging into the vein.
Ye Tian landed on the vein and carefully examined its material.
“This is…”
Ye Tian formed a guess in his mind.
This vein was black-gold in color and extremely sturdy. Even he found it difficult to damage, and it was nearly impossible to refine. It also possessed a strong rebound effect, yet it perfectly integrated with Forbidden rules.
These characteristics matched a special material he knew—Dark Dull Gold! Dark Dull Gold was an excellent raw material for forging Forbidden weapons, even more suitable than Forbidden artifacts themselves.
Ordinary Forbidden artifacts or those forged from Forbidden supreme treasures, although powerful, were prone to breaking. For example, Fengyang Emperor Son’s Forbidden artifact had once been shattered by him.
However, Forbidden artifacts forged from Dark Dull Gold possessed the property of being nearly indestructible. Unless one encountered a Half-Step Domain Ancestor or Domain Ancestor far stronger than oneself, it would not be broken.
But such situations were extremely rare. If a Dao Ancestor wielding a Dark Dull Gold weapon encountered such an opponent, they would likely be killed directly, and the enemy would not even bother attacking the weapon.
In short, Dark Dull Gold was extremely valuable. In Black Wind Mountain’s resource exchange list, Dark Dull Gold existed, but it was extremely scarce—only a few grains could be exchanged, far from enough to forge a weapon. At best, a few grains could be added when forging a Forbidden weapon.
But here was an entire Dark Dull Gold vein! Ye Tian was excited, but he quickly calmed down.
“I can’t act rashly. This vein is too large. It was likely formed from excess materials after the Forbidden Insect nest refined various Forbidden treasures, accumulating here as Dark Dull Gold.
If I expose myself, I’ll be doomed—and I won’t be able to take this vein away anyway!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Therefore, he had to be extremely cautious, ensuring that when he took this vein, it would not cause any disturbance. Otherwise, he would easily be discovered within the nest.
“Let me first see if I can move this Dark Dull Gold vein!”
Ye Tian thought.
When he enveloped the vein with his power and attempted to store it in his inner world, he found that it caused the vortex to tremble, which in turn made the entire nest slightly shake.
Whoosh! Ye Tian quickly left, not daring to remain.
Not long after, a Commander-level Forbidden Insect arrived, glanced at the pile of “trash,” and, seeing nothing unusual, left.
In its view, its kind would not touch such garbage. The disturbance was probably just a minor issue with the nest.
With its low intelligence, it did not consider the possibility of an intruder.
....“That was close. I was almost discovered!”
Ye Tian muttered.
He now understood that with his current strength, he could not take away that Dark Dull Gold vein. He would have to find another way in the future.
Afterward, he explored other parts of the nest.
“Is that a fragment of a Forbidden continent?”
While flying, Ye Tian saw a black landmass floating crookedly in the void. It was extremely damaged. If not for the faint traces of structures on it, he would not have guessed that it was a fragment of a Forbidden continent.
Based on his speculation, this fragment was likely part of a shattered domain world that had fallen into the Dark Forbidden Domain, becoming a Forbidden continent, and was later dragged into the nest by the Forbidden Insects.
Ye Tian stepped onto this fragment and searched around. He indeed found a few sect ruins and some inheritances, but they were of low value and useless to him.
After some time, Ye Tian suddenly sensed an extremely powerful aura of Forbidden laws.
He immediately flew toward it and saw a stone stele.
“This is a natural Forbidden stele from the Dark Forbidden Domain!”
Ye Tian looked at the human-height stele and exclaimed inwardly.
This was different from the Forbidden steles of Black Wind Mountain. Strictly speaking, those were artificial steles, engraved with the insights of Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
But such insights were incomplete and could not compare to the naturally existing Forbidden Dao within the Dark Forbidden Domain.
For example, the fragment of a Forbidden stele that Ouyang Jiuer once gave Ye Tian was a true natural stele. Even though it was only a fragment, its value was immeasurable.
And the stele before him was even more precious. It was a complete Forbidden stele, containing a full Forbidden Dao. The power of the Dao within it was immense—so valuable that even Half-Step Domain Ancestors would fight over it.
What excited Ye Tian even more was that this stele had been discarded here by the Forbidden Insects, surrounded by piles of waste.
Clearly, the Forbidden Insects had plundered it from the Dark Forbidden Domain and brought it back, only to find that it had no use in nurturing their kind and contained no usable energy. Thus, they threw it away as trash.
After all, the Forbidden Insect Race did not cultivate or comprehend the Forbidden Dao, so they did not understand its value.
“It’s not connected to the nest. I can take it!”
Ye Tian stepped forward, waved his hand, and stored the Forbidden stele into his inner world.

Chapter 1205 Found Jiuer!

Chapter 1205: Found Jiuer
！【Fifth Update】
After taking the Forbidden stele, Ye Tian did not linger there and quickly left, nor did he plan to continue investigating.
After all, if he were to fall, it would not matter much if this replicated body died, but the Forbidden stele would be lost! So he had to get out first and deliver the Forbidden stele to his true body. Only then would he truly feel at ease.
Ye Tian returned the way he came. Along the way, he encountered no accidents and safely flew out through the same passage he had used to enter.
Silently and without drawing the attention of any Forbidden Insects.
Only after Ye Tian flew out of the Forbidden Insect nest and kept moving farther away from that area did he truly breathe a sigh of relief.
“I’m back!”
Ye Tian stepped onto the ground of the Black Wind Mountain base, feeling extremely pleased.
At this moment, Ye Tian was no longer using the Forbidden talent Stealth, “Zero Four Seven”
because he was afraid of drawing the attention of the two Half-Step Domain Ancestors. For the time being, he did not want to expose this Forbidden talent of his.
Ye Tian casually used an invisibility secret technique and arrived at his residence, transferring the Forbidden stele into the hands of his true body.
“Not bad, I’ve obtained the Forbidden stele. With this Forbidden stele, it will be much easier for me to comprehend the Forbidden Dao in the future.
At present, my comprehension of the Endless Forbidden Dao is still far too shallow. I estimate I haven’t even reached the beginner level—I’ve only just initially grasped the complete Forbidden Dao.
If one-tenth of the Endless Forbidden Dao is considered beginner level, then I currently seem to have only grasped 0.
of the Endless Forbidden Dao!”
Ye Tian muttered.
Immediately afterward, Ye Tian sent the replicated body away to continue acting under the identity of the Dark King.
After that.
Ye Tian’s avatar that remained with the human race entered Wind Mountain to search for information about the Dark Dull Gold vein. Unfortunately, there was too little information on the subject, and there was nothing at all about Dark Dull Gold being connected to a Forbidden Insect nest.
Helpless, he could only give up.
Of course, he could also go ask Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor for relevant information and report the existence of the Dark Dull Gold vein, but in that case, he could not guarantee whether Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor might harbor selfish intentions.
After all, the value of that Dark Dull Gold vein was simply too great. Even if Eternal Dao Ancestor had no particularly bad intentions and had a way to take the Dark Dull Gold, he probably would not give Ye Tian very much of it.
People were selfish! Ye Tian was no exception. He had no desire to share too much of the Dark Dull Gold with Eternal Dao Ancestor and the others, so he did not ask them.
More importantly, Ye Tian had another person who was even more suitable to ask.
“Ouyang Jiuer!”
Ouyang Jiuer had once also been a Half-Step Domain Ancestor. She was highly knowledgeable and had an extraordinary background, so she should very well know something about Dark Dull Gold veins and might even have a way to take the Dark Dull Gold vein away.
Given the relationship between him and Ouyang Jiuer, he believed she definitely would not cheat him.
Previously, Ye Tian had not contacted Ouyang Jiuer for fear of disturbing her.
But this time, he had no choice and could only send her a message.
Ye Tian’s avatar sent a message within human territory, but it failed to reach her.
“Could Ouyang Jiuer be in the Dark Forbidden Domain?”
Ye Tian guessed.
If she were in the Dark Forbidden Domain, ordinary communication treasures would be useless. Special Forbidden communicators were needed, but if Ouyang Jiuer was really at one of the bases in the Dark Forbidden Domain, Ye Tian did not have her Forbidden communicator and had no way to contact her.
However, Ye Tian still had a method.
He used his Copy Talent to investigate one base after another. With the ability of his Copy Talent, even if someone were cultivating in seclusion inside a secret chamber behind layers of formations, he could still easily probe their talents.
Therefore, as long as Ouyang Jiuer was staying at one of the bases, he would be able to find her.
Whoosh! Ye Tian’s Copy Talent covered the Black Wind Mountain base, but he did not find her there. This was normal, since Black Wind Mountain base was basically full of Black Wind Mountain Dao Ancestors, and Ouyang Jiuer naturally would not come there.
Then.
Ye Tian went to the other bases under the pretext of paying visits, thus not arousing suspicion from the other bases.
He visited one base after another, yet still did not find any trace of Ouyang Jiuer.
On this day.
Ye Tian arrived at one of the independent cultivator bases, Nine Rivers Base, a base established by Nine Rivers Dao Ancestor, one of the Invincible Dao Ancestors among the independent cultivators. There were quite a few Dao Ancestors stationed there, though their overall level was not especially high.
After arriving at the base, Ye Tian used his Copy Talent to cover the entire area.
“Eh, I found her!”
Ye Tian said in surprise.
....Nine Rivers Base, a certain residence.
Ye Tian arrived there and sent his voice inside, asking to visit the master of the residence... Very soon, a dark-faced burly man came out, and the aura on him was unmistakably that of a Supreme Dao Ancestor.
Seeing this dark-faced burly man, Ye Tian smiled and transmitted his voice: “Jiuer, have you been well lately?”
The dark-faced burly man widened his eyes and said in disbelief, “Big Brother Ye, even after I became like this, you still recognized me?”
Then the dark-faced burly man invited Ye Tian into the residence.
Whoosh! The dark-faced burly man removed the disguise and turned into a woman. It was indeed Ouyang Jiuer.
“Big Brother Ye, did you put some kind of tracking mark on me? What I used was a supreme secret treasure, one of the supreme treasures from my previous life. Even Invincible Dao Ancestors and Half-Step Domain Ancestors shouldn’t be able to see through my disguise!”
Ouyang Jiuer asked curiously.
Ye Tian coughed lightly and explained, “I have a talent. This talent is a Forbidden talent, and it can ignore all disguises!”
“A Forbidden talent!!!”
Ouyang Jiuer was astonished.
She believed him, because only a Forbidden talent could be that heaven-defying.
At once, she became envious of Ye Tian’s Forbidden talent.
“Big Brother Ye, what do you need from me?”
Ouyang Jiuer asked curiously.
She knew Ye Tian would not come looking for her without reason, especially after searching everywhere before finally finding her at Nine Rivers Base.
“I discovered a Dark Dull Gold vein!”
Ye Tian said solemnly.
“Really?”
Ouyang Jiuer’s eyes widened again.
“Really!”
Ye Tian said firmly: “And the vein is very large, worth 2.
2—its value is beyond estimation!”
“You can’t take it away, so that’s why you came to me, right?”
Ouyang Jiuer rolled her eyes and said.
“Exactly!”
Ye Tian hurriedly said: “Just tell me—will you help or not? If it succeeds, I’ll give you half the vein. How about it?”
“I’m in!”
Ouyang Jiuer nodded.
Half a vein of Dark Dull Gold—what kind of value was that? She only needed to help a little and could get it. This was practically a gift! “Where is the vein? Why can’t it be taken away? Tell me the details.”
Ouyang Jiuer said.
“The Dark Dull Gold vein is inside the Forbidden Insect nest....”
Before Ye Tian could finish, Ouyang Jiuer hurriedly said, “Big Brother Ye, I think keeping my life is more important. I’m not going to help retrieve that vein!”

Chapter 1206 Tai’e Crow Blood!

Chapter 1206: Tai’e Crow Blood
！【First Update】
Ouyang Jiuer refused too quickly, leaving Ye Tian stunned.
Soon, he reacted.
Even Half-Step Domain Ancestors did not dare to enter the Forbidden Insect nest. Ouyang Jiuer was not even a Half-Step Domain Ancestor yet—she was only a Supreme Dao Ancestor. Entering the nest would be courting death. So even if there were the most precious treasures inside, she would not dare go in! “Jiuer, hear me out!”
Ye Tian said helplessly: “I’ve been inside the Forbidden Insect nest before and came out safely, so don’t worry—I have a high chance of preserving my life!”
“You’ve been inside?”
Ouyang Jiuer found it hard to believe.
Then Ye Tian explained how his clone had entered the nest and told her about the Dark Dull Gold vein he had seen.
When Ye Tian mentioned that he possessed the Forbidden talent Stealth, Ouyang Jiuer’s eyes widened again in disbelief.
“Big Brother Ye, don’t you think you have a bit too many Forbidden talents? And before, it didn’t seem like you had this one!”
Ouyang Jiuer said suspiciously.
Previously, she had guided Ye Tian with the Heavenly Illusion Divine Step, and Ye Tian himself had been quite weak in concealment techniques, far inferior to her.
If he had already possessed the Forbidden talent Stealth back then, then he must have been hiding it from her.
Thinking of this, Ouyang Jiuer stared at Ye Tian, waiting for an explanation.
Ye Tian quickly said: “My body is rather special. Every time I break through a realm, I awaken a new talent, so I have many, many talents!”
He felt this explanation should be enough to fool her.
“Could it be that you’re a Child of Forbidden?”
Ouyang Jiuer exclaimed in shock.
“What is a Child of Forbidden?”
Ye Tian asked curiously.
Ouyang Jiuer explained: “The so-called Child of Forbidden is our term for a type of person who possesses immense fortune, like a favored child of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Moreover, every time such a person breaks through a realm, there is a chance their soul mutates, granting them new talents. For ordinary people, their talents are basically fixed from birth. Only certain treasures can increase talents, and even then, the added talents are usually mediocre. Being able to obtain a Dao-level innate talent is already considered the peak.
But a Child of Forbidden can naturally give birth to Dao-level innate talents without relying on treasures—and even Forbidden talents! However, Children of Forbidden are only legends even in the Divine Heaven Domain. And you don’t quite match the description. According to the legends, a Child of Forbidden is born with a Forbidden body, causing terrifying phenomena at birth and even altering the Forbidden laws of heaven and earth. But you were originally just a being from an ordinary universe!”
Ye Tian didn’t expect his casual excuse to be linked to something like the Child of Forbidden, so he immediately said: “Jiuer, the Dark Forbidden Domain is vast, and there are countless realms. It’s normal for some unknown special physiques to exist.
Let’s talk about the Dark Dull Gold instead—what should we do now?”
Ouyang Jiuer did not dwell further on Ye Tian’s physique. After thinking for a moment, she said: “Big Brother Ye, the Dark Dull Gold vein is indeed formed from the residue of Forbidden artifacts refined by the Forbidden Insect Race. To them, it’s garbage; to us, it’s a treasure.
To move the Dark Dull Gold vein, it will inevitably disturb the discharge outlet of the Forbidden Insect nest.
Once you tamper with the vein, it’s equivalent to affecting that outlet, and the nest will naturally react.
If you want to take the vein without causing any disturbance, you must sever the connection between the outlet and the vein!”
“How do we sever that connection?”
This was Ye Tian’s biggest problem.
“Make the nest itself sever the connection!”
Ouyang Jiuer said: “You can think of the Dark Dull Gold vein as something inside a living organism. Right now, it’s connected—neither beneficial nor harmful.
But if it becomes harmful to the nest, the organism will no longer want to stay connected to it!”
“How do we do that?”
Ye Tian understood the theory but not the method.
“Do you know what Forbidden Insects fear the most?”
Ouyang Jiuer asked.
“No idea!”
Ye Tian shook his head.
He really didn’t know. In his impression, Forbidden Insects seemed fearless and capable of devouring anything.
“Insects fear birds. Ordinary birds don’t scare Forbidden Insects, but they do fear Forbidden bird-type creatures! I happen to have a drop of blood from a Forbidden creature—the Tai’e Crow. This drop doesn’t contain much power anymore, but it is extremely valuable.
Of course, compared to Dark Dull Gold, it’s not as valuable.
And if we successfully take the Dark Dull Gold, I can even refine a bit more Tai’e Crow blood from the vein afterward.”
Ouyang Jiuer said.
“So you’ll enter the Forbidden Insect nest?”
Ye Tian asked.
“Of course not!”
Ouyang Jiuer rolled her eyes. “Your clone can die as many times as you want—I don’t want to die! Even if your Forbidden talent is powerful, if you’re discovered by a Lord-level Forbidden Insect, it’s over!”
Then, Ouyang Jiuer handed Ye Tian a sealed sphere containing the Tai’e Crow blood, clearly reluctant to part with it.
“Big Brother Ye, be careful. It doesn’t matter if your clone dies, but don’t lose this drop of Tai’e Crow blood!”
she warned.
“Don’t worry!”
Ye Tian assured her.
After taking the Tai’e Crow blood, Ye Tian left Nine Rivers Base.
Soon, he sent a replicated body carrying the Tai’e Crow blood, activated the Forbidden talent Stealth, and headed toward the Forbidden Insect nest.
Before long, Ye Tian arrived once again at the nest and carefully entered through a passage.
This time, everything went smoothly. He passed close to several groups of Forbidden Insects but did not encounter any Lord-level ones, so he was not discovered.
Finally, Ye Tian arrived once again at the location of the Dark Dull Gold vein.
“Now let’s see whether this drop of Tai’e Crow blood works!”
Ye Tian muttered.
He crushed the sealed sphere, and a drop of Tai’e Crow blood fell into the Dark Dull Gold vein.
Though it was just a single drop, once it entered the vein, it quickly dyed the black Dark Dull Gold vein blood-red. Threads of blood-colored laws spread out, affecting the vortex above the vein.
Suddenly.
The vortex trembled, seemingly displeased with this aura. It wasn’t fear—after all, it was only a single drop of blood—but it clearly rejected it.
Crack! A faint sound of rupture echoed, and the vortex actually severed its connection with the Dark Dull Gold vein, as if it found the vein repulsive.
“Collect!”
Seizing the moment, Ye Tian quickly stored the Dark Dull Gold vein into his inner world.

Chapter 1207 Top-Tier Forbidden Weapon!

Chapter 1207: Top-Tier Forbidden Weapon
！【Second Update】
“Hurry and leave!”
Ye Tian had no intention of staying here any longer. Using Tai’e Crow blood to make that vortex sever the connection on its own would inevitably have caused a disturbance in the Forbidden Insect nest, and those Forbidden Insects would surely become aware of the anomaly here.
So, Forbidden Insects would arrive here very soon.
Moreover, there were intelligent beings among the Forbidden Insects. If they discovered that the Dark Dull Gold vein had vanished, they might realize that an outsider had infiltrated the nest. After all, the Forbidden Insects themselves would never take away the Dark Dull Gold vein, so it could only have been an outsider.
Therefore, the time left to him was very limited, and he had to leave this place as quickly as possible.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!! Ye Tian moved rapidly and darted through the area. Fortunately, with the concealment effect of the Forbidden talent Stealth, he was not discovered by the Forbidden Insects he passed along the way.
Soon, a squad of Forbidden Insects arrived at the place where the Dark Dull Gold vein had disappeared.
When they saw that this pile of “garbage,” the Dark Dull Gold vein, had vanished, they were very puzzled. But with their lack of intelligence, they merely reported the situation to the Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
Very soon, the intelligent Forbidden Insects learned of the situation and immediately ordered a search for the intruder.
The Lord-level Forbidden Insects inside the nest also mobilized and began searching for the enemy.
At this moment.
Ye Tian had already reached the passage of the Forbidden Insect nest and was flying through it at top speed.
In a short while, he arrived outside the nest, and without stopping for even a moment, he immediately fled into the distance.
Not long after Ye Tian left, the two Lord-level Forbidden Insects stationed outside the nest began probing the area around the nest, and their search range kept expanding into the surrounding territory.
From afar, Ye Tian sensed the violent aura of those two Lord-level Forbidden Insects and knew that the Forbidden Insects had realized an enemy had infiltrated. They were likely investigating at this moment, so he felt fortunate that he had moved quickly enough. Otherwise, he might not have escaped successfully.
....The rest of the journey was comparatively safe. With no Lord-level Forbidden Insects present, the other Forbidden Insects simply could not detect him.
He even saw several Forbidden Insects on the way back toward the base and casually killed them.
Nine Rivers Base.
Ye Tian arrived here and entered Ouyang Jiuer’s residence.
“Big Brother Ye, how did it go? Did you succeed?”
Ouyang Jiuer asked eagerly.
“Succeeded!”
Ye Tian projected a corner of his inner world, and the Dark Dull Gold vein appeared before them.
“It really is a Dark Dull Gold vein!”
Ouyang Jiuer recognized it at a glance and said excitedly.
However, the Dark Dull Gold vein was currently stained with Tai’e Crow blood, and that had to be separated out.
Ouyang Jiuer and Ye Tian busied themselves for a long time before finally extracting the blood, though some Tai’e Crow blood was inevitably wasted in the process.
The Dark Dull Gold vein was extremely sturdy and very difficult to refine. Ye Tian used his Forbidden weapon—the Sky-Slaying Spear—and empowered it with the Forbidden talent: Dark Spear, cutting the Dark Dull Gold vein bit by bit. After cutting for a long time, he finally split the Dark Dull Gold vein into two parts.
One part was given to Ouyang Jiuer, while he kept the other part for himself.
Ouyang Jiuer put away her share of the Dark Dull Gold vein, then casually gave Ye Tian an inheritance of a Forbidden weapon forging method.
“This is a top-tier Forbidden weapon forging method. It is extremely precious. Without a top-tier Forbidden weapon forging method, the Forbidden weapon you forge will be very difficult to raise to the top-tier level. At best, you’ll only be able to forge a high-grade Forbidden weapon!”
Ouyang Jiuer said.
“Many thanks!”
Ye Tian said.
Afterward, Ye Tian returned to the Black Wind Mountain base and began studying how to forge Forbidden weapons.
First, he carefully comprehended and studied that top-tier Forbidden weapon forging method, namely the Black Heaven Refining Art.
After fully comprehending it, Ye Tian began separating out a bit of Dark Dull Gold and started integrating it into his Sky-Slaying Spear.
The Sky-Slaying Spear was a mid-grade Forbidden weapon, not too far from becoming a high-grade Forbidden weapon, but for the current Ye Tian, such a weapon was no longer enough.
This time, having obtained so much Dark Dull Gold, he could finally forge an even higher-grade Forbidden weapon.
In an environment of accelerated time, Ye Tian tempered his Sky-Slaying Spear day after day. As more and more Dark Dull Gold was added, together with the Black Heaven Refining Art he had mastered, the spear’s sharpness and Forbidden laws gradually became more and more powerful.
On this day.
Ye Tian’s Sky-Slaying Spear finally completed its advancement and became a high-grade Forbidden weapon, far more powerful than before.
But Ye Tian continued integrating Dark Dull Gold. After all... he simply did not care about Dark Dull Gold, nor did he care about wasting it. If it were anyone else, even a Half-Step Domain Ancestor would feel heartbroken and would never dare consume Dark Dull Gold so casually.
As a large amount of Dark Dull Gold was expended, the Sky-Slaying Spear completed another advancement and reached the level of a top-tier Forbidden weapon.
“Not bad. The Sky-Slaying Spear is now more than dozens of times sharper than before!”
Ye Tian said excitedly.
With such a Forbidden weapon, his strength had become much greater than before.
Of course, Ye Tian was not satisfied with just one top-tier Forbidden weapon. After all... he had more Dark Dull Gold than he could ever use, so he could completely forge several more top-tier Forbidden weapons.
He did not forge any more offensive Forbidden weapons. Instead, he planned to forge a defensive armor set, one that covered the entire body.
Under normal circumstances, no one would forge full-body defensive armor, because it was far too wasteful of materials. But Ye Tian was not afraid of waste.
After spending more time, Ye Tian used quite a bit of Dark Dull Gold to forge a full suit of armor, naming it the Indestructible Dull Armor! “.
Yue’er, Xingchen, Xingyue, Xiao Yu, and the others also need Forbidden weapons. Giving them top-tier offensive Forbidden weapons is not a good idea. They fight often, and once such weapons are exposed, they would easily become targets.
However, if I give them defensive armor, then in a life-or-death situation, they can activate the top-tier defensive armor and preserve their lives!”
Thus, Ye Tian forged four sets of top-tier Forbidden weapon-grade defensive armor for Xiao Yue, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and Ye Yu.
When Xiao Yue, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and Ye Yu came before Ye Tian and looked at the four sets of Forbidden armor, they were all stunned: .
They were all Dao Ancestors, so naturally they understood the value of top-tier Forbidden weapons. Even Invincible Dao Ancestors did not possess them. At present, only Half-Step Domain Ancestors had top-tier Forbidden weapons, and not even such full-body defensive armor! Such Forbidden weapons were simply too extravagant! When Ye Tian told them that he had obtained a great deal of Dark Dull Gold and explained its uses, the four of them immediately understood.
Then, they accepted the defensive armor with peace of mind and promised not to reveal it casually. Unless absolutely necessary, they would never use it.
Ye Tian also distributed a bit of Dark Dull Gold to them, allowing them to upgrade their own offensive Forbidden weapons. At the very least, raising them to mid-grade Forbidden weapons would pose no problem, and for their current level, that was entirely sufficient.
If in the future they wanted to continue upgrading their Forbidden weapons, they could come to Ye Tian and receive more Dark Dull Gold. That would be much safer.

Chapter 1208 Rapid Improvement!

Chapter 1208: Rapid Improvement
！【Third Update】
Year after year passed. Ye Tian spent his time hunting Forbidden Insects and cultivating, and his cultivation grew higher and higher. His physical strength, Forbidden Dao power, and soul power also became increasingly stronger.
In the blink of an eye, 300 years had passed.
During these 300 years, a great number of Dao Ancestors had fallen, but a great number had also risen. There were even six newly advanced Invincible Dao Ancestors, one of whom was Wind King.
Wind King had accumulated strength over time and, by sacrificing a large number of Forbidden Insect corpses in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, broke through his bottleneck in one stroke and advanced to become an Invincible Dao Ancestor. His power instantly far surpassed what it had once been.
In addition, there were also many newly advanced Dao Ancestors, so the number of Dao Ancestors at the major bases did not decrease and remained almost stable.
The only thing that left the Dao Ancestors helpless was that the Forbidden Insects reproduced far too quickly. They had killed nearly ten million Forbidden Insects, already equivalent to the original total number of the Forbidden Insect Race, yet the Forbidden Insects still numbered more than ten million, as if they could never be exterminated.
Moreover, the number of Commander-level Forbidden Insects had recovered to over fifty, though the number of Lord-level Forbidden Insects had not increased further.
But for the major bases, pressure and opportunity existed in equal measure.
In just these short 300 years, the improvement of the Dao Ancestors was greater than in the previous 300,000 years, so for the strong, the Dark Forbidden Domain was indeed an excellent place for tempering themselves.
And because the Xuanxu Ancient Realm had received sacrifices of a huge number of Forbidden Insects, although it had bestowed some origin power upon many Dao Ancestors, its own origin power was still expanding, becoming at least several times stronger than before.
One had to know that it was extremely, extremely difficult for an ancient realm to grow, usually requiring a vast amount of time. Yet in just a few thousand years, it had grown several times stronger. Such a growth rate was terrifying.
At this rate of growth, the Xuanxu Ancient Realm likely would not take long before advancing into a Supreme Ancient Realm.
....On this day.
Ye Xingchen sent news that made Ye Tian extremely excited.
“Xingchen actually broke through to the Supreme Dao Ancestor level!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Moreover, he knew his son’s cultivation situation very well—Ye Xingchen had only chosen to break through after reaching his current ultimate limit.
However, Ye Xingchen had not comprehended a Forbidden Dao Technique. Instead, he had comprehended a Supreme Dao Technique, which was already an extraordinary achievement.
Ye Tian did not place excessive demands on Ye Xingchen. After all, Ye Xingchen did not possess a Forbidden talent, and for him, comprehending a Forbidden Dao Technique at the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor level was simply too difficult! Even so, once Ye Xingchen broke through to become a Supreme Dao Ancestor, he still surpassed ordinary Supreme Dao Ancestors and was enough to rival a Supreme Dao Ancestor like Fire King.
And soon after Ye Xingchen became a Supreme Dao Ancestor, he also became one of the Ten Kings of Black Wind Mountain, taking over the title of Earth King.
As for Xiao Yue, Ye Yu, and Ye Xingyue, they had already become Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors at the absolute peak, and all of them possessed formidable combat power.
Ye Tian’s own improvement had also been considerable. His Forbidden Dao, physical strength, and soul power were all far greater now than when he had first broken through to become a Supreme Dao Ancestor. This was all the result of his cultivation using a large quantity of Forbidden artifacts and certain treasures from Black Wind Mountain.
By Ye Tian’s estimation, if he now fought a Supreme Dao Ancestor like Fire King, he could probably severely injure him in a single move and kill him within a few moves. Even when facing a weaker Invincible Dao Ancestor, he could still contend with them for a while.... ....Even if he could not defeat them, they should not dream of killing him either.
What made Ye Tian happiest was the development of the human race. For example, Ye Tian’s Nine Extremes Legion had been continuously cultivating in the Forbidden Void Realm and had improved enormously. After all, the Forbidden Void Realm possessed a thousandfold time flow, giving them a thousand times more cultivation time than others.
In addition, over the years, Ye Tian had constantly distributed some Forbidden artifacts that he himself could not use, and occasionally even granted Forbidden Insects to the members of the Nine Extremes Legion so they could offer sacrifices.
By now, all several hundred thousand members of the Nine Extremes Legion were above the True Ancestor level. Among them, there were already ten Invincible True Ancestors, over ten thousand Supreme True Ancestors, and nearly all the rest were Elite True Ancestors.
As for the Dao Ancestor level, the Nine Extremes Legion now also had several hundred members, and almost all of them were above the Third Heaven Dao Ancestor level. The strongest among them had already cultivated to the Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestor level.
This was the current state of the Nine Extremes Legion! The number of Dao Ancestors in the human race as a whole was even greater, already reaching several thousand, more than the number possessed by those mid-tier Sixth Heaven forces, and even somewhat more than some Seventh Heaven forces.
However, Ye Tian had not invested much in the other human Dao Ancestors, so their rate of improvement was not very fast. Most of them remained at the Second Heaven or Third Heaven Dao Ancestor level.
On this day.
While Ye Tian was hunting Forbidden Insects in the Dark Forbidden Domain, he suddenly received a transmission.
“A medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm has been born in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm!!!”
After hearing this news, Ye Tian immediately returned to the Black Wind Mountain base.
Black Wind Mountain Base.
Ye Tian, Ye Xingchen, Fire King, Ice King, Time King, and Wood King all took their seats. Wind King, who had already become an Invincible Dao Ancestor and was now known as Xuanfeng Dao Ancestor, also participated in this meeting alongside Liuhuo Dao Ancestor and the other Invincible Dao Ancestors.
The meeting was presided over by the Half-Step Domain Ancestors Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor.
At the meeting, Eternal Dao Ancestor said, “I imagine you have all already received the news. The Xuanxu Ancient Realm has indeed given birth to a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm. The value of a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm far exceeds that of a small Forbidden Void Realm.
Once a force obtains a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, Supreme Dao Ancestors, Invincible Dao Ancestors, and even Half-Step Domain Ancestors can cultivate within it. Although it no longer provides the effect of accelerated time flow, the cultivation environment within a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm is simply too good. Moreover, once a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm is brought under control, it is almost impossible to destroy. Therefore, any force that controls one is almost impossible to exterminate.
Therefore, all major forces will compete for this medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm.”
Shenxu Dao Ancestor added, “Because of the matter of the Forbidden Insect Race, we Half-Step Domain Ancestors are not allowed to participate in the struggle for the Forbidden Void Realm. Otherwise, it would be too easy for the Forbidden Insects to seize the opportunity to attack the major bases or even invade the Dao Mountain Domain.
In addition, the Invincible Dao Ancestors must also remain to counter the Commander-level Forbidden Insects and may not leave either.
I hope that none of you Invincible Dao Ancestors go there on your own.
We Half-Step Domain Ancestors have already discussed this. If any Invincible Dao Ancestors privately break into that Forbidden Void Realm, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors will join forces to kill them! In short, only Supreme Dao Ancestors are allowed to compete. Whichever force has the ability to seize the Forbidden Void Realm, it shall belong to that force!”
When the Invincible Dao Ancestors heard that they were not permitted to compete, each of them felt rather disappointed. After all, even if they could not seize the Forbidden Void Realm itself, they could still seize a large number of Forbidden artifacts and perhaps even Forbidden supreme treasures.
Forbidden supreme treasures were also incomparably precious to them.
However, since the Half-Step Domain Ancestors had spoken so firmly, they did not dare to disobey and could only agree one by one.

Chapter 1209 One Ancient Supreme Dao Ancestor After Another!

Chapter 1209: One Ancient Supreme Dao Ancestor After Another
！
Black Wind Mountain’s meeting ended very quickly. This time, Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor placed Ye Tian in command and sent him to that medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, striving to seize it.
And the number of Supreme Dao Ancestors under Ye Tian’s command amounted to more than a hundred, which showed that Black Wind Mountain was also determined to obtain the Forbidden Void Realm.
At the same time, the three major Ninth Heaven forces and the Heavenly Emperor Palace also dispatched quite a few Supreme Dao Ancestors to that medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm.
In terms of the number of Supreme Dao Ancestors, Black Wind Mountain far surpassed the three major Ninth Heaven forces, and Black Wind Mountain’s Supreme Dao Ancestors were all quite powerful. Only a few Supreme Dao Ancestors subordinate to Invincible Dao Ancestors or Half-Step Domain Ancestors were somewhat weaker. The others were former Ten Kings from previous generations, each one powerful enough to rival top-tier Supreme Dao Ancestors.
But Ye Tian also knew very clearly that this time the hidden Supreme Dao Ancestors of the major forces would probably also appear. For example, Black Wind Mountain had mobilized over a hundred Supreme Dao Ancestors, yet Wind Mountain base itself did not even have that many. In truth, the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain had the power to eradicate the Forbidden Insect Race, but they had not exerted themselves fully because the current threat posed by the Forbidden Insect Race was not too great, and they needed to use the Forbidden Insect Race to strengthen the Xuanxu Ancient Realm.
This was equivalent to raising poisonous insects in a gu jar! That was why they had chosen to wage a drawn-out war against the Forbidden Insect Race while concealing their strength.
But a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm was different. That was a true great opportunity, enough to allow a force to develop at a tremendous pace, so naturally they would do everything they could to seize control of the Forbidden Void Realm.
Therefore, this time they would probably fight one another, and the alliance would temporarily fall apart.
However, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors were also worried that if the Invincible Dao Ancestors joined, too many Invincible Dao Ancestors might fall, which would affect the final plan. That was why only Supreme Dao Ancestors were allowed to participate.
This was good news for Ye Tian. Hardly anyone truly knew the extent of his strength. Others only knew that he had entered the ranks of Supreme Dao Ancestors, but he had never revealed his Forbidden Dao Techniques in front of others, and he had always held back in battle.
But this time, in order to compete for that medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, he would have to display his true strength.
Before leaving, Ye Tian contacted Ouyang Jiuer and asked whether she had any interest in seizing that medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, but Ouyang Jiuer refused.
In Ouyang Jiuer’s words, her identity was somewhat special, and among Supreme Dao Ancestors there were some incomparably ancient existences who might recognize her. Once battle broke out, she might accidentally expose her identity.
Although Ouyang Jiuer was walking a path different from her previous life, there were still many shared aspects, and she also possessed some unique Forbidden Dao Techniques that no one else would know. After all, everyone’s Forbidden Dao Techniques were self-comprehended. Once she used them, it would be easy for her identity to be exposed.
Therefore, Ouyang Jiuer did not intend to go.
But Ouyang Jiuer did lend Ye Tian a treasure, namely the World-Suppressing Stele.
Back then, Ouyang Jiuer had used the World-Suppressing Stele to refine a small Forbidden Void Realm, and along the way had even tricked Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace.
The World-Suppressing Stele could also be used to refine a Forbidden Void Realm, but the laws of a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm were incomparably complete, making it very difficult to find loopholes. Therefore, silently refining a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm was impossible.
But if one used the World-Suppressing Stele to refine a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, the efficiency would increase many times over, the speed would be much faster, and the success rate would be far higher.
Without the World-Suppressing Stele, refining a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm would be far too difficult. It would even require a large number of Supreme Dao Ancestors to hold off the other Supreme Dao Ancestors, piling up lives, just for there to be hope of refining the Forbidden Void Realm.
....Xuanxu Ancient Realm.
The medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm gradually stabilized, and one Supreme Dao Ancestor after another arrived here. This made many Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestors and Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors who had originally been observing the area feel very nervous, because they too wanted to enter the medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm in search of Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures.
But judging from the current situation, with Supreme Dao Ancestors descending one after another, the fighting would likely be extremely brutal, and their chances of falling were simply too high.
Thus, many weaker Dao Ancestors departed one after another, leaving behind only a small number of Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors willing to take the risk. After all, with one great harvest, they too could enter the ranks of Supreme Dao Ancestors.
Whoosh!!!! A group wearing black battle robes and masks descended.
Everyone recognized them at once—these were the Supreme Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain, and the one leading them was one of Black Wind Mountain’s Ten Kings, Dark King—Ye Tian.
Ye Tian’s gaze was mainly directed toward four areas: the Heavenly Emperor Palace, Mitian Sect, Tianhai Sect, and Myriad Domain Divine Hall. He found that he saw many Supreme Dao Ancestors who had never appeared before.
Fire King stood beside Ye Tian and transmitted his voice: “Dark King, you need to pay attention to the following Supreme Dao Ancestors. Over at the Heavenly Emperor Palace, the Dao Ancestor with long red hair is called Yan Ancestor. He is an incomparably ancient Supreme Dao Ancestor. Rumor has it that the reason he has never advanced to the Invincible Dao Ancestor level is not because his talent or strength is insufficient... but because he once suffered a severe injury, so it is very difficult for him to advance. Yet his strength is incredibly, incredibly great. He created many Supreme Dao Techniques and cultivated each of them to the ultimate level. His physical strength, soul strength, and Dao power have basically all been cultivated to the utmost peak of a Supreme Dao Ancestor!”
Ye Tian was also slightly astonished. To create multiple Supreme Dao Techniques and cultivate them all to the ultimate level was indeed terrifying.
In addition, through his Copy Talent, he had indeed seen that the man possessed multiple Dao-level innate talents, which meant he must have encountered many opportunities. Only then could he have acquired so many Dao-level innate talents.
Probably even the former Wind King was far, far inferior to this Yan Ancestor! Then, Fire King continued: “That burly young man over at the Heavenly Emperor Palace who radiates black light is Xuanhu Dao Ancestor. It is said that he has invincible defense. Even some weaker Invincible Dao Ancestors have been unable to break through his defenses. It is rumored that he has cultivated more than six defensive Supreme Dao Techniques, each one to the ultimate level.
The key is that the six defensive Supreme Dao Techniques he created complement one another: they almost form a complete system of Supreme Dao Techniques and can perfectly amplify each other. That is why he is so terrifying!”
After introducing the two Supreme Dao Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, Fire King began introducing Tianlin Dao Ancestor of Tianhai Sect, Wutian Dao Ancestor of Mitian Sect, and Kunxing Dao Ancestor of Myriad Domain Divine Hall.
These three Dao Ancestors were only slightly inferior to Xuanhu Dao Ancestor and Yan Ancestor, while Black Wind Mountain also had one Dao Ancestor who could rival them. He too was among the hundred-plus Dao Ancestors this time, but he was very low-key and followed the orders of the two Half-Step Domain Ancestors, taking Ye Tian as the leader.

Chapter 1210 Medium-Grade Forbidden Supreme Treasure!

The position of the Ten Kings in Black Wind Mountain was very special. At the level of Supreme Dao Ancestors, the Ten Kings reigned supreme. If Niekong Dao Ancestor were to lead the other Supreme Dao Ancestors or even the Ten Kings, the rules would be thrown into disorder.
Niekong Dao Ancestor had once served as one of the Ten Kings, so he understood the rules and likely would not have any objections.

Whoosh!!! One Dao Ancestor after another crossed into this medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, and Ye Tian also led the Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain into it.
After entering, everyone found themselves in an environment similar to a Forbidden Continent.
“Zero Four Seven”
Endless mountain ranges stretching on and on, a Forbidden river running across the continent, Forbidden forests covering one region after another.... “So it’s a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm of the Forbidden Continent type. A Forbidden Void Realm like this has concentrated resources, and its value far exceeds that of a starry-sky-type Forbidden Void Realm!”
Ye Tian murmured.
