If any force dares to start refining this Forbidden Void Realm first, regroup immediately and stop them, understood?”
Ye Tian ordered.
“Yes, Dark King!”
the many Supreme Dao Ancestors responded.
Whoosh! One Supreme Dao Ancestor after another from Black Wind Mountain departed and soon vanished from sight.
There were not many Supreme Dao Ancestors who had entered, but the range their divine sense could cover was too vast, so their speed in finding Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures was also very fast. Those Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors could only rely on luck.
If no Supreme Dao Ancestors targeted them, they might be able to obtain some Forbidden artifacts. But if a Supreme Dao Ancestor targeted them, even the Supreme Dao Ancestors of their own force might not have time to save them.
After all, the gap between a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor and a Supreme Dao Ancestor was simply too great. Some powerful Supreme Dao Ancestors could almost instantly kill a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor.
Ye Tian’s divine sense covered the surrounding region and locked onto the locations of one Forbidden artifact after another.
For Supreme Dao Ancestors, unless it was a Forbidden supreme treasure, an ordinary Forbidden artifact, even if it contained great terror, could not really do much harm to them.
And now, Ye Tian gradually understood why some Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures contained great terror.
It was said that Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures were projections of some kind of supreme forbidden object. In the Dark Forbidden Domain, they had corresponding forbidden objects guarded by Forbidden creatures.
And seizing Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures would attract the attention of those Forbidden creatures. A trace of power would descend through the Forbidden origin across the endless Dark Forbidden Domain and fall upon the person touching the Forbidden artifact, thus creating the phenomenon of great terror.
Of course.
Some Forbidden artifacts had already lost the protection of their Forbidden creatures and would not trigger any great terror, allowing them to be taken easily.
As for Forbidden supreme treasures, their connection with those supreme forbidden objects was deeper, so the projected power of the Forbidden creatures was stronger as well. Hence, the great terror they triggered was correspondingly far more terrifying! Of course.
With Ye Tian’s strength, even if he directly withstood the great terror of an ordinary Forbidden supreme treasure, he would not die—he would merely be injured.
As time passed, one Forbidden artifact after another fell into Ye Tian’s hands, their number far exceeding before.
However, these Forbidden artifacts did not all belong entirely to Ye Tian.
After all, this time the Half-Step Domain Ancestors themselves did not enter and restrained the Invincible Dao Ancestors from entering as well, so naturally they would not allow all the Forbidden artifacts here to belong solely to the Supreme Dao Ancestors. Thus, before entering, these Supreme Dao Ancestors had agreed to hand over half of the Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures to their respective forces.
This was very fair. Otherwise, no one would get any benefits.
Ye Tian did not mind. Even if he handed half the Forbidden artifacts to Black Wind Mountain, he would still obtain an enormous number of Forbidden artifacts. And with his strength, he could run rampant among Supreme Dao Ancestors. If Invincible Dao Ancestors were allowed to participate, he probably would not be able to seize many Forbidden artifacts at all.
Therefore, he was not losing out at all.
Soon, he discovered a Forbidden supreme treasure, and it was actually a medium-grade Forbidden supreme treasure.
....“Hahaha, a medium-grade Forbidden supreme treasure. This great opportunity is destined to belong to me, Lin’an Dao Ancestor!”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor said excitedly.
This was a bead-type Forbidden supreme treasure, likely a cultivation-assisting Forbidden supreme treasure, making it quite suitable for him.
However, a shadow of a black giant beast floated above this Forbidden supreme treasure, clearly showing that it contained great terror. If touched directly, it would immediately trigger a terrifying event.
So he immediately captured one Forbidden-bloodline creature after another from the surrounding area, forcibly making them trigger the terrifying event. Boom!!!! One Forbidden-bloodline creature after another was震死 by the power of the great terror, until at last the terrifying event completely dissipated.
But just as he was about to take away this bead-type Forbidden supreme treasure, the void solidified, and he suddenly failed to seize the bead.
“Who is it?”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor shouted angrily.
Yet his hands did not slow in the slightest, and he instantly grabbed forward, trying to seize the bead-type Forbidden supreme treasure first before dealing with the enemy.
However, a Forbidden spear stabbed toward him, carrying terrifying power.
Lin’an Dao Ancestor’s expression changed drastically, and he turned to evade the Forbidden spear.
But precisely because he had to evade it, he lost the best opportunity to take the bead.
The next moment, a figure appeared in front of the bead.
That person was Ye Tian.
“Dark King of Black Wind Mountain, what do you mean by this?”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor roared in anger.
“Lin’an Dao Ancestor, I’m taking this bead!”
Ye Tian declared domineeringly.
“Dark King, you’re nothing more than a newly advanced Supreme Dao Ancestor of Black Wind Mountain. Don’t be too arrogant!”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor said coldly.
As for the identity of the Dark King, many people had their guesses. Some thought he was the former Nine Extremes Heavenly King, while others believed he was not.
But no matter who the Dark King was, he had definitely not been a Supreme Dao Ancestor for long.
And who was Lin’an Dao Ancestor? He was one of the top independent-cultivator Supreme Dao Ancestors. Even compared with Black Wind Mountain’s former Wind King, he was not much weaker.... And now a newly advanced Supreme Dao Ancestor actually dared to threaten him.
Moreover, he had not felt that the power of that previous Forbidden spear strike was especially strong.
“You won’t leave?”
Ye Tian asked.
“I won’t leave!”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor said coldly. “Unless you get out of the way and let me take this Forbidden supreme treasure bead, only then will I leave.
Otherwise, today I’ll teach you a lesson and let people know what a true powerhouse is!”
“I really didn’t want to kill too many Supreme Dao Ancestors at a time like this, but if you insist on courting death, then die!”
Ye Tian condensed another Forbidden spear, but its power was vastly greater than before.
The previous Forbidden spear had merely been an ordinary Forbidden spear, but this one was now empowered by the Forbidden talent: Dark Spear, as well as Ye Tian’s own Endless Forbidden Dao. Its might was utterly different from before.
When this Forbidden spear came striking over, Lin’an Dao Ancestor finally changed color.

Chapter 1211: Instantly Killing a Top Supreme Dao Ancestor
！【Second Update】
“How could he be this strong?”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor could not believe it. The speed of this Forbidden spear was far too fast, and it had locked onto him, leaving him no way to dodge.
Whoosh! A top-grade Dao artifact armor appeared on his body, and he also activated a defensive Supreme Dao Technique.
As an independent cultivator, he truly was not wealthy. He did not possess a Forbidden weapon at all, and this was one of the tragedies of being an independent cultivator.
Puchi!!! The Forbidden spear instantly pierced through his defenses, even penetrating the top-grade Dao artifact armor.
Under this single strike, Lin’an Dao Ancestor was severely wounded.
“One strike seriously wounded me!!!”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor looked at Ye Tian with fear filling his eyes. This was the first time he had ever fought such a terrifying Dao Ancestor.
In his impression, the only Supreme Dao Ancestors capable of severely wounding him in a single strike were Yan Ancestor and Xuanhu Dao Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace. Tianlin Dao Ancestor, Wutian Dao Ancestor, and Kunxing Dao Ancestor might not even be able to seriously wound him with one strike.
Run! Lin’an Dao Ancestor was completely cowed, completely terrified.
Boom!!! The Forbidden Domain descended, and the Great Thousand Dao Technique, Ten Directions Space-Fixing Art, was also unleashed.
Although the power of a Great Thousand Dao Technique was not especially strong, using it together with the Forbidden Domain to bind Lin’an Dao Ancestor was not difficult.
“Lin’an Dao Ancestor, ever since I broke through to become a Supreme Dao Ancestor, I have never used the Forbidden Dao Technique I created against anyone. Today, I shall use you as its first target!”
Ye Tian muttered.
Forbidden Dao Technique! Upon hearing this, Lin’an Dao Ancestor’s pupils shrank sharply, and he begged for mercy: “Dark King, don’t kill me! I truly did not mean to fight you over this Forbidden supreme treasure. It is yours!”
However, Ye Tian did not listen to his nonsense and instead unleashed the Dark Extreme Dao Spear.
Dark to the utmost, the Dark Extreme Dao Spear, containing terrifying Forbidden laws, instantly condensed into form and pierced forward with terrifying Forbidden power.
“No!”
Lin’an Dao Ancestor cried out in terror.

Of course, this was also related to the fact that Lin’an Dao Ancestor did not have a Forbidden defensive weapon. If Lin’an Dao Ancestor had possessed a Forbidden defensive weapon and had cultivated one defensive Supreme Dao Technique to the ultimate level, Ye Tian would not have been able to kill him with one strike.
Still, he now had a clearer understanding of his own strength.
At the very least, ordinary top Supreme Dao Ancestors were not worthy enemies of even a single strike from him. He would definitely be able to kill them within two or three moves, perhaps even in a single move.
Ye Tian casually put away Lin’an Dao Ancestor’s belongings and then took the Forbidden supreme treasure bead as well.
He did not inspect the bead carefully, instead leaving quickly and continuing to search for Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures.
To him, time itself was... Forbidden treasures! As time passed, a great number of Forbidden artifacts fell into the hands of these Supreme Dao Ancestors. Every Supreme Dao Ancestor reaped rich rewards, though some of the weaker Supreme Dao Ancestors did die, albeit in relatively small numbers.
After all, everyone was busy searching for Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden treasures. If the difference in strength between two sides was not too great, they would not fight at all. Otherwise, it would waste time, and if neither could kill the other, the Forbidden artifacts would... simply be snatched away by other Supreme Dao Ancestors.
Only in situations like Ye Tian and Lin’an Dao Ancestor, where the gap in strength between both sides was too great, would one side make a move.
Several days passed quickly.
At this point, the Forbidden artifacts in this medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm had basically all fallen into the hands of the Supreme Dao Ancestors.
“More than ten thousand Forbidden items!”
This was Ye Tian’s harvest in three days. After all, it was almost like picking up Forbidden artifacts off the ground, so naturally the collection speed was very fast. Among them were many top-grade Forbidden artifacts, and he had also obtained eight Forbidden supreme treasures.
In a small Forbidden Void Realm, Forbidden supreme treasures were not common, but in a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, there were quite a few of them.
At present, although there were still some Forbidden artifacts left in this Forbidden Void Realm, the number was definitely very small.
“It’s time to try refining this Forbidden Void Realm!”
Ye Tian muttered.
Thus, he began summoning the Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain.
Soon, one Supreme Dao Ancestor after another from Black Wind Mountain arrived at his side.
On a towering Forbidden giant mountain, all one hundred-plus Supreme Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain arrived. Only one had fallen, most likely due to bad luck—perhaps running into a Supreme Dao Ancestor like Yan Ancestor and being instantly severely wounded or even killed outright.
“I am preparing to refine the Forbidden Void Realm. You all will stand guard here. If the enemy is too powerful and you are not their match, then I will intervene!”
Ye Tian ordered.
At this moment, Niekong Dao Ancestor, who rarely ever spoke, said, “Dark King, are we really going to refine the Forbidden Void Realm just like this? If we do, the Supreme Dao Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, Tianhai Sect, Mitian Sect, and Myriad Domain Divine Hall will all come attack us. In that case, we won’t be able to hold them off at all! I suggest letting the other forces try refining the Forbidden Void Realm first. Once they start fighting each other, we can wait until their strength is mostly exhausted before refining the Forbidden Void Realm ourselves. That would greatly improve our chances of success!”
Ye Tian said coldly, “Niekong Dao Ancestor, if you can think of such a method, do you think the other forces cannot? If we wait like that, how long would we have to wait? Moreover, once another force dares to refine the Forbidden Void Realm, it means they must already have great confidence.
Likewise, since I dare to refine the Forbidden Void Realm, I naturally also have great confidence!”
Niekong Dao Ancestor did not refute him, because refuting him would be useless.
Just at that moment, Ye Tian took out the World-Suppressing Stele and set it atop this mountain peak.
Boom!!!! As soon as the stele appeared, under Ye Tian’s activation it began suppressing the Forbidden laws in this region of space, even spreading into the origin of the medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm and gradually invading the core of its origin.
At the same time, a portion of Ye Tian’s power began refining the origin of the Forbidden Void Realm through the World-Suppressing Stele.
When Niekong Dao Ancestor and the other Supreme Dao Ancestors saw the World-Suppressing Stele, they were immediately shocked. They could all tell that this World-Suppressing Stele was absolutely the finest supreme treasure for refining a world.
“Could it have been bestowed upon him by the two Half-Step Domain Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain?”
Niekong Dao Ancestor asked doubtfully.
But after thinking about it carefully, that did not seem right either. Though Black Wind Mountain’s rules were not excessively strict, it still would not casually bestow treasures—especially not one this precious.
For example, when he himself had once been the Space King, no such treasure had ever been bestowed upon him, so it was even less likely that such a supreme treasure would be bestowed upon Ye Tian.
Niekong Dao Ancestor did not think further about it and instead focused fully on observing the surrounding void, guarding against any surprise attacks by Supreme Dao Ancestors.
At the same time.
The Supreme Dao Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, Tianhai Sect, Mitian Sect, and Myriad Domain Divine Hall also learned that someone was refining the medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, and they all gathered and rushed toward Ye Tian’s location.
Meanwhile, many independent cultivators and Supreme Dao Ancestors from Eighth Heaven forces were also filled with curiosity and came over one after another, preparing to observe the coming battle.
If there happened to be an opportunity to profit, they certainly would not mind making a move to seize something.

In addition, the power of the Forbidden origin continuously repaired his physical injuries, so his wounds were not too severe.

the Azure Dragon Palace Master said. “In the future, more Forbidden Void Realms will definitely be born, perhaps even Forbidden Void Realms.
Our Heavenly Emperor Palace’s strongest level is the Invincible Dao Ancestor level. If Invincible Dao Ancestors had not been barred from participating this time, Black Wind Mountain would never have gotten such a bargain!”
The True Martial Palace Master and White Tiger Palace Master both very much agreed with this statement. Besides, even if Black Wind Mountain controlled a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, it still could not increase its strength rapidly. It merely meant that it possessed a base that could not be breached.
Therefore, Black Wind Mountain still could not threaten the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s position.
....Nine Rivers Base.
Ye Tian once again came to Ouyang Jiuer’s residence and returned the World-Suppressing Stele to her.
“Not bad. Your strength has actually surpassed Yan Ancestor and the others!”
Ouyang Jiuer commented.
Once upon a time, when she had first met Ye Tian, he had not counted as any particularly powerful existence. Although his talent had been very good, there had been nothing about him that truly shocked her.
After all, she had once been a Half-Step Domain Ancestor, and in the Divine Heaven Domain she had seen no shortage of geniuses.
But now, at the Supreme Dao Ancestor level, Ye Tian had defeated Yan Ancestor, Xuanhu Dao Ancestor, and the others, suppressing five Supreme Dao Ancestors of that level by himself. His combat strength had already become terrifying to a certain degree. Even in the entire Divine Heaven Domain, such a Supreme Dao Ancestor would be exceedingly rare.... Only the very top few legendary forces in the Divine Heaven Domain could nurture a Supreme Dao Ancestor like this.
Moreover, she knew very well that Ye Tian had still not reached his limit at the Supreme Dao Ancestor level and could continue improving.
Once Ye Tian reached the ultimate limit of the Supreme Dao Ancestor level, his combat power would likely become impossible to estimate. He might even become capable of crossing levels to kill an Invincible Dao Ancestor.
“Jiuer, don’t praise me anymore. In terms of strength, you might not necessarily be weaker than me. You may even be stronger than I am!”
Ye Tian said with a smile.
Ouyang Jiuer rolled her eyes. She was the reincarnation of a Half-Step Domain Ancestor and had mastered more than one or two Forbidden Dao Techniques. Her attainments in both the Forbidden Dao and Forbidden Dao Techniques were extremely high, so under such circumstances, her combat strength naturally could not be weak.
But she knew very well that the reserves from her previous life were almost exhausted. Once she entered the Invincible Dao Ancestor level, the foundation from her previous life would not help her much anymore.
Once that time came, it would be effortless for Ye Tian to surpass her.
After chatting for a while, Ye Tian finally left Ouyang Jiuer’s residence.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian occasionally hunted Forbidden Insects and occasionally entered the Void Dark Realm to cultivate.
4.4 However, he did not transfer the Nine Extremes Legion or some of the human race’s Dao Ancestors into the Void Dark Realm. After all, if one had not reached the Supreme Dao Ancestor level, cultivating in a small Forbidden Void Realm was more effective, because of the accelerated flow of time.
But once one reached the Supreme Dao Ancestor level, one could no longer enter a small Forbidden Void Realm, and only a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm was truly suitable for them.
In addition.
Ye Tian controlled half the authority over the Void Dark Realm, and could even mobilize a small portion of the Void Dark Realm’s origin to temper his body and accelerate his cultivation. This was also one of the privileges of being a world master of a medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm.
Of course, he did not dare consume too much of the Void Dark Realm’s origin, otherwise the impact on the Void Dark Realm would be too great.
Time slowly passed, and in the blink of an eye, ten thousand years went by.

Chapter 1216 The Forbidden Insect Race Came Prepared! ..

Chapter 1216: The Forbidden Insect Race Came Prepared
！【Third Update】
Forbidden Insect nest, Forbidden Insect Tree.
Originally, there had been three Lord-level Forbidden Insect cocoons on the Forbidden Insect Tree, but at this moment there were still two Lord-level Forbidden Insect cocoons left.
In addition, two Lord-level Forbidden Insects were guarding this place, while outside there were eight Lord-level Forbidden Insects. If the two Lord-level Forbidden Insect cocoons were to hatch, the Forbidden Insect Race would possess twelve Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
Suddenly.
One of the Lord-level Forbidden Insect cocoons began to crack open, and a golden long leg stretched out from inside. Immediately after, a ferocious-looking Lord-level Forbidden Insect emerged, its terrifying aura spreading out and shaking the surrounding void.
This meant that the Forbidden Insect Race had once again given birth to a Lord-level Forbidden Insect.
Not long afterward, the second Lord-level Forbidden Insect cocoon also began to break apart, and the second Lord-level Forbidden Insect appeared.
A newly born Lord-level Forbidden Insect was at its weakest, but as one Forbidden Insect after another brought over various energy resources to be devoured by these two Lord-level Forbidden Insects, their shells grew increasingly sturdy, and their auras became more and more powerful and stable.
In the end, they fully matured.
Compared with the other Lord-level Forbidden Insects, they might still be somewhat weaker, but they were absolutely not weaker than ordinary Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
Soon after, the aura of the Forbidden Insect Tree weakened somewhat, but the Lord-level Forbidden Insects showed no panic whatsoever.
Very quickly, one cocoon after another began to break apart, and dense masses of Forbidden Insects crawled out from within the cocoons.
In no time at all, nearly five hundred thousand Forbidden Insects had been born.
Originally, the Forbidden Insect Race already had about one million two hundred thousand members, and now that another five hundred thousand Forbidden Insects had been born all at once, that meant the total number of Forbidden Insects had now reached one million seven hundred thousand.
Suddenly.
Three Lord-level Forbidden Insects from inside the nest led a large number of Forbidden Insects out of the nest, leaving behind only one Lord-level Forbidden Insect and a portion of the Forbidden Insects to guard the nest and the Forbidden Insect Tree.
Outside the Forbidden Insect nest.
One Lord-level Forbidden Insect after another returned, and large numbers of Forbidden Insects also gathered here.
This entire region was practically covered by Forbidden Insects, their numbers gradually approaching two million.
1 Lord-level Forbidden Insect, 1.2 million ordinary Forbidden Insects, elite-level Forbidden Insects, and more than fifty Commander-level Forbidden Insects.
The gathering of so many Forbidden Insects was naturally not for a meeting, but for war.
Awooo...!!! One of the Lord-level Forbidden Insects let out a roar, and the Forbidden Insect army set out, flying toward one of the bases in the Dao Mountain Domain.
They were going to attack a base! All this time, the Forbidden Insect Race had employed a strategy of gradual attrition while attacking the various bases of the Dao Mountain Domain, but this time they had changed their strategy.
Without question, this had to do with the birth of the two Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
The Forbidden Insect Race had continually clashed with the various bases of the Dao Mountain Domain, leading them to believe that the bases possessed only eight Half-Step Domain Ancestors in total. If there were more Half-Step Domain Ancestors, why had they not appeared? Even though the Forbidden Insect Race possessed intelligent insects, they would not think that hidden forces existed in the Dao Mountain Domain.
Therefore, they believed that with their Lord-level Forbidden Insects plus an army of 1.2 million Forbidden Insects, they had enough power to destroy the bases of the Dao Mountain Domain one by one and then fully invade the Dao Mountain Domain.
....Mitian Base.
This base, established by the Mitian Sect, was one of the largest among all the bases. It was guarded by the Half-Step Domain Ancestor Migudao Ancestor, along with several Invincible Dao Ancestors and many Supreme Dao Ancestors, making it extremely powerful.
At this moment.
Migudao Ancestor was investigating the situation in the territory surrounding Mitian Base.
Suddenly, he received a transmission from Dao Ancestors currently hunting Forbidden Insects in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
“What? The Forbidden Insect Race is mobilizing on a large scale and seems to be heading toward Mitian Base!”
Migudao Ancestor’s expression changed drastically.
This was no small matter. If they really were attacking Mitian Base, then with Mitian Base’s strength alone, it absolutely could not hold! “Call for reinforcements!”
Migudao Ancestor sent requests for aid one by one to the Heavenly Emperor Palace, Black Wind Mountain, Myriad Domain Divine Hall, Tianhai Sect, and the other bases, asking them to come support Mitian Base and prepare to fight the incoming Forbidden Insect Race.
Naturally, forces like the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain could not possibly stand by and watch Mitian Base be breached. After all, Mitian Base was one of the key lines of defense. Once it fell, this direction would be left undefended, and the Forbidden Insect Race would very likely invade the Dao Mountain Domain directly.
Moreover, without the strength of Mitian Base, the various bases would lose one share of their combat power, which was definitely not a good thing.
Thus.
The Dao Ancestors of one base after another rushed toward Mitian Base, with many bases dispatching almost half of their forces.
Black Wind Mountain Base.
Ye Tian also received the news and led a large number of Dao Ancestors toward Mitian Base.
This time, both his true body and his replicated body, the Dark King, were mobilized. His wife Xiao Yue was cultivating in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm and was currently not at Black Wind Mountain Base, so she did not go to provide support. But his son and daughter were at Black Wind Mountain Base, so they followed Ye Tian to reinforce it.
The Forbidden Insect army was simply too numerous, so before the Dao Ancestors of the major bases had gathered together, none of them dared fight it alone.... Thus, they could only wait until they had all assembled at Mitian Base before engaging the Forbidden army.
Several of the bases closer to Mitian Base arrived one after another to provide support, while the other Half-Step Domain Ancestors rushed over first. Otherwise, if those Lord-level Forbidden Insects attacked, Migudao Ancestor probably would not be able to hold them off and would be killed in a short time.
“Migudao Ancestor, have you clarified the situation of the Forbidden Insect army this time?”
The Azure Dragon Palace Master arrived and asked Migudao Ancestor.
“The number of Forbidden Insects is roughly 1.2 million. As for the Lord-level Forbidden Insects, we have only detected nine so far. But whether there are only nine Lord-level Forbidden Insects or not is still unclear!”
Migudao Ancestor said.
“Nine Lord-level Forbidden Insects? If there are only nine, then the pressure is not too great. But if there is even one more, then this battle will become extremely difficult!”
the True Martial Palace Master said with a frown.
“No matter what, we hold them off first!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor said.
As time slowly passed, the Forbidden Insect army arrived.
Looking into the distance, the Forbidden Insect army resembled a surging black tide, rushing forward at terrifying speed, as if a single wave could drown the entire Mitian Base.
Outside Mitian Base, the eight Half-Step Domain Ancestors and a large number of Dao Ancestors had basically all arrived as well.
One astonishing grand formation after another had been set up, waiting for the arrival of the Forbidden Insect army.
Ye Tian, Ye Xingchen, and Ye Xingyue stood in one area, their gazes fixed on the distance.
“This battle will be very hard to win!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
The Forbidden Insect Race had come prepared and naturally must have had complete confidence. If the major bases had only this much strength, they would probably collapse very quickly.
Of course.
Both the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain still had hidden strength.

Chapter 1217 Slaying a Commander-Level Forbidden Insect! ..

Chapter 1217: Slaying a Commander-Level Forbidden Insect
！【Fourth Update】
Boom! The Forbidden Insect army had arrived! The Dao Ancestors made their move, meeting the 1.2 million Forbidden Insect army in battle as the two sides clashed.
Meanwhile, the eight Half-Step Domain Ancestors also began fighting the nine Lord-level Forbidden Insects. Among them, the Azure Dragon Palace Master alone fought two of the strongest Lord-level Forbidden Insects, and only then was he able to hold back those nine Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
Ye Tian’s true body, meanwhile, maintained the combat strength of a top Supreme Dao Ancestor. He did not use Forbidden Dao Techniques, and even held back all kinds of methods, doing his best not to make his techniques match those of the Dark King.
But the Dark King did not need to worry about any of that. Going all out in battle, he was almost able to kill an elite-level Forbidden Insect with a single move.
“Die!”
Holding the Sky-Slaying Spear, Ye Tian slaughtered one Forbidden Insect after another, his invincible figure sweeping across this battlefield.
Elite-level Forbidden Insects could not stop Ye Tian, and ordinary Forbidden Insects were even less worth mentioning. With a single sweep, Ye Tian wiped out a huge swath of them. Not a single Forbidden Insect could survive.
The intelligent insects among the Forbidden Insect Race were not stupid. They knew that no matter how many elite-level or ordinary Forbidden Insects they sent, they could not stop Ye Tian, so they dispatched a Commander-level Forbidden Insect to kill him, determined to slay Ye Tian.
....“A Commander-level Forbidden Insect!”
Ye Tian fixed his gaze on the Commander-level Forbidden Insect darting toward him from not far away, gripped the Sky-Slaying Spear tightly, and began fighting it.
Boom!!! With a single collision, Ye Tian was sent flying backward.
This Commander-level Forbidden Insect was not weak. Even Ye Tian’s strongest attack could do nothing to it, and in terms of offensive power, he was actually weaker than it.
Very soon, Ye Tian was injured, while that Commander-level Forbidden Insect had barely suffered any damage at all.
However, Ye Tian could use the power of the Forbidden origin to heal his injuries, so it was not too serious.
But if the battle continued like this, it would undoubtedly be a waste of time. If he could not kill it, then it meant this share of his combat power was being wasted, and he would not be able to kill more Forbidden Insects.
“I have to kill it!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
But killing a Commander-level Forbidden Insect was extremely difficult—far from an ordinary challenge.
Suddenly.
The Sky-Slaying Spear in Ye Tian’s hand vanished, and in the next instant it appeared at a vulnerable point on the abdomen of that Commander-level Forbidden Insect, piercing straight through its body in one strike.
At this moment.
That Commander-level Forbidden Insect was extremely puzzled. It did not understand why Ye Tian had suddenly struck its abdomen when it had not sensed a thing.
“As expected, it can’t sense the path of my attack at all!” Ye Tian smiled.
This was the second Forbidden Dao Technique he had created. It had only been created recently, and strictly speaking it was still somewhat incomplete. Forcefully using it would cause some harm to his body, but not much—something that could be fully repaired with the power of the Forbidden origin.
Originally, he had not wanted to use this not-yet-fully-created Dao Technique, but he truly could not do anything to this Commander-level Forbidden Insect, so he had no choice but to use it.
He had given this Forbidden Dao Technique a name: Shadow Pierce. It could attack silently and without a trace, and its offensive power was only slightly inferior to Dark Extreme Dao Spear.
But Dark Extreme Dao Spear’s attack could be evaded or even blocked, whereas Shadow Pierce resembled the effect of the Forbidden talent Stealth. Unless one was a Half-Step Domain Ancestor, there was simply no way to detect it.
Thus, Ye Tian’s strike had worked. That Commander-level Forbidden Insect had no way to dodge it and was directly struck at the weakest part of its body, suffering injury at once.
Very soon, Ye Tian launched a second Shadow Pierce attack, once again striking the weak point of the Commander-level Forbidden Insect’s body and injuring it again.
In this way, Ye Tian used Shadow Pierce from time to time, causing the wounds of that Commander-level Forbidden Insect to grow more and more severe.
That Commander-level Forbidden Insect was also quite crazed, attacking Ye Tian furiously and injuring him again and again. But Ye Tian could rapidly recover his injuries with the power of the Forbidden origin, so the Commander-level Forbidden Insect simply could not kill him.
If it had been another Invincible Dao Ancestor, by this point they probably would have chosen to flee. But before receiving an order, this Commander-level Forbidden Insect would never think of running away. It only wanted to kill Ye Tian.
Time passed bit by bit, and before long, this Commander-level Forbidden Insect was already gravely wounded and on the verge of death.
Suddenly, Ye Tian unleashed a strike of Dark Extreme Dao Spear. This time, not only was the Commander-level Forbidden Insect unable to block it, but even its defensive power had dropped greatly. Unable to withstand it, it was directly pierced through by Ye Tian’s strike.
This attack completely left the Commander-level Forbidden Insect heavily wounded and dying! At this moment, several nearby elite-level Forbidden Insects seemed to want to come rescue this Commander-level Forbidden Insect, but Ye Tian attacked the Commander-level Forbidden Insect even faster.
By the time those elite-level Forbidden Insects arrived, Ye Tian had already completely slain the Commander-level Forbidden Insect.
Immediately, Ye Tian took away the corpse of the Commander-level Forbidden Insect, then used Shadow Pierce once more, finding a tricky angle. With a single Shadow Pierce strike, he pierced through all of those elite-level Forbidden Insects at once, instantly killing them.
At this moment.
Ye Tian did not continue fighting, but instead seized the time to recover his injuries.
In order to kill that Forbidden Insect, he himself had not escaped injury. His recovery speed had not quite been able to keep up with the rate at which he was being injured. Although the wounds on his body were not considered devastating, they were certainly not light either.
Therefore, he wanted to fully recover before continuing to kill other Forbidden Insects more effectively.
And the scene of Ye Tian slaying the Commander-level Forbidden Insect was captured by quite a few nearby Supreme Dao Ancestors, all of whom fell into shock.
A Supreme Dao Ancestor slaying a Commander-level Forbidden Insect—this was equivalent to a Supreme Dao Ancestor killing an Invincible Dao Ancestor. It was simply heaven-defying! “He’s become even stronger!”
Yan Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace said in shock.
Previously, Ye Tian’s invisibility had been terrifying and almost impossible to guard against. But after disappearing and then attacking, he would still reveal his position, leaving enough time to react. It was only that the five of them had been unable to cooperate properly to defend against him back then.
But this time, Yan Ancestor had seen Ye Tian’s attack clearly—it was simply impossible to defend against, impossible to dodge. The instant he moved, the attack had already struck the body of the Commander-level Forbidden Insect. Such a method was far too terrifying.
If Ye Tian had possessed this move back then, he and the other four Supreme Dao Ancestors would probably have been defeated very quickly, perhaps even killed.
Elsewhere.
Migudao Ancestor was fighting a Lord-level Forbidden Insect when two more Lord-level Forbidden Insects suddenly appeared beside him.
He only sensed them when they were already very close.
“Not good!”
Migudao Ancestor cried out in alarm.
Boom boom!! The two Lord-level Forbidden Insects launched their attacks instantly, their two long legs piercing through Migudao Ancestor’s defenses in a flash and striking his defensive Forbidden armor, sending him coughing blood as he staggered backward.
Then, the three Lord-level Forbidden Insects surrounded him and launched another coordinated assault! At this moment, Migudao Ancestor’s situation was extremely dangerous.

But now, three Lord-level Forbidden Insects were dealing with him, and the two hidden Forbidden Insects were both extremely powerful, each stronger than him.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!! The three Lord-level Forbidden Insects began besieging Migudao Ancestor, completely crushing him.

Once he lost that Forbidden weapon-grade defensive armor, his situation would become unimaginably dire.
Suddenly.
One of the Lord-level Forbidden Insects drove a long leg directly through Migudao Ancestor’s head. Although his head healed, that strike had penetrated into his soul sea and even damaged his soul, making his head ache as if it were splitting apart.
Crack crack crack!!! The cracks in the Forbidden weapon defensive armor grew larger and larger. For now, it could still offset part of the attacks, but as time passed, its ability to offset damage grew weaker and weaker.

the Azure Dragon Palace Master said.

Chapter 1219 A Lord-Level Forbidden Insect Has Fallen!..

Chapter 1219: A Lord-Level Forbidden Insect Has Fallen
！【First Update】
After Shenxu Dao Ancestor agreed to the Azure Dragon Palace Master’s plan, he began shifting the battle toward the Azure Dragon Palace Master’s side.

Elsewhere.

the Vermilion Bird Palace Master transmitted.

Shenxu Dao Ancestor said solemnly.
It was said that the Vast Sea Domain Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace had forged several Heavenly Emperor Weapons for the Heavenly Emperor Palace. The materials used for Heavenly Emperor Weapons were extremely special, and they also required a very long time to forge, while preserving them also consumed a great deal of energy.
Therefore, the Heavenly Emperor Palace did not possess many Heavenly Emperor Weapons, and the Vast Sea Statue was one of them. It carried a trace of the Vast Sea Domain Ancestor’s might, and when combined with the Vermilion Bird Palace Master’s Dao power, it could unleash a terrifying strike.
Even Shenxu Dao Ancestor did not dare take a strike from a Heavenly Emperor Weapon head-on. Without some special means to block it, even he would be severely wounded or perhaps even die.
At this moment.
That Lord-level Forbidden Insect also sensed the danger and desperately tried to flee, but Shenxu Dao Ancestor had bound it, and it had no way to escape.
Boom!!! The Vast Sea Statue transformed into a towering figure, and under the Vermilion Bird Palace Master’s control, it slowly opened both hands and reached toward the body of the Lord-level Forbidden Insect.
Looking at that figure, the Lord-level Forbidden Insect seemed to feel something like the might of an Insect King. Its body trembled uncontrollably, but it still struggled with all its strength, its long legs turning into countless afterimages as it tried to block those two immense hands.
But it was all futile! Crack! The Lord-level Forbidden Insect was caught in the two hands of the Vast Sea Statue, and its body began breaking apart under the crushing grip.
A terrifying trace of Domain Ancestor power continuously ravaged the body of the Lord-level Forbidden Insect, eroding away its life force.
“Shenxu Dao Ancestor, keep attacking!”
the Vermilion Bird Palace Master shouted.
Shenxu Dao Ancestor nodded and no longer hesitated, unleashing offensive Forbidden Dao Techniques again and again onto the body of the Lord-level Forbidden Insect, inflicting repeated damage.
Of course, Shenxu Dao Ancestor was only providing support. The true source of damage was still the Heavenly Emperor Weapon: Vast Sea Statue! Suddenly, the Lord-level Forbidden Insect lost all signs of life. It had already been crushed to death by the Vast Sea Statue.
After confirming it, Shenxu Dao Ancestor also ceased his attacks.
“It’s dead!”
the Vermilion Bird Palace Master confirmed that the other side had not faked its death.
Immediately, he collected the corpse of the Lord-level Forbidden Insect and did not immediately dismiss the Vast Sea Statue.
He was also wary that Shenxu Dao Ancestor might try to seize the corpse of the Lord-level Forbidden Insect. If Shenxu Dao Ancestor did so, then the still-active Vast Sea Statue would immediately attack Shenxu Dao Ancestor.
Only after the corpse of the Lord-level Forbidden Insect had been completely put away by the Vermilion Bird Palace Master did he dismiss the Vast Sea Statue.
At this point, the surface of the Vast Sea Statue was covered in cracks, as if it might shatter at any moment.
“What a pity!”
the Vermilion Bird Palace Master sighed.
This Heavenly Emperor Weapon could still be used, but only one or two more times. At most, it could be used to kill an Invincible Dao Ancestor. Killing a Half-Step Domain Ancestor with it was no longer possible.
After killing one Lord-level Forbidden Insect, the Vermilion Bird Palace Master went to help the Azure Dragon Palace Master, while Shenxu Dao Ancestor instead went off to kill Commander-level Forbidden Insects. As for Migudao Ancestor, he could still hold on for the time being, so there was no need for help there.
The three Lord-level Forbidden Insects fighting the Azure Dragon Palace Master, upon seeing Shenxu Dao Ancestor hunting Commander-level Forbidden Insects, grew furious and wanted to stop him.
However, the arrival of the Vermilion Bird Palace Master cut off their hope of leaving.
0Their methods were too one-dimensional. Without a numerical advantage, they were easily pinned down.
Thus, the fall of a single Lord-level Forbidden Insect instantly turned the situation around.
In truth, the Lord-level Forbidden Insects had never expected that two more Half-Step Domain Ancestors would appear in the Dao Mountain Domain. If they had known, they would never have come to attack the base.
As time passed, one Commander-level Forbidden Insect after another fell. In addition, Shenxu Dao Ancestor was extremely fast and killed at no slow pace, so more and more Forbidden Insects died at his hands.
Suddenly.
Shenxu Dao Ancestor split into countless incarnations, appearing on one battlefield after another and instantly wiping out huge numbers of Forbidden Insects.
At this point, the Forbidden Insects realized that they had lost.
0The Lord-level Forbidden Insects and some of the intelligent Forbidden Insects began leading the rest of the Forbidden Insects in retreat, no longer continuing the slaughter.
Naturally, many Forbidden Insects were sacrificed during the retreat.
Ye Tian also continuously hunted down the fleeing Forbidden Insects, and Shadow Pierce was simply too terrifying. Almost no Forbidden Insect could escape, and one after another died under his Shadow Pierce.
Several hours later, the Forbidden Insect army had vanished without a trace, and the Dao Ancestors did not continue the pursuit.
Afterward, they began cleaning up the battlefield, collecting the corpses of their companions as well as the corpses of the Forbidden Insects.
“Father!”
Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue flew over to Ye Tian and called out.
“Are you two all right?”
Ye Tian asked with concern.
“We’re fine, just a few minor injuries. Nothing serious!”
Ye Xingchen quickly said.
Ye Xingyue also said that she had not suffered any serious injuries.
“Let’s go. We’re returning to Black Wind Mountain Base!”
Ye Tian said.
After returning to Black Wind Mountain Base, Ye Tian began sorting through the Forbidden Insect corpses he had killed.
Among them were one Commander-level Forbidden Insect, 116 elite-level Forbidden Insects, and 243 ordinary Forbidden Insects. Such a record was already incomparably brilliant, while for other Supreme Dao Ancestors, being able to kill even one elite-level Forbidden Insect was already considered an incredible achievement.
Most Supreme Dao Ancestors could only kill a few ordinary Forbidden Insects and were unable to kill even a single elite-level Forbidden Insect.
Many Supreme Dao Ancestors had even become prey to elite-level Forbidden Insects and fallen at their hands.

Chapter 1220 Human Realm! Greatly Increased Strength!

Chapter 1220: Human Realm
！Greatly Increased Strength!【Second Update】
Ye Tian bestowed some of the ordinary Forbidden Insect corpses upon certain outstanding Dao Ancestors of the human race and the top performers within the Nine Extremes Legion, allowing them to sacrifice the Forbidden Insects and thereby obtain enhancements in strength and cultivation.
As for himself, he went to sacrifice that Commander-level Forbidden Insect along with the elite-level Forbidden Insects. After the sacrifice, his cultivation speed greatly increased, and his strength also improved somewhat.
For Dao Ancestors, sacrificing Forbidden Insects was undoubtedly one of the fastest ways to increase their cultivation, and it had almost no side effects. Moreover, the boost to cultivation speed was nearly permanent, and that was the most important part.
It was precisely because of this that Dao Ancestors longed to kill Forbidden Insects for sacrifice, or to collect Forbidden Insect corpses.
And at this time.
Many Dao Ancestors were dissatisfied with the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain. Clearly, both the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain still had other Half-Step Domain Ancestors, so why had they not appeared from the beginning? Why had they waited until the injuries were “seven nine, seven”
so severe before showing up? If the Half-Step Domain Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain had participated from the very start, they might have already wiped out the Forbidden Insect Race.
However, those who said such things were basically foolish Dao Ancestors or Dao Ancestors with little strength. The truly knowledgeable Dao Ancestors all understood very clearly that the Xuanxu Ancient Realm had the power to easily wipe out the Forbidden Insect Race.
It was just that the Xuanxu Ancient Realm was treating the Forbidden Insect Race like gu poison breeding stock and was unwilling to exterminate them.
As time passed, those Dao Ancestors gradually stopped talking about it, because they had no way to resist the Half-Step Domain Ancestors anyway.
As the years passed, in the days that followed, the various bases completely crushed the Forbidden Insect Race. After all, the various bases had gained two additional Half-Step Domain Ancestors, and could easily suppress the Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
It could be said that as long as one Half-Step Domain Ancestor was split off, they could slaughter Commander-level Forbidden Insects on a large scale.
Thus, the number of Forbidden Insects sharply decreased, and soon dropped to less than five million.
At that point, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors rarely made moves anymore, lest the Forbidden Insect Race collapse completely.
And so, ten thousand years passed after ten thousand years, and who knew how many Forbidden Insect corpses were sent into the Xuanxu Ancient Realm as sacrifices, causing the Xuanxu Ancient Realm to continuously expand and grow.
During that period, the Xuanxu Ancient Realm also gave birth to several medium-sized Forbidden Void Realms.
Ye Tian personally seized one medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm, and seized another Forbidden Void Realm for Black Wind Mountain. After that, he did not continue fighting for more.
It was not that he did not want to continue competing for Forbidden Void Realms, but because the rules later changed, and the major forces allowed Invincible Dao Ancestors to compete as well. At that point, Ye Tian could no longer manage it.
Thus, the Heavenly Emperor Palace seized one Forbidden Void Realm, while Tianhai Sect, Mitian Sect, and Myriad Domain Divine Hall joined forces and paid a terrible price to seize one Forbidden Void Realm. In the process, two Invincible Dao Ancestors even fell, and they expended one top-tier Forbidden supreme treasure.
The Forbidden Void Realm Ye Tian seized personally belonged entirely to him, and he held one hundred percent of its authority.
Ye Tian moved the entire human race directly into it, hiding nothing at all. All the major forces knew about it, but with Black Wind Mountain as his backer, the other forces did not dare make a move against him.
Once the entire human race had moved into that Forbidden... Ye Tian then set up grand formations and completely transformed the Forbidden Void Realm.
At that point, without his permission, even Half-Step Domain Ancestors had no way to break into the human race’s Forbidden Void Realm, unless a Domain Ancestor personally took action.
....Human race.
Ye Tian named this medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm the Human Realm, distinguishing it from the other Forbidden Void Realms. Otherwise, as more and more Forbidden Void Realms appeared, the naming issue would become... a small nuisance, so each Forbidden Void Realm had to be given a name.
And the name Human Realm gradually spread throughout the Xuanxu Ancient Realm and became known to countless forces.
Ye Tian even, for the convenience of Dao Ancestors and True Ancestors traveling freely between the small Forbidden Void Realm and the Human Realm, specifically mobilized the authority of the two Forbidden Void Realms and opened a passage between them.
Of course, authority was still required to pass through that passage, so he forged some tokens. Only by means of these tokens could one enter and leave the two Forbidden Void Realms.
After the human race stabilized, Ye Tian occasionally went out to hunt Forbidden Insects, but spent most of his time cultivating.
In the blink of an eye, three hundred thousand years passed.
At this time.
Ye Xingyue, Xiao Yue, and Ye Yu had all already become Supreme Dao Ancestors, and the human race had also produced quite a few Fifth and Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestors. Even one or two Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors had been born, and the number of Dao Ancestors in the human race had become enormous.
Even the Nine Extremes Legion was now nearly half composed of Dao Ancestors, while the rest were basically top Dao Ancestors, Supreme Dao Ancestors, and Invincible Dao Ancestors.
Of course.
It was not only the human race whose strength had greatly increased. The number of Dao Ancestors in the other forces had also increased enormously, and their prosperity had even surpassed that of the Vast Sea Domain Realm in those days. After all, the Vast Sea Domain Realm had not had Forbidden Insect sacrifices back then, nor such a massive quantity of Forbidden artifacts 0.... For the Vast Sea Domain Realm at that time, any single Forbidden artifact was exceedingly precious.
But now, Forbidden artifacts seemed to have become ordinary resources, so how could the birth of Dao Ancestors and the growth rate of Dao Ancestors possibly not be fast? “The Forbidden Dao Technique: Dark Extreme Dao Spear has finally reached entry level!”
Ye Tian said happily.
After cultivating for so long, with the cultivation boost of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, the assistance of the Forbidden Void Realm, and the effect of his Forbidden talents, he had only just brought Dark Extreme Dao Spear to the entry level. That showed just how difficult it was for a Forbidden Dao Technique to reach even the beginner stage! As far as he knew, the Forbidden Dao Techniques of people like Migudao Ancestor were also only at the entry level.
However, the Forbidden Dao Technique Shadow Pierce had not yet reached entry level, though it was not far off.
In addition, during these years he had also created two more Forbidden Dao Techniques. One was a speed-type Forbidden Dao Technique—Shadow Escape. It was the worst of his Forbidden Dao Techniques, because he did not possess a speed-type Forbidden talent, and being able to create even this Forbidden Dao Technique had already been extremely difficult.
The other Forbidden Dao Technique he created was a defensive Forbidden Dao Technique—Nine Extremes Armor! This Forbidden Dao Technique was also rather ordinary, but when paired with the Forbidden Body, its power was quite impressive.
With four Forbidden Dao Techniques on him, Ye Tian’s weaknesses were almost completely made up for, and along with the increase in his cultivation, his combat power was already 2.
0 far beyond what it had been before.
If he were to fight those five Supreme Dao Ancestors like Yan Ancestor again now, he could absolutely kill them all with ease in a short time. Even if he fought that Commander-level Forbidden Insect again, he could kill it without injury.
Although his realm was still only that of a Supreme Dao Ancestor, his combat power was already enough to rival fairly strong Invincible Dao Ancestors, and in some aspects even surpass them.
“What a pity—my Endless Dao is too powerful. Who knows how long it will take to comprehend the Endless Dao to the ultimate limit? Fortunately, becoming an Invincible Dao Ancestor does not require comprehending the Endless Forbidden Dao to the ultimate limit. Otherwise, I probably would never have any hope in this lifetime!”
Ye Tian murmured.
The Forbidden Dao was vast and profound. Even Domain Ancestors had no way to comprehend it to the ultimate limit, so there was no way he could hope to fully comprehend the Endless Forbidden Dao. Thus, his current goal was no longer to comprehend the Forbidden Dao itself, but rather to do his utmost to comprehend the Endless Dao portion of it.

Chapter 1221 A Forbidden Creature Corpse! Part..

Chapter 1221: A Forbidden Creature Corpse
！【Third Update】
Ye Tian still could not glimpse where the limit of the Endless Dao lay, though of course that did not hinder him from increasing his strength.
Even if he could not advance to Invincible Dao Ancestor over the course of endless years, as long as his strength kept rising, he would still be able to kill Invincible Dao Ancestors. And if his Forbidden Dao Techniques became powerful enough and his attainments in the Forbidden Dao grew even higher, he might even be able to contend somewhat with Half-Step Domain Ancestors....
Of course, that step was incredibly, incredibly difficult.
One day not long afterward.
The Xuanxu Ancient Realm was very peaceful, and the Dark Forbidden Domain was also relatively calm, with only small-scale battles taking place.
Yet a huge shadow drifted through the Dark Forbidden Domain, and along with it came a terrifying biological pressure.
....“What is that?”
Several Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors were searching for Forbidden Insects when they suddenly saw a huge shadowy mass and felt that terrifying biological pressure. Their bodies began trembling uncontrollably, as if they had seen true great terror itself.
They wanted to use their divine senses to investigate the situation there, but once their divine senses stretched over, they found it difficult to advance and could not see clearly what that shadowy mass actually was.
They did not dare approach rashly, afraid of encountering danger.
Thus, one of the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors used an eye technique at the level of a Great Thousand Dao Technique—Thousandfold Heavy Pupil! Boom!!!! Layer upon layer of the void split apart, and the pupil light cut through the darkness, staring directly at the true body of that unknown shadowy mass. .
At last, he saw it.
It was an incomparably enormous body, like a majestic world itself. A single thread of its aura could crush eternal ages, existing on a level vastly beyond so-called Primordial Chaotic Lifeforms, as if it were a truly supreme existence.
Judging from its appearance, this was a creature somewhat like an eagle, but its entire body was covered in black-gold scales, and it had four claws, each one incomparably sharp.
“This... this is a Forbidden creature!!!!”
that Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor said in shock.
He was not sure whether this Forbidden creature was truly dead. If it was not dead, then the three of them would probably be annihilated instantly, with not the slightest chance of survival.
A legendary Forbidden creature! That was a terrifying existence comparable to a Domain Ancestor.
“Retreat!”
“Everyone, retreat now!”
that Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor transmitted.
They did not dare retreat too quickly, lest they cause fluctuations, and instead withdrew silently and slowly. Only after retreating a very, very great distance, so far that they could no longer sense the existence of that Forbidden creature, did they speed up and fly back to their base.
Very soon, a piece of news spread through the major bases.
A Forbidden creature had appeared, and this news was simply too shocking.
It filled countless people with fear.
After all, once a Forbidden creature appeared, they would all be killed, with absolutely no chance of survival. However, Ye Tian received the news at the earliest possible moment.
“A fallen Forbidden creature!”
Ye Tian’s heart stirred, and great interest appeared on his face.
What he first thought of was the Forbidden creature’s Forbidden talents. If he could copy the Forbidden creature’s talents, it would greatly help his strength.
Only after that did he think about the opportunities and treasures on the Forbidden creature’s body.
Whoosh! Ye Tian’s replicated body—the Dark King—set out, following many Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain toward the fallen Forbidden creature.
As for Black Wind Mountain’s Half-Step Domain Ancestors, they had gone long ago and had not waited for Ye Tian and the others at all.
After all, for Half-Step Domain Ancestors, something involving the corpse of a Forbidden creature was an opportunity beyond imagination! If this had been back in the Divine Heaven Domain, even Domain Ancestors would have fought over it. How could it ever have been the turn of Half-Step Domain Ancestors like them! Before long, Ye Tian also arrived at the place where the Forbidden creature’s corpse was located.
At the place where the Forbidden creature had fallen, quite a few Supreme Dao Ancestors, Invincible Dao Ancestors, and Half-Step Domain Ancestors had already gathered.
As for Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors, they simply did not dare approach, because their physical bodies could not withstand the dissipating power of the Forbidden creature. One had to possess a Forbidden Body to endure such power.
Thus, those Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors who possessed Forbidden Bodies could also approach this place, but how many Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors could possess Forbidden Bodies at that level? So the vast majority of Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors had no way to get close. Even if there were opportunities here, they were not for them.
If even Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors were not qualified to approach, then weaker Dao Ancestors had even less hope.
“It really is a Forbidden creature!”
Ye Tian, in the identity of the Dark King, also arrived here. Looking at that Forbidden creature corpse and feeling its pressure, he exclaimed inwardly in surprise.
What made him even more curious was that the body of this Forbidden creature seemed very intact, without any visible injuries.
How powerful were Forbidden creatures? They were comparable to Domain Ancestors. Without having gone through a brutal battle, how could one possibly have fallen? As for dying of old age, that was utterly impossible! The lifespan of a Forbidden creature was almost equal to that of the Dark Forbidden Domain itself. So long as the Dark Forbidden Domain did not perish, the Forbidden creature’s lifespan would remain eternal and indestructible. How could it possibly die because its lifespan had run out? “Could it be that its soul was annihilated?”
Ye Tian guessed.
In addition, he was also curious whether the Mountain Lord of Wind Mountain would appear. Even if the Mountain Lord of Wind Mountain were the legendary Domain Ancestor, he ought to be interested in the corpse of a Forbidden creature, perhaps even taking it away.
“If the Wind Mountain Lord were coming, then with his speed he should already have arrived long ago. Yet he still hasn’t come. Did he give it up? Could it be that the Wind Mountain Lord has some even more important plan, something so important that even the corpse of a Forbidden creature cannot draw him out early?”
Ye Tian wondered.
At this moment, Shenxu Dao Ancestor, Eternal Dao Ancestor, Gengjin Dao Ancestor of Black Wind Mountain, along with the Half-Step Domain Ancestors from the other bases, had all arrived, and they were all studying the corpse of this Forbidden creature.
“Collect!”
The Azure Dragon Palace Master’s power spread across the body of this Forbidden creature, trying to take the corpse away. Yet a force rebounded instantly, directly shaking the Azure Dragon Palace Master until his body cracked all over, even injuring him.
“It won’t work!”
The Azure Dragon Palace Master shook his head. “A Forbidden creature already surpasses all rules. It cannot be taken into an inner world and cannot be carried away! Unless the rules of our inner worlds could rival those of the Dark Forbidden Domain—but that is impossible!”
“Azure Dragon Palace Master, I already told you it couldn’t be taken away, but you refused to believe it. Even Domain Ancestors cannot take away the corpse of a Forbidden creature. Back in the Divine Heaven Domain, those Domain Ancestors all cut the corpse of a Forbidden creature apart and then continuously extracted the power from the corpse. Only after special processing could they take away fragments of the Forbidden creature’s body.
We are not Domain Ancestors, so we truly have no way to deal with this Forbidden creature corpse!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor said with a smile.
Immediately after, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors flew in through the gigantic mouth of this Forbidden creature corpse, preparing to enter the Forbidden creature’s inner world to search for opportunities and seize treasures.
And at this moment, Ye Tian also moved closer to the Forbidden creature corpse. Using his Copy Talent, he extended it forward and barely managed to touch the corpse of this Forbidden creature.
“As expected, it has Forbidden talents!”
Ye Tian was overjoyed.

Chapter 1222 Five Great Worlds!

Chapter 1222: Five Great Worlds

Elsewhere.
Ye Tian’s true body had also arrived, bringing Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue with him. However, Xiao Yue and Ye Yu had not come, as they were still stationed in the Human Realm, managing its affairs, and had long since rarely come out to hunt Forbidden Insects.
“Father, are we going in?”
Ye Xingchen asked.

Time passed little by little, and soon the Half-Step Domain Ancestors sent out a message.
Safe! Thus, one Supreme Dao Ancestor and Invincible Dao Ancestor after another flew into the giant mouth of the Darkwing Roc Eagle, entering its inner world.
Ye Tian and his replicated body, the Dark King, also entered the giant mouth of the Darkwing Roc Eagle.
After many Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors entered the Darkwing Roc Eagle’s body, another group of powerful experts flew over through the void of the distant Dark Forbidden Domain, including some Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors. There were even two mysterious figures who crossed over in an instant and entered the Darkwing Roc Eagle’s body, though it was impossible to tell much about their strength....
These two might have been Invincible Dao Ancestors, or they might have been Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
In any case, with the appearance of this Forbidden creature corpse, many Dao Ancestors who had never appeared before now emerged, clearly hoping to obtain some opportunities from inside the Darkwing Roc Eagle.
....After entering through the Darkwing Roc Eagle’s giant mouth, there was a long passageway. This was the esophagus, and at this moment, countless currents of dark forbidden power had formed into terrifying hurricanes throughout the passage. Anyone below the level of Supreme Dao Ancestor who entered here would be torn into countless fragments in an instant.
Therefore, even if one possessed a Forbidden Body, without the strength of a Supreme Dao Ancestor there was no way to enter. That would be courting death! Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen naturally did not fear these forbidden hurricanes. They easily blocked them and quickly went deeper into the Darkwing Roc Eagle’s inner world.
“Five worlds!”
Ye Tian sensed the fluctuations of five worlds. These five worlds should correspond to the five internal organs of the Darkwing Roc Eagle, representing the five worlds of metal, wood, water, fire, and earth. Each one probably rivaled an ancient realm.
Under normal circumstances, there was no way Ye Tian and the others could invade the five great worlds inside the Darkwing Roc Eagle.
But the situation was different now. The Darkwing Roc Eagle had already fallen. Though there were no wounds on the outside, its inner worlds had lost their normal operation and had begun to crack apart, causing chaos within, with countless spatial fissures densely packed everywhere.
“Be careful!”
Ye Tian reminded his son Ye Xingchen and daughter Ye Xingyue.
Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue both nodded and obediently followed behind Ye Tian.
Since the Dark King was leading the way ahead, Ye Tian’s true body only needed to follow the established route, so the danger was not too great.
Ye Tian passed through one spatial fissure after another, constantly changing routes, and finally entered the first world—the World of Fire.
The World of Fire represented the position of the heart, meaning they had arrived in a world opened up inside the heart of the Darkwing Roc Eagle.
“The laws here are even stronger than those of an ancient realm!”
Ye Tian said in surprise after entering.
But after thinking about it carefully, that made sense. This was one of the five great worlds inside a Forbidden creature, so it was only natural that its laws would be powerful.
“So many Forbidden artifacts!”
Ye Tian said after a casual sweep of his senses.
The Half-Step Domain Ancestors must have come in earlier, but they had not taken away these Forbidden artifacts. They probably looked down on them, and after all, time was very important to them as well, so there was no need to collect Forbidden artifacts that were of little value in their eyes.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!! Ye Tian continuously darted through region after region of the World of Fire, constantly collecting these Forbidden artifacts, practically as if he were picking them up off the ground.
The other Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors were also collecting Forbidden artifacts. No one had time to fight, and everyone remained quite friendly.
Before long, Ye Tian had already collected around a hundred thousand Forbidden artifacts, many of them top-grade Forbidden artifacts.
Unfortunately, he had not collected a single Forbidden supreme treasure. Clearly, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors had casually taken those earlier.
Of course.
Aside from Forbidden artifacts, the World of Fire was hardly devoid of good things.
World of Fire, beneath a spatial fissure.
One Supreme Dao Ancestor and Invincible Dao Ancestor after another gathered here. Ye Tian, Ye Xingchen, and Ye Xingyue also arrived here.
Everyone’s eyes were fixed on a lake of blood. This was no ordinary blood lake, but one formed from the blood of a Forbidden creature, containing terrifying energy.
Of course, this blood lake could not possibly be all of the blood. Otherwise, the Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors present would have gone mad long ago, and even the Half-Step Domain Ancestors would not have ignored it and would already have taken it away.
In truth, this blood river was just a tiny amount of blood leaking out from internal bleeding inside the Darkwing Roc Eagle through this spatial fissure. After evolving over the course of long ages and merging with dark forbidden power, it had eventually become this blood lake.
“…” A Supreme Dao Ancestor who had just arrived looked at the blood lake and could not help but speak.
He immediately made a move to collect the blood lake.
However, a black tentacle shot out from within the blood lake and instantly pierced through that Supreme Dao Ancestor’s body, killing him in a single blow.
“Foolish. He didn’t even notice the Forbidden-bloodline creature beneath the blood lake!”
an Invincible Dao Ancestor said disdainfully.
If there were no danger, how could they possibly not take away this blood lake? After all, the value of this blood lake was immense. Just taking away a little of the lake water and refining it afterward would yield energy liquid suitable for increasing the cultivation of Supreme Dao Ancestors and even Invincible Dao Ancestors.
“Everyone, let’s join forces. This blood lake has already given birth to a Forbidden-bloodline creature. Its strength is far beyond that of an ordinary Invincible Dao Ancestor and likely comparable to the very strongest kind of Invincible Dao Ancestor. If we do not cooperate, we probably have no way to take away this Forbidden blood lake.
And if we waste time here, it will become difficult for us to obtain more opportunities. Time is... resources. Don’t waste any more time!”
an Invincible Dao Ancestor suggested.
“Fine, let’s join forces and kill this Forbidden-bloodline creature first!”
one Invincible Dao Ancestor and Supreme Dao Ancestor after another agreed.
Whoosh! One Invincible Dao Ancestor activated a chain-type Forbidden weapon, which extended directly beneath the blood lake and forcibly dragged out the Forbidden-bloodline creature below.
Roar! A Forbidden-bloodline creature somewhat resembling an octopus appeared, its terrifying aura spreading out and shaking the entire area.
“Attack!”
One Invincible Dao Ancestor and Supreme Dao Ancestor after another made their move.
Ye Tian, Ye Xingchen, and Ye Xingyue also attacked, striking at this Forbidden-bloodline creature with full force.
With so many powerful experts attacking, they almost instantly tore apart the body of that Forbidden-bloodline creature and heavily injured it.

Chapter 1223: Forbidden Blood Crystals
！【First Update, Please Subscribe Fully】
Once the Forbidden-bloodline creature died, everyone began dividing up the blood lake.

However, as the blood lake gradually dried up and the treasure at the bottom was fully exposed, the situation changed abruptly.
At the bottom of the blood lake were black-red crystals, each radiating strands of life aura and Forbidden laws.
“These are blood crystals formed from the coagulated blood of a Forbidden creature—Forbidden Blood Crystals that require endless years of evolution to be born! A single Forbidden Blood Crystal is comparable to a low-grade Forbidden weapon!”
a Dao Ancestor cried out in shock.
Forbidden Blood Crystals were transcendent objects, one of the existences that ignored the rules, so they could not be captured by divine sense. Earlier, when everyone probed the lake bottom with divine sense, they had failed to detect the Forbidden Blood Crystals.
Everyone swept their eyes over them and saw that there were more than sixty Forbidden Blood Crystals in total. But the number of Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors here combined was far greater than sixty! “These Forbidden Blood Crystals are ours!”

But now, in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, there were far too many Forbidden artifacts, so forging Forbidden weapons was no longer especially difficult.
Nowadays, if one wanted to exchange a low-grade Forbidden weapon for a single Forbidden Blood Crystal, one was dreaming! Moreover, even back in the Vast Sea Domain Realm, hardly anyone had been willing to exchange Forbidden Blood Crystals for Forbidden weapons, because the uses of Forbidden Blood Crystals were simply too great.
Forbidden Blood Crystals could repair origin injuries. That alone was enough to attract many Supreme Dao Ancestors who had been unable to advance to Invincible Dao Ancestor because of origin injuries.
In addition, Forbidden Blood Crystals were one of the best cultivation treasures for increasing dark forbidden power, and they could also allow Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors to grasp dark forbidden power. One could imagine how immense their value was! If not for the fact that the energy within Forbidden Blood Crystals was too vast and too advanced for True Ancestors to endure, then Forbidden Blood Crystals would also be supreme treasures for True Ancestors, allowing them to grasp dark forbidden power at the True Ancestor level.
“Hahaha, as long as I seize some Forbidden Blood Crystals, I can repair the origin injury I suffered in the past. I can also greatly increase my dark forbidden power and push my Forbidden Body to minor achievement or even major achievement. My strength will soar by leaps and bounds!”
the Supreme Dao Ancestor—Youming Dao Ancestor—said excitedly.

The Heavenly Demon Sect was one of the Eighth Heaven forces.

Even so, the Heavenly Demon Sect still had not advanced into a Ninth Heaven force.
The main reason was that the Heavenly Emperor Palace had raised the threshold for Ninth Heaven forces: one had to possess ten Supreme Dao Ancestors and at least three Invincible Dao Ancestors to qualify as a Ninth Heaven force. Otherwise, one could only count as an Eighth Heaven force.

Somewhere in the Earth World.
Grain after grain of sand floated in the air, as if fixed in place.
Azure Dragon Palace Master, Eternal Dao Ancestor, and the others were all fighting over those grains of sand, to the point of battle, causing the void in this region to crack apart continuously.
These were no ordinary grains of sand, but Myriad Things Star Sand. To these Half-Step Domain Ancestors, these grains were true supreme treasures.
Myriad Things Star Sand could help Half-Step Domain Ancestors break the shackles of the fleshly body, allowing them to possess up to ten percent of a Domain Ancestor’s bodily might. A body of this level was known as the Myriad Things Body Realm, and its strength could completely overwhelm other Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
Azure Dragon Palace Master was indeed very powerful, but he had not yet condensed the Myriad Things Body Realm, so he also wanted to seize these grains of Myriad Things Star Sand in order to break the shackles of his physical body and reach that realm.
If he succeeded, his strength would surge by another level, completely rising above ordinary Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
But one or two grains of Myriad Things Star Sand were certainly not enough, so they needed to seize as much of it as possible.
Suddenly.

In any case... this person was definitely not from the Heavenly Emperor Palace. Of that point, he was certain.

Everyone, be careful not to be ambushed by the Heavenly Emperor Palace!”

However, the Star Sand Beast was not interested in Myriad Things Star Sand at all, and even somewhat loathed it.

When he saw the Star Sand Beast’s function, Ye Tian smiled.

Chapter 1226 Crazy Collection!

Chapter 1226: Crazy Collection
！【Second Update】
Ye Tian prepared to dismiss… the clone body of Dark King and intended to copy the Star Sand Beast.
Although dismissing the clone body and then using the clone ability again required ten thousand years, even with a hundred-thousand-fold time acceleration, it would still take over a month before the ability could be used again.
Given the current situation, if another month passed, the Myriad Things Star Sand in the Earth World would likely already be completely taken, leaving little behind.
Even a hundred-thousand-fold time acceleration was already the limit under the rules. However, nothing was absolute—if one possessed a time-type forbidden treasure, this limit could be broken, allowing acceleration of a million times or even more.
But time-type forbidden treasures were extremely rare and precious. Even if someone obtained one, they would not waste it merely on time acceleration.
Over these years, Ye Tian had obtained countless forbidden treasures, and he happened to possess a high-grade time-type forbidden treasure that could be used once, accelerating time by about two million times.
By that calculation, ten thousand years would pass for him while only a little over a day would pass outside.
Delaying for just over a day was nothing, since the Earth World was as vast as an ancient realm. With divine sense useless, even half-step Domain Ancestors would need a long time to fully search it.
Ye Tian separated from Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue to search independently, and secretly had Dark King approach his main body.
With a single thought, Ye Tian dissipated the Dark King clone. The forbidden armor, the Slaughtering Heaven Spear, and all previously obtained treasures fell out and were collected by him.
Immediately afterward, Ye Tian began copying the body of the Star Sand Beast.
Whoosh! A massive Star Sand Beast appeared, resembling an enlarged sand mouse covered in thick black scales.
As Ye Tian controlled this body, he felt a strange sensation—somewhere far away, something evoked a strong sense of disgust within the beast. By instinct, the Star Sand Beast would avoid that place.
But Ye Tian was not truly the beast, so he ignored that instinct.
“That place should have Myriad Things Star Sand!”
Ye Tian speculated.
He then controlled the Star Sand Beast to burrow underground toward that location.
Soon, he arrived—and indeed found Myriad Things Star Sand.
However, he did not let the Star Sand Beast collect it. Without the Copy Talent, the beast could not detect surrounding dangers. If a half-step Domain Ancestor or another Dao Ancestor happened to be nearby, the body would be destroyed instantly.
He had no second time-type forbidden treasure, so he could not afford such risks.
The Star Sand Beast’s role was only to locate the sand, while his main body followed behind to check for danger before retrieving it.
Shortly after the beast left, Ye Tian’s main body arrived, scanned the surroundings with his Copy Talent, and safely collected the grain of Myriad Things Star Sand.
And so.
The Star Sand Beast continued locating sand throughout the Earth World, while Ye Tian’s main body gathered it piece by piece. Working together, they harvested a massive amount of Myriad Things Star Sand.
Time passed day by day. The amount of Myriad Things Star Sand dwindled, and after forty days, even the Star Sand Beast could no longer sense any.
Perhaps some still remained in remote areas, but Ye Tian no longer wished to wait.
This time, he had obtained a total of 872 grains of Myriad Things Star Sand.
He did not know how much the half-step Domain Ancestors had gained, but it was certainly less than him.
Afterward, Ye Tian reunited with his children.

Ye Xingchen sighed.
