“Alright!”
The two nodded.
Whoosh whoosh!!! The three left the Earth World through a spatial crack and, after traversing several more, finally arrived in the Metal World.
As soon as they entered, battles erupted everywhere—even half-step Domain Ancestors were fighting.
The place where Ye Tian and the others arrived happened to be a battlefield where four or five Supreme Dao Ancestors were fighting over a mineral vein.
An attack struck toward Ye Tian the moment he appeared.
“Get lost!”
Ye Tian casually blocked it and shouted coldly.
“It’s Myriad Dharma Dao Ancestor!”
The others were startled and immediately fled, not daring to continue fighting.
After they left, Ye Tian and the others looked at the vein.
“Father, it’s a Black Pattern Heavenly Stone vein!”
Ye Xingchen identified it.
“Yes,” Ye Tian nodded. “It contains a trace of forbidden attribute. While it’s not enough to forge forbidden weapons, it can create Dao weapons with forbidden properties. This vein alone could produce tens of thousands of top-tier Dao weapons.”
The three quickly extracted the entire vein and stored it.
Ye Tian knew that the greatest treasures of the Metal World were mineral veins. The Black Pattern Heavenly Stone vein was relatively low-tier, so it did not attract half-step Domain Ancestors or Invincible Dao Ancestors.
Those stronger experts were surely competing for far more valuable veins.
Soon, Ye Tian found several more veins and left his children to gather the lower-value ones.
Meanwhile, he donned Dark King’s equipment and went to compete for the truly valuable veins.
Before long, he arrived at a battlefield where multiple Invincible Dao Ancestors were fighting—including Flowing Fire Dao Ancestor, Jade Cauldron Dao Ancestor, and Golden Buddha Dao Ancestor from Black Wind Mountain.
Ye Tian glanced at the shattered mineral vein—and his pupils shrank.
“This is… an Indestructible Black Gold vein!!!!”

Chapter 1227 Eternal Origin Stone Statue!

Chapter 1227: Eternal Origin Stone Statue
！【Third Update】
The Indestructible Black Gold vein was no ordinary vein, but one capable of forging forbidden weapons. Although it was inferior to the Dark Blunt Gold vein Ye Tian had obtained earlier, its value was still immense.
Even when used alone, Indestructible Black Gold could be forged into mid-grade forbidden weapons. If used in large quantities and refined with high-level craftsmanship, it could even produce high-grade forbidden weapons.
Most importantly, Indestructible Black Gold possessed an indestructible nature—if a weapon made from it were broken, it could automatically restore itself. Other forbidden weapons, once broken, were truly broken, and repairing them would require an enormous cost.
Even Ye Tian’s Slaughtering Heaven Spear would be difficult to repair if shattered by another top-tier forbidden weapon. But if it incorporated Indestructible Black Gold, it could regenerate automatically, greatly increasing its value.
Thus, Indestructible Black Gold was an extremely precious treasure to Ye Tian.
Without hesitation, Ye Tian immediately joined the battle, competing with the Invincible Dao Ancestors for the Indestructible Black Gold.
Using his concealment ability, he approached a chunk of Indestructible Black Gold that had been blasted away, grabbed it instantly, and stored it in his inner world.
In this way, Ye Tian continuously used his concealment to seize pieces of Indestructible Black Gold. The other Invincible Dao Ancestors could not detect him at all—many times, just as someone was about to grab a piece, it would suddenly vanish into Ye Tian’s hands.
“Dark King, you’ve gone too far!”
Wushuang Dao Ancestor roared angrily.
Others relied on strength to compete fairly, but Ye Tian simply snatched everything through concealment—it was shameless.
Of course, what they truly felt was envy.
If they had such an ability, they too could seize far more Indestructible Black Gold.
Ye Tian ignored their anger and continued happily collecting it, quickly gathering a large amount.
Before long, however, the entire vein was exhausted, leaving behind only a massive pit.
The Invincible Dao Ancestors then departed one by one to search for other rare veins.
As time passed, more and more veins were mined, and the resources of the Metal World grew increasingly scarce.
Suddenly.
A strange aura spread out, causing all Dao Ancestors in the Metal World to tremble and instinctively look toward a certain direction.
This aura carried no danger, yet it contained profound forbidden Dao principles, drawing their minds into deep comprehension.
“A great opportunity!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Instantly, Invincible Dao Ancestors and Supreme Dao Ancestors rushed toward that location.
In the Metal World, at the center of a shattered mountain, stood an ancient black statue.
It was a statue of an ape-like figure, holding a spear and standing upright like a human.
Azure Dragon Palace Master, Eternal Dao Ancestor, and the other half-step Domain Ancestors all stared intently at it.
Earlier, they had been fighting here over a top-tier forbidden treasure. During the battle, the mountain shattered—revealing this statue.
Although Azure Dragon Palace Master had taken that treasure, everyone had now completely forgotten about it, their attention fully focused on the statue.
“What material is this statue made of? It gives me a terrifying aura!”
Azure Dragon Palace Master said in shock.
“It should be Eternal Origin Stone,” Eternal Dao Ancestor replied in a low voice.
Eternal Origin Stone was an ancient name—so ancient that even half-step Domain Ancestors barely understood it.
It was said to originate from the depths of the Dark Forbidden Domain, a primordial energy stone that even Domain Ancestors could not absorb.
In historical records of the Divine Heaven Realm, a thumb-sized piece once appeared, sparking fierce competition among Domain Ancestors. Yet in the end, none could make use of it, and it gradually lost attention.
Even so, its value remained unimaginably high.
And here stood an entire statue made of Eternal Origin Stone—an astonishing sight.
Unfortunately, they discovered they could not take it away. It seemed fused with the Metal World itself.
“This statue definitely didn’t originate here naturally. That forbidden creature must have taken it from somewhere in the Dark Forbidden Domain and bound it to this world,” Eternal Dao Ancestor speculated.
“That must be it,” others agreed.
Though they could not take it, none of them left. Instead, they closed their eyes and began cultivating and comprehending it.
The statue was not merely material—it contained profound forbidden Dao principles. Even its posture and spear stance held endless mysteries.
Boom!!! In their perception, the statue transformed into a terrifying giant ape standing in the void, roaring and shaking countless regions of the Dark Forbidden Domain, slaying innumerable forbidden creatures with a single spear strike.
It stood above forbidden creatures—an existence beyond their imagination.
Pfft! Pfft! Pfft!!!
Several half-step Domain Ancestors coughed blood, their expressions drastically changing.
“Retreat! We can’t comprehend it from this distance!”
Azure Dragon Palace Master ordered.
Instantly, they withdrew to a safer distance and resumed comprehension.
Only then did the pressure lessen enough for them to continue safely.
“The original owner of this statue must have been unimaginably powerful!”
they all thought.
Some even speculated that the death of the Darkwing Roc Eagle might have been caused by this statue.
Perhaps it had stolen the statue and attempted to flee, only to be struck down from afar by a being far beyond forbidden creatures, ultimately dying and drifting into this region.
If that were true, the value of this statue would be immeasurable.
“We must comprehend it well. Perhaps it will allow us to break through and become Domain Ancestors—or go even further!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor said excitedly.
Soon, Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors also arrived and witnessed the Eternal Origin Stone statue.

Chapter 1228 Golden Crow Palace Master!

Chapter 1228: Golden Crow Palace Master
！
The Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors did not recognize the Eternal Origin Stone statue at all. One after another, they rushed over, trying to take it away. When they realized it could not be taken, they prepared to use it for comprehension and cultivation instead.
At this moment, those from the three major Ninth-Heaven forces—Black Wind Mountain and Heavenly Emperor Palace—received warnings via voice transmission from the half-step Domain Ancestors. They did not approach to cultivate.
However, the Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors from Eighth-Heaven forces or independent cultivators were unaware of the danger. They moved close to the statue and began comprehending it.
Suddenly.
The aura of a rogue Supreme Dao Ancestor rapidly declined—he silently perished.
And this was only the beginning. Soon, more Supreme Dao Ancestors died one after another. In an instant, seven or eight had fallen, while even Invincible Dao Ancestors were gravely injured and on the verge of death.
“Retreat!”
Only then did those unaware of the situation understand the danger. They quickly withdrew, not daring to continue their comprehension.
“Damn it! The half-step Domain Ancestors clearly knew the situation but only informed their own people!”
Some of them were furious. Fortunately, they had been slower to begin comprehension—otherwise, they might have been among the dead.
At this moment, Ye Tian also arrived and immediately received a warning via voice transmission from Eternal Dao Ancestor.
“Eternal Origin Stone statue!”
It was Ye Tian’s first time hearing of such a thing. But the material itself was secondary—the statue was extraordinary, to the point that even half-step Domain Ancestors would be injured if they approached too closely.
However, Eternal Dao Ancestor also mentioned that the statue contained powerful forbidden Dao principles. If comprehended properly, it would greatly benefit cultivation.
Moreover, this was the final world—most treasures had already been collected. Since they could not do anything with the Darkwing Roc Eagle’s corpse, cultivating here was not a waste of time.
Ye Tian sat cross-legged at a safe distance and began comprehending.
Boom!!!! The statue revealed scene after scene—each depicting a terrifying giant ape fighting in the Dark Forbidden Domain, effortlessly slaying forbidden creatures. Its power was overwhelming.
Every movement was flawless, containing boundless profundity.
Due to the distance, the pressure on Ye Tian was manageable, allowing him to endure.
This was like witnessing a supreme existence demonstrating its forbidden Dao—just understanding a fraction was enough to yield immense benefits.
“What level of existence is this giant ape? Could it be that forbidden creatures aren’t the strongest beings in the Dark Forbidden Domain?”
Ye Tian wondered.
He wanted to ask Ouyang Jiu’er, but after searching, he couldn’t find her.
Since entering the Darkwing Roc Eagle’s inner world, he had not seen her at all. Perhaps she was deliberately keeping a low profile to avoid being discovered by the half-step Domain Ancestors.
Still, based on his understanding of her, she must have entered.
He continued comprehending.
As time passed, Ye Tian’s understanding of the forbidden Dao deepened. From observing the giant ape’s battles, he gradually grasped the direction for creating forbidden Dao techniques.
If he were to create one again, it would take far less time.
And the more he comprehended, the more he realized just how terrifying that existence was.
In the blink of an eye, a month passed.
On this day, the entire Metal World began to tremble violently.
Not just the Metal World—but the entire Darkwing Roc Eagle’s corpse was shaking.
“What’s happening?”
Many Dao Ancestors panicked.
“Everyone, get out!”
The half-step Domain Ancestors ordered.
Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!!! They exited first, quickly leaving the inner world and returning outside.
The Supreme and Invincible Dao Ancestors followed closely behind. Since they already knew the path, exiting was much faster.

At this moment, Ye Tian also sensed Ouyang Jiu’er’s presence.

Ye Tian had no time to communicate with Ouyang Jiu’er.
At this moment, everyone’s attention focused on a few individuals.
Their auras were unfamiliar—but they were undoubtedly half-step Domain Ancestors.
These individuals were attacking the Darkwing Roc Eagle’s corpse—specifically its scales—trying to break them off.
After all, even a single scale from a forbidden creature was an absolute treasure. With minimal refinement, it could become a top-tier forbidden weapon.
Among the three unfamiliar half-step Domain Ancestors, one was even stronger than Azure Dragon Palace Master. He wielded a top-tier forbidden sword and continuously struck the scales, causing the corpse to tremble violently.
“So it’s the Golden Crow Palace Master of Heavenly Emperor Palace. I didn’t expect you to still be alive!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor said.
This revealed their identities—they were from Heavenly Emperor Palace.
Previously, Heavenly Emperor Palace had already revealed four half-step Domain Ancestors. With these three, that made seven—an extremely terrifying force.
“Eternal Dao Ancestor, are you provoking me?”
Golden Crow Palace Master stopped and said coldly.
As the strongest palace master under the Domain Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace in the Hao Hai Domain Realm, his status surpassed Azure Dragon Palace Master.
It had been rumored that he died in the Domain Realm war—but now it was clear he had not.
Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!!! Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, and True Martial Palace Masters appeared beside him.
The seven palace masters of Heavenly Emperor Palace faced the three half-step Domain Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain, and the atmosphere became extremely tense.
Eternal Dao Ancestor said again: “You want to dismantle this forbidden creature’s corpse, right? Why not cooperate and split it equally?”
However, Golden Crow Palace Master sneered: “Split it? No. This corpse belongs to Heavenly Emperor Palace. Whoever disagrees—Eternal Dao Ancestor, if you dare oppose me, I will kill you. You should know I have that ability.”
Having learned about the Eternal Origin Stone statue, his greed had grown even stronger.
With seven palace masters present and his own strength, he believed they could claim the entire corpse.

Chapter 1229 Myriad Realm Body, Myriad Realm Dao!

Chapter 1229: Myriad Realm Body, Myriad Realm Dao

“Migudao Ancestor, Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, Tianfan Dao Ancestor, what are your opinions?”

The main reason was simply that Golden Crow Palace Master was too powerful, and his reputation in the past was too overwhelming.
Azure Dragon Palace Master was very strong, but in truth he did not have many truly terrifying battle achievements. Golden Crow Palace Master was different. In the Divine Heaven Domain, he had once fought five Half-Step Domain Ancestors alone and killed three of them, making his name thunder across the heavens—far beyond Azure Dragon Palace Master.
It was said that during the great war when the domain realm shattered, Golden Crow Palace Master fought an opposing Half-Step Domain Ancestor who had stepped into the Myriad Realm Body level and was slain by that opponent.
But now it seemed that news had been false. Golden Crow Palace Master’s true strength was likely not weaker than a Half-Step Domain Ancestor who possessed a Myriad Realm Body.
Therefore, Migudao Ancestor, Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, and Tianfan Dao Ancestor simply did not dare become enemies of Golden Crow Palace Master.

If this is all you have, then you are still doomed!”

Suddenly.
A terrifying bodily pressure burst forth from Golden Crow Palace Master. Holding the Golden Crow Sword, he struck Eternal Dao Ancestor with a single slash, blasting him away. The terrifying force directly cracked Eternal Dao Ancestor’s body all over.
Boom! Golden Crow Palace Master displayed an unparalleled posture. Every strike wounded the five Half-Step Domain Ancestors, while the five of them could not injure Golden Crow Palace Master at all. His body was simply too terrifying. Moreover, he possessed a supreme Forbidden Dao Source, allowing him to continuously heal his injuries. Even if he suffered a slight wound, he could recover almost immediately.

Unfortunately, only my body entered the Myriad Realm. My Forbidden Dao did not enter the Myriad Realm. If both my Dao and body had entered the Myriad Realm, then at this very moment I would already have stepped into the second stage of Half-Step Domain Ancestor, becoming a true Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor grew extremely solemn. If Golden Crow Palace Master’s Forbidden Dao had also entered the Myriad Realm, then there would be no need to continue fighting at all. Golden Crow Palace Master could easily kill them, these Half-Step Domain Ancestors who were still only in the first stage.
Strictly speaking, the level of Half-Step Domain Ancestor consisted of only three stages.
The first stage was the level of Half-Step Domain Ancestors like them—those whose Forbidden Dao and physical body had not both entered the Myriad Realm.
The second stage was when both the Forbidden Dao and the physical body entered the Myriad Realm, known as a Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
As for the third stage, that was complete perfection in the Myriad Realm. The body would possess power equivalent to thirty percent of a Domain Ancestor’s body, and the Forbidden Dao would likewise hold thirty percent of a Domain Ancestor’s might. At that point, when the body and Forbidden Dao were combined, one could form a Myriad Realm Domain, easily suppressing first-stage and second-stage Half-Step Domain Ancestors. Taking one more step beyond that would be to become a true Domain Ancestor.
In reality, Half-Step Domain Ancestors who entered the second stage almost never appeared in public. They would remain in seclusion until reaching the third stage, and then attempt to break through to the Domain Ancestor level. The struggles of the outside world hardly concerned them.
Thus, even back in the Divine Heaven Domain, it was rare to see a second-stage Half-Step Domain Ancestor, much less a third-stage one.
A Half-Step Domain Ancestor like Golden Crow Palace Master, whose body had entered the Myriad Realm, was already among the most supreme beings in the Half-Step Domain Ancestor realm, far beyond ordinary Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
In the distance.
Ye Tian, Ouyang Jiuer, and others watched the battle. Seeing Golden Crow Palace Master single-handedly suppressing five Half-Step Domain Ancestors, they were filled with shock.
“Golden Crow Palace Master is far too powerful. He is much stronger than Azure Dragon Palace Master!”
Ye Tian thought to himself.
At this moment, he was somewhat worried about Eternal Dao Ancestor and the others. If they were to fall, the consequences would be disastrous.
“No need to worry!”
Ouyang Jiuer’s voice sounded beside him. “If Black Wind Mountain dared to provoke Golden Crow Palace Master, then naturally they are not afraid of him.”
Ye Tian looked toward Ouyang Jiuer, and she continued, “If my guess is correct, Black Wind Mountain has probably also sent a Half-Step Domain Ancestor who is not weaker than Golden Crow Palace Master. That person may be about to act.”
As soon as her words fell, the battle in the distance changed.
Golden Crow Palace Master was suddenly forced back and withdrew from the battle.
On his body, a tiny wound appeared. Someone had just attacked him and broken through his defense in a single strike.
“Who?”
Golden Crow Palace Master said in a grave tone.
Whoosh! The void rippled, and a woman stepped out from it.
“Black Wind Mountain, Miaofa Dao Ancestor!”
the woman said lightly.
“Your Dao has entered the Myriad Realm, but your body has not!”
Golden Crow Palace Master saw through her at once, and his expression became filled with deep wariness.
Dao entering the Myriad Realm was even harder than the body entering the Myriad Realm, because the Dao entering the Myriad Realm had to rely entirely on one’s own comprehension, whereas the body could be brought into the Myriad Realm by means of certain treasures. Myriad Things Star Sand, for example, was one such treasure.
If she had enough Myriad Things Star Sand, this Miaofa Dao Ancestor could raise her body into the Myriad Realm as well, which would mean directly stepping into the second stage of Half-Step Domain Ancestor and completely overwhelming all other Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
At that point, Miaofa Dao Ancestor would need only a few moves at most to kill ordinary Half-Step Domain Ancestors.

“Take it!”
Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor moved first at once.

Golden Crow Palace Master thought to himself.
But did Black Wind Mountain truly possess such a terrifying expert? Or had this person always been hidden in the Vast Sea Domain Realm, staying behind the scenes all along?
In any case, this person might belong to Black Wind Mountain, or to some other force, or might even be a rogue cultivator.
The Eternal Origin Stone statue had been snatched away, and Golden Crow Palace Master could not sense the other party’s presence at all, so naturally there was no way to track them.
And even if he really could track them, he would not dare. If the other party decided to kill him, there was a real chance he would die.
“Let’s go, back to the Heavenly Emperor Palace!”
Golden Crow Palace Master ordered.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!! One Half-Step Domain Ancestor after another of the Heavenly Emperor Palace departed. They did not dare linger here any longer. After all, they had already gained tremendous benefits this time, and they also feared being ambushed by that mysterious powerhouse.
Only after returning to the Heavenly Emperor Palace would even a third-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor be unable to break in.
After the Half-Step Domain Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace left, Miaofa Dao Ancestor spoke up as well: “Let us return too!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor, Shenxu Dao Ancestor, and the others all agreed, following Miaofa Dao Ancestor back to Black Wind Mountain.
Meanwhile, many Dao Ancestors were still snatching up the treasures scattered everywhere after the five great worlds shattered. Some even collected the slightest traces of the Forbidden creature’s blood. Even if they could gather only a single thread of it, it would still be a great harvest.
Ye Tian had little interest in these leftover treasures, so he took Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue and left.
Black Wind Mountain Base.
Ye Tian began organizing his gains. This time, he had obtained an immense number of Forbidden artifacts, multiple Forbidden supreme treasures, and fragments of a top-grade Forbidden Spirit Root Tree.
In addition, something else extremely precious was the Forbidden Blood Crystals.
Forbidden Blood Crystals could enable Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors to master Dark Forbidden Power, and Ye Tian had obtained more than fifty of them. If he used them to cultivate Dao Ancestors, that alone would be enough to foster more than fifty Supreme Dao Ancestors! Of course.
Ye Tian would not use them all for cultivation. He himself also needed to use the Forbidden Blood Crystals to strengthen his Dark Forbidden Power, which would greatly help raise his Forbidden Body.
But the most precious treasure of all this time was undoubtedly the Myriad Things Star Sand. He had obtained over 800 grains of Myriad Things Star Sand, completely enough to bring his physical body into the Myriad Realm.
Of course, refining Myriad Things Star Sand was something for after becoming a Half-Step Domain Ancestor, so for the moment he still could not make use of it.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian began using the top-grade Forbidden Spirit Root Tree fragments to strengthen his Forbidden Dao Power, and occasionally used the Forbidden Blood Crystals to temper his Dark Forbidden Power, thereby improving his Forbidden Body.
Thus, year after year passed, and in the blink of an eye several hundred years had gone by.
At this time.
Ye Tian’s Forbidden Dao Power had increased greatly, and his Forbidden Body had been tempered from seventy-eight percent all the way up to eighty percent.
In just a few hundred years, Ye Tian’s strength had grown a great deal.
On this day.
Ye Tian received a message from Eternal Dao Ancestor, telling him to return to Wind Mountain for a trip.
Ye Tian discovered that his son Ye Xingchen had also received the same message, so he and Ye Xingchen returned to Wind Mountain together.
Xuanxu Ancient Realm, Wind Mountain.
Using the Dark King and Earth King tokens, Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen entered Wind Mountain and met Eternal Dao Ancestor and the others.
“Greetings, Eternal Dao Ancestor!”
“Greetings, Shenxu Dao Ancestor!”
“Greetings, Gengjin Dao Ancestor!”
....Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen greeted each of the Half-Step Domain Ancestors, though they did not see Miaofa Dao Ancestor.
“Dark King, Earth King, the reason we called you back this time is to take you to a certain place!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor said.
“Where are we going?”
Ye Tian asked curiously.
“Come with me!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor brought Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen to a black pagoda. This pagoda had not been here before, so it had clearly been built recently.
Ye Tian discovered that although this pagoda was not a Forbidden weapon, it had used a great many Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures in its construction. Even ores of the level of Indestructible Black Gold had been used in abundance, completely blocking divine sense.
Had he not seen the pagoda with his own eyes, he likely would have been unable to sense its existence at all.
When Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen entered the pagoda, they saw an immense void and, within it, a statue standing in the middle of that vast emptiness.
“The Eternal Origin Stone statue!”
Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen cried out in shock.
At this moment, Ye Tian finally understood that the expert who had snatched away the Eternal Origin Stone statue back then was indeed someone from Black Wind Mountain.
“Eternal Dao Ancestor, was it one of Black Wind Mountain’s experts who seized the Eternal Origin Stone statue?”
Ye Tian asked in astonishment.
“That’s right. It was the Wind Mountain Lord who acted!”
Eternal Dao Ancestor replied. “After all, the value of the Eternal Origin Stone statue is simply too great. It is of enormous help even to the Wind Mountain Lord, so the Mountain Lord was the one who personally took action!”
Ye Tian nodded repeatedly. This Eternal Origin Stone statue was useful even to Domain Ancestors. So even if the Wind Mountain Lord was a Domain Ancestor, there was no way he would let such a statue go. If he had not acted, that would have been truly strange! Eternal Dao Ancestor continued: “Dark King, Earth King, as two of the Ten Kings, you are entitled to one hundred years of comprehension time here. If you wish to continue comprehending here after that, you will need to pay a certain amount of Black Wind Mountain contribution points. That is the rule. Even for me, entering here to cultivate also requires paying contribution points!”
“Understood!”
Ye Tian nodded.
“Remember, this matter must not be leaked. Understood?”
Eternal Dao Ancestor warned them.
Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen both nodded repeatedly, promising not to reveal anything.
After that, Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen did not leave, instead staying behind to cultivate and comprehend here for a period of time.
Back then, Ye Tian had only comprehended the statue for a short while, yet he had already gained immense benefits. If he were allowed to comprehend here for ten thousand years, his Forbidden Dao would certainly advance tremendously, and he might even easily create powerful Forbidden Dao Techniques.
In short, if he could comprehend here for ten thousand years, his strength would inevitably soar.

Chapter 1232 Strength Soars!

Chapter 1232: Strength Soars
！【Please Subscribe Fully】
In the days that followed, Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen remained here comprehending the Eternal Origin Stone statue.
This place was divided into separate regions, with a comprehension tower built in each one. Each person occupied one comprehension tower, without interfering with anyone else.
If one wished to leave, one could simply leave directly from the comprehension tower.
And so, time passed bit by bit.
In the blink of an eye, ten thousand years went by. Aside from occasionally going outside to learn about the situation, Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen spent all their other time cultivating.
Now that many Half-Step Domain Ancestors had revealed themselves in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, the Forbidden Insect Race was no longer considered a threat. It had long since been suppressed into a single region, and the Xuanxu Ancient Realm was raising it like gu, even frequently sending dead creatures to the Forbidden Insect Race so that the nest could breed even more Forbidden Insects.
The Half-Step Domain Ancestors also knew that there was an Insect King cocoon inside the Forbidden Insect nest, but they were not worried.
Since the Half-Step Domain Ancestors were not worried, Ye Tian naturally was not too worried either.
After all, even knowing that an Insect King cocoon existed, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors remained calm, which meant they likely understood the situation of the Insect King cocoon and thus were not afraid of any accidents.
....On this day.
Ye Tian ended his seclusion, as his time for comprehension had run out. Although he could continue comprehending by paying points, there was no particular need for that right now.
After all, he still needed to digest and absorb the gains from this time. Otherwise, if he advanced too quickly, it would bring him no real benefit and would only make him overly ambitious.
At this point, the strength of Ye Tian’s Forbidden Dao was already several times greater than before, and it had also greatly improved his Endless Dao.
Previously, Ye Tian had had no idea where the limit of his Endless Dao lay. If he could not even sense the limit, how could he charge toward the Invincible Dao Ancestor level?
But now, he had sensed the limit of the Endless Dao. If he measured the Endless Dao in percentages, he had already reached about thirty percent. Although he was still very far from the ultimate limit of the Endless Dao, at least he could finally see the end point.
Moreover, he had gained countless insights into Forbidden Dao Techniques, but he still needed to digest them thoroughly before he could truly transform those gains into strength.
Thus, Ye Tian left the comprehension tower, left Wind Mountain, and returned to the Human Realm where the human race was currently located.
After that, Ye Tian began comprehending and cultivating Forbidden Dao Techniques in an environment accelerated by a hundred thousand times.
At present, he had mastered a total of four Forbidden Dao Techniques: Dark Extreme Dao Spear, Shadow Pierce, Shadow Escape, and Nine Extremes Armor. Of these four, only Dark Extreme Dao Spear had reached the entry level.
But now, Ye Tian was confident that he could cultivate all four Forbidden Dao Techniques to the minor mastery level. This showed just how great the help of the Eternal Origin Stone statue had been to him.
In addition, Ye Tian had previously obtained three Forbidden talents from the Darkwing... Among them, the Forbidden talent: Gold Devour was an extremely rare and powerful Forbidden talent. It allowed Ye Tian to devour ores and strengthen his bodily defense.
It could even devour materials such as Indestructible Black Gold. If he had enough ore veins, he could temper his body to a level beyond that of top-tier Forbidden defensive weapons.
At that point, even a Half-Step Domain Ancestor would be unable to kill him in a single strike.
Thus, while comprehending and cultivating the Forbidden Dao, Ye Tian also used the Forbidden talent: Gold Devour to devour all sorts of rare ores in order to improve his bodily defense.
In the blink of an eye, tens of thousands of years passed in the outside world once again.
On this day.
All four of Ye Tian’s Forbidden Dao Techniques had reached the minor mastery level, and the power of each had increased greatly, far beyond that of an uninitiated Forbidden Dao Technique.
This rate of improvement was much faster than before, but Ye Tian had also almost completely exhausted the insights he had gained from comprehending the Eternal Origin Stone statue.
Aside from that, Ye Tian had also created another Forbidden Dao Technique—Myriad Devour! This Forbidden Dao Technique was created entirely based on the Forbidden talent: Gold Devour. It could accelerate the refinement of all kinds of rare ores and materials, and it could also devour part of the enemy’s attack energy, making it extremely terrifying in power.
In addition, with the help of the top-grade Forbidden Spirit Root Tree and the Forbidden Blood Crystals, Ye Tian had raised his cultivation to almost the ultimate limit of a Supreme Dao Ancestor. If his Endless Dao reached its limit, he could even attempt to break through to the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm.
However, Ye Tian’s current combat power had also far surpassed what it had been before, to the point that even he himself could no longer accurately estimate it.
But if he were compared with ordinary Invincible Dao Ancestors, he could easily crush them and even kill them.
“I wonder, if compared with the top existences among Invincible Dao Ancestors, whose combat power would be greater?”
Ye Tian murmured to himself.
On this day.
Many Dao Ancestors discovered that the benefits gained from sacrificing Forbidden Insects had become very small, far less than what they had been at the beginning. As a result, the value of Forbidden Insect corpses kept decreasing, and very few Dao Ancestors were still willing to hunt Forbidden Insects.
Ye Tian knew that this was because the origin of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm no longer had much need for Forbidden Insects. Or rather, sacrificing Forbidden Insects to the origin could no longer significantly strengthen the origin.
If this continued, the Forbidden Insect Race would eventually bring no benefit whatsoever to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm.
Thus, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors of the major forces gathered together for a meeting.
Those attending the meeting were Azure Dragon Palace Master, Eternal Dao Ancestor, and the others. Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor were not interested in this matter, so they did not participate.
At the meeting.
Azure Dragon Palace Master proposed: “.
Everyone, the Forbidden Insect Race no longer has much value to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm. If we continue raising it like gu, it likely will not serve much purpose. I propose that we exterminate the Forbidden Insect Race completely!”
Migudao Ancestor frowned and said, “Azure Dragon Palace Master, although the strength of the Forbidden Insect Race has greatly declined, even we cannot shake the Forbidden Insect nest. I fear that even second-step or even third-step Half-Step Domain Ancestors would be unable to destroy the Forbidden Insect nest.
Moreover, once we enter the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest, we are simply no match for the Lord-level Forbidden Insects. So how are we supposed to wipe out the Forbidden Insect Race completely?”
Migudao Ancestor’s concern was also shared by Zhenyu Dao Ancestor and Tianfan Dao Ancestor. They likewise did not dare rashly enter the depths of the Forbidden Insect nest.
“Rest assured, when the time comes, Golden Crow Palace Master of our Heavenly Emperor Palace and Miaofa Dao Ancestor of Black Wind Mountain will also enter the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest. Your targets will merely be the Commander-level Forbidden Insects.
Don’t tell me that even inside the Forbidden Insect nest, you still can’t defeat Commander-level Forbidden Insects?”
Azure Dragon Palace Master said.
“Then I have no problem with it!”
Migudao Ancestor agreed.
After that, both sides began discussing the issue of dividing the benefits.
In short, once they entered the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest, if there were any gains at all, they would be distributed according to contribution, and no one would be allowed to snatch from one another.
Not long afterward.

Chapter 1233 Charging into the Forbidden Insect Nest!

Chapter 1233: Charging into the Forbidden Insect Nest
！
On this day.
Miaofa Dao Ancestor of Black Wind Mountain led Eternal Dao Ancestor, Shenxu Dao Ancestor, Gengjin Dao Ancestor, Hengguang Dao Ancestor, and Linghe Dao Ancestor—a total of six Half-Step Domain Ancestors—to take part in the battle against the Forbidden Insect Race.
In addition, many Invincible Dao Ancestors and a large number of Supreme Dao Ancestors also joined the battle one after another.
Ye Tian and Ye Xingchen also participated in this battle.
On the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s side, Golden Crow Palace Master led Azure Dragon Palace Master, True Martial Palace Master, White Tiger Palace Master, Vermilion Bird Palace Master, and several other palace masters, along with many emperors and a large number of Supreme Dao Ancestors. Their formation even seemed to surpass Black Wind Mountain’s.
Although the three major Ninth-Heaven forces were somewhat weaker, they still dispatched more than half of their fighting power.
The remaining Eighth-Heaven forces, Seventh-Heaven forces, and Middle Three-Heaven forces also sent many Dao Ancestors to join the battle. Otherwise, even with only the Heavenly Emperor Palace, Black Wind Mountain, and the three major Ninth-Heaven forces, it would still take a long time to wipe out so many Forbidden Insects.
....Dark Forbidden Domain.
Countless Dao Ancestors pushed forward, killing any Forbidden Insects they encountered. Before long, the number of Forbidden Insects had been reduced to fewer than 3 million, and they were directly confined to the territory near the Forbidden Insect nest.
In the void of the Dark Forbidden Domain, one Forbidden Insect after another was pierced through by streaks of light and fell dead.
The Dao Ancestors advanced continuously until they finally pushed to a position close to the Forbidden Insect nest.
At this point, the Forbidden Insects still numbered roughly 2 million, and almost all of them had retreated back into the Forbidden Insect nest.
Clearly, the Forbidden Insect Race understood very well that if all of them remained outside fighting, they would likely all die. It was better to pull their forces back inside the nest and rely on home-field advantage to resist the Dao Ancestors.
“Let’s go in!”
Golden Crow Palace Master said.
Miaofa Dao Ancestor also had the Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain charge into the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest, preparing to battle the Forbidden Insects inside the nest itself.
When the Dao Ancestors of the other forces saw that Black Wind Mountain and the Heavenly Emperor Palace had taken the lead in charging in, they followed them into the interior of the Forbidden Insect nest as well.
Forbidden Insect Nest.
The Dao Ancestors flooded in, and a great number of Forbidden Insects attacked them at once.
Inside the Forbidden Insect nest, the Forbidden Insects could exert even greater power than outside, while the Dao Ancestors could at most bring out thirty percent of their strength.
It could be said that here, Commander-level Forbidden Insects directly crushed Invincible Dao Ancestors, while elite-level Forbidden Insects directly crushed Supreme Dao Ancestors.
However, the Dao Ancestors were too numerous, and the Forbidden Insects’ top combat power was now far too scarce.
The number of Lord-level Forbidden Insects was no longer in the double digits. At present, there were at most seven or eight left, while the Commander-level Forbidden Insects numbered only around twenty-plus.
Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor directly took on all the Lord-level Forbidden Insects, while Azure Dragon Palace Master and the other Half-Step Domain Ancestors were responsible for killing the Commander-level Forbidden Insects. After all, inside the nest, the Invincible Dao Ancestors were simply no match for Commander-level Forbidden Insects and could even be easily killed by them.
Therefore, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors had to fight the Commander-level Insects.
Ye Tian directly took on an elite-level Forbidden Insect. Most other Supreme Dao Ancestors could not defeat elite-level Forbidden Insects, but Ye Tian completely overwhelmed them with ease.
“Shadow Pierce!”
With one strike of the Slaughtering Heaven Spear, he directly pierced through an elite-level Forbidden Insect, heavily wounding it instantly.
After a few more attacks, that elite-level Forbidden Insect fell dead.
“I’m being suppressed far too much. If this were outside, I could kill it with a single easy strike!”
Ye Tian muttered.
Even so, he still did his utmost to kill elite-level Forbidden Insects.
As for Commander-level Forbidden Insects, there was nothing he could do for now—not because he could not defeat them, but because it was extremely difficult to kill one.
Killing Commander-level Forbidden Insects was currently the task of the Half-Step Domain Ancestors, not the task of a mere Supreme Dao Ancestor like him.
As time passed, the number of Forbidden Insects sharply decreased, and soon dropped to around 1 million.
At this point, the Forbidden Insect Tree was still continuously producing Forbidden Insects, but lacking energy, it could not create very many.
Thus, the Forbidden Insect Tree began focusing all its effort on nurturing the Forbidden Insect King.
If someone were to come to the Forbidden Insect Tree, they would be able to see that countless cocoons were beginning to wither, instantly turning to ash, while the energy from those cocoons was being transferred into the Insect King cocoon at the very top.
By sacrificing countless cocoons and exhausting the very origin of the Forbidden Insect Tree, it was possible to forcibly catalyze the Forbidden Insect King into being.
Very quickly, the aura of the Forbidden Insect Tree grew weaker and weaker and gradually began to wither, while the aura of the Insect King cocoon became more and more powerful.
And as the Forbidden Insect Tree withered, the entire Forbidden Insect nest began to develop problems. The suppression on the Dao Ancestors grew lower and lower.
The Forbidden Insect Tree was the core energy source of the Forbidden Insect nest. Once the Forbidden Insect Tree weakened, the nest itself naturally began to fail as well.
But the Forbidden Insects had no other choice. If they did not do this, then once the Forbidden Insect Race was exterminated, what use would an intact Forbidden Insect nest be? Thus, they would rather allow the Forbidden Insect nest to suffer great damage if it meant catalyzing the birth of the Insect King.
Once the Insect King was born, with its strength, it would certainly be able to save the Forbidden Insect Race.
At that point, the Insect King could lead the Forbidden Insect Race over long years and eventually restore both the Forbidden Insect Tree and the Forbidden Insect nest.
80,000! 70,000! 60,000! The number of Forbidden Insects kept dropping, and the pressure on the Dao Ancestors became smaller and smaller.
About three more days passed.
At this point, the number of Forbidden Insects had already dropped below 100,000, and a significant portion of them were elite-level Forbidden Insects.
And basically every elite-level Forbidden Insect required at least more than ten Supreme Dao Ancestors to surround and attack it in order to barely contend with it, while top Commander-level Forbidden Insects could even preserve their lives against Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
In particular, the strongest Commander-level Forbidden Insect had still not been seriously wounded up to now. Its strength was incomparably terrifying.
As for the Lord-level Forbidden Insect battlefield, although Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Palace Master had tied down the Lord-level Forbidden Insects, they too were heavily suppressed here, while the Lord-level Forbidden Insects had grown stronger.
Therefore, Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Palace Master still needed a certain amount of time to kill these Lord-level Forbidden Insects.
However, as the Forbidden Insect Tree grew weaker and weaker, the power that Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor could unleash naturally became stronger, and the situation of the Lord-level Forbidden Insects became extremely dangerous.
Suddenly.
A Lord-level Forbidden Insect that had long since been badly wounded was directly killed by Golden Crow Palace Master with a single sword strike.
Then the other Lord-level Forbidden Insects also began to suffer heavy injuries and edge toward death. The gap in strength between the two sides was simply too great! “Miaofa Dao Ancestor, let’s hurry. Don’t let that Insect King come out, otherwise it will be a huge problem!”
Golden Crow Palace Master urged.

Chapter 1234 Low-Grade Bug King!

Chapter 1234: Low-Grade Bug King
！
Miaofa Dao Ancestor also knew that the Forbidden Bug King must not be allowed to emerge, otherwise things would truly become troublesome.
After all, they were far, far from being a match for a Bug King.
Immediately, Miaofa Dao Ancestor and Golden Crow Palace Master went all out and charged toward the Forbidden Bug Tree.
However, those Lord-level Forbidden Insects blocked Miaofa Dao Ancestor at all costs, even forcibly enduring the attacks of Miaofa Dao Ancestor and Golden Crow Palace Master without dodging at all.
Under such circumstances, another Lord-level Forbidden Insect soon failed to withstand its injuries and fell dead.
At this moment.
The void inside the Forbidden Insect Nest kept collapsing. This was because the Bug King cocoon was drawing too much of the Forbidden Bug Tree’s origin, causing the Forbidden Insect Nest to collapse on a large scale.
Of course, even so, the Forbidden Insect Nest itself would not shatter or be destroyed.
Buzz!!!! A ripple spread throughout the entire Forbidden Insect Nest, making countless Dao Ancestors tremble in spirit.
This was the aura fluctuation of the Bug King! “Not good, the Bug King is about to emerge!”
Miaofa Dao Ancestor cried out in alarm.
At this point, there were only four Lord-level Forbidden Insects left, and each was heavily injured. All the other Lord-level Forbidden Insects had already fallen.
At once, Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor used some kind of Forbidden supreme treasure to instantly trap two Lord-level Forbidden Insects, then forcibly broke free from the interception of the other two and shot toward the Forbidden Bug Tree.
Very soon, they arrived at the tree and each unleashed their strongest attack.
Golden Crow Palace Master activated a Heavenly Emperor weapon and unleashed a terrifying strike onto the Bug King cocoon.
Miaofa Dao Ancestor also used a terrifying great killing weapon capable of erupting with a full-force strike comparable to that of a second-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor, and it too struck the Bug King cocoon.
Crack!!! The Bug King cocoon split open, and a purple insect leg stretched out from inside.
Seeing this insect leg, both Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor’s expressions changed drastically.
The Bug King was not dead. It had truly been born.
Boom!!! The Bug King cocoon completely shattered, and a Forbidden Bug King only half the size of an ordinary Forbidden Insect emerged.
Its terrifying aura spread out, forcing Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor to keep retreating.
“It hasn’t reached the Domain Ancestor level!”
Golden Crow Palace Master said in relief.
“Indeed, it hasn’t reached the Domain Ancestor level!”
Miaofa Dao Ancestor nodded. “We had already estimated before that, with the Forbidden Insect Nest in its current state, it was simply impossible to nurture a true Bug King.
Even if the Forbidden Insects exhausted their origin and sacrificed all the cocoons, they still could not create a true Bug King.
This Bug King is only a low-grade version. Its strength is far from the Domain Ancestor level. It should only be equivalent to a top second-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor, though its defense probably surpasses that of a third-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor, second only to a Domain Ancestor!”
A top second-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor was already an incredibly powerful existence, one they simply could not defeat.
Of course, this was already the best possible situation.
If a true Bug King had emerged, it would have killed them in a single strike.
“We must stop it! Otherwise, once it devours too many living beings, even if it still can’t become a true Bug King comparable to a Domain Ancestor, it will probably still become strong enough to match a third-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor. At that point, we won’t even have the qualifications to resist!”
Golden Crow Palace Master warned Miaofa Dao Ancestor.
“I understand!”
Miaofa Dao Ancestor nodded.
Then the two of them transmitted messages to the other Dao Ancestors, telling them to withdraw from the Forbidden Insect Nest.
....“The Bug King has emerged!”
Ye Tian sensed the Bug King’s aura in the distance and received Miaofa Dao Ancestor’s transmission, and his expression changed drastically.
The only fortunate thing was that this was just a low-grade Bug King, with combat power only equivalent to a top second-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor. Otherwise, there would be no point in even fighting.
“Withdraw!”
One Dao Ancestor after another retreated out of the Forbidden Insect Nest.
And at this point, there were very few Forbidden Insects left, so they had no way to stop the Dao Ancestors.
At this moment, Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor were also doing their utmost to resist the Bug King.
Fortunately, this Bug King had poor combat technique and possessed very few methods. It relied purely on attack power and speed at the level of a second-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor, and occasionally even Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor could not block it.
But Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor could only use Forbidden Dao Techniques and various secret arts to evade and restrict the Bug King. They simply did not dare let themselves be struck by it, because even one touch would heavily injure them.
Before long, almost all the Dao Ancestors had withdrawn from the Forbidden Insect Nest.
Outside the Forbidden Insect Nest.
A great number of Dao Ancestors fled in all directions as fast as they could, not daring to remain here at all.
Although the Half-Step Domain Ancestors had said that this Bug King was only equivalent to a top second-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor, its strength still far exceeded Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor. Because of that, they truly had no confidence at all in Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor.
Ye Tian’s true body left together with Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue. Although he was curious and also wanted to copy the Bug King’s Forbidden talents, there was no way he would risk his true body.
As for the copied body, Dark King, it only remained watching from afar and did not charge over, because if Dark King’s identity were exposed, it would not be worth it.
Soon.
Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor rushed out dragging their injured bodies behind them, followed by a purple Forbidden Insect—the Bug King itself.
At this moment, the Bug King was incomparably furious, wishing it could kill every last Dao Ancestor.
At this point, Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor could no longer bother with the other Dao Ancestors and fled with all their might, quickly shaking off the Bug King.
0After all, the Bug King’s pursuit methods relied only on speed, which was too one-dimensional, making it difficult for it to truly catch Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor.
Those Dao Ancestors who were slower or still watching the battle were miserable. They were slaughtered cleanly by the Bug King, and their corpses were devoured into its body, becoming nourishment for its growth.
In the void of the Dark Forbidden Domain, Ye Tian’s copied body, Dark King, stood there, sensing the Bug King’s aura growing closer and closer.
All the treasures on him had already been transferred to the true body, so even if he fell here, there would be no real loss.
He was waiting for that Bug King, curious about what talents it possessed.
Very soon, the Bug King arrived. Upon seeing Ye Tian, it prepared to swallow him in one gulp.
Copy Talent, investigate! In an instant, all the Bug King’s talents were seen through by Ye Tian.
【Forbidden Talent: Dark Spear】【Forbidden Talent: Purple Armor】【Forbidden Talent: Perception】Three great Forbidden talents—more than other Lord-level Forbidden Insects. Fortunately, it did not possess the Forbidden Talent Stealth, otherwise this Bug King’s threat level would have risen several times over.
Without a second word, Ye Tian directly copied all three Forbidden talents.
Then, he canceled the copied body ability. This copied body instantly collapsed and dissipated, not giving the Bug King any chance to devour it.
“”
The Bug King was very puzzled. Where had that little bug just gone? Why had it suddenly disappeared? It did not think too much about it and immediately went off to chase and kill the other Dao Ancestors.

Chapter 1235 Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor!

Chapter 1235: Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor
！【Please Subscribe Fully】
The Bug King was almost impossible for anyone to defeat. Any Dao Ancestor it pursued was nearly unable to escape, and all were killed and devoured by it one after another.
Shortly after the Bug King gave chase, a figure appeared and blocked its path.
This person wore a black robe and a white mask, and with one hand he sent the Bug King flying, displaying incomparably terrifying combat power.
“What a pity. You are only an underdeveloped Bug King. If you were a true Bug King, I would still fear you somewhat!”
the man said.
Roar! The Bug King flew into a rage and charged at the man.
Yet no matter how it attacked, it could not injure the man in the slightest, while any casual strike from the man was enough to wound it.
Its shell, said to have defense surpassing even third-step Half-Step Domain Ancestors, gradually began to crack, and purple blood flowed out, splattering across the void.
The Bug King was not lacking in intelligence. Realizing it was no match for the man, it prepared to flee.
However, the man pointed a finger, and this stretch of void seemed to be isolated from the outside world, completely sealed off. No matter how the Bug King tried to flee, it could not escape this place.
“Stop trying to run. This is my Forbidden Dao Technique—Infinite Void. Unless you possess an attack method at the Domain Ancestor level, ‘Zero Four Seven’
you will never be able to break out of here. You will remain trapped here forever!”
the man said calmly.
Suddenly.
A Forbidden spear was condensed directly by the man, carrying terrifying Forbidden laws as it descended.
Bang! The Bug King was blasted flying by a single strike, and the shell on its body cracked open, leaving a small hole.
Just like that, the Bug King was beaten continuously, and before long it was badly injured.
“Don’t worry, I won’t kill you. A living Forbidden Bug King is worth far more than a dead one.
If you hand over your soul origin, I can spare your life!”
the man said.
However, the Bug King was not afraid of death at all, so naturally it would not surrender its soul origin.
It only attacked the man more furiously, refusing to yield even though it had already been gravely wounded.
Seeing this, the man sighed. “So be it. Then I can only heavily injure you first and subdue you slowly afterward!”
Boom!!! The man transformed into a giant tens of millions of feet tall, then unleashed a fist-type Forbidden Dao Technique, striking the Forbidden Bug King with a single punch.
With a thunderous crash, the void shattered, and the Forbidden Bug King was heavily wounded by one punch, its body sent flying hundreds of thousands of miles away.
Then the giant hand of the man seized the Forbidden Bug King in one grasp, and the terrifying force caused the Bug King’s body to crack continuously, its aura growing weaker and weaker.
When the Bug King’s aura had weakened to a certain point and it was nearly unable to resist, the man took out a sealing-type supreme treasure, preparing to seal the Forbidden Bug King inside and take it away.
But at that very moment, a ray of light pierced through the void and shot over.
Bang! The man raised his hand and blocked the attack, but a small bloody hole was punched through his palm.
One had to know that even the attacks of the Forbidden Bug King had not caused him the slightest damage, yet this unknown attack had broken through his defense. Clearly, the enemy was no weakling.
Whoosh! The man looked toward the distant void, where a person shrouded in mist appeared.
The person was staring directly at the man.
“A Half-Step Domain Ancestor at the peak of the Unity Realm. Who are you? Your aura is unfamiliar—I have not even heard of you!”
the man said.
The second step of the Half-Step Domain Ancestor realm was generally referred to as the Myriad Realm. Merely having the body enter the Myriad Realm, or merely having the Forbidden Dao enter the Myriad Realm, did not count as a true Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor. Only when both the body and the Forbidden Dao had entered the Myriad Realm could one truly be called a Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
But once one reached the third step, when both the Myriad Realm body and the Myriad Realm Forbidden Dao had been cultivated to the utmost perfection, that realm was called the Unity of Myriad Things—known as a Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
If the body and Forbidden Dao were completely fused, the Forbidden Body reached tenfold perfection, and one grasped the true meaning of a Domain Ancestor, then one could attempt to break through into the Domain Ancestor realm.
In truth, any Half-Step Domain Ancestor could, by steadily cultivating and enduring through endless years, eventually enter the Domain Ancestor realm. It was just that for some Half-Step Domain Ancestors, the years required were far too long—so long that even they themselves could not bear to wait.
Not every Half-Step Domain Ancestor could continue to endure like that, so many of them also sought opportunities to accelerate their cultivation and reach the Unity Realm as quickly as possible, in order to then challenge the Domain Ancestor realm.
And this mysterious person cloaked in mist was precisely a Half-Step Domain Ancestor at the ultimate perfection of the Unity Realm, only one step away from the Domain Ancestor level.
What the other party lacked was merely one condition—either the fusion of Forbidden Dao and body, or perhaps the Forbidden Body had not yet reached perfect completion, or perhaps the true meaning of a Domain Ancestor had not yet been mastered.
In short, the other party was definitely missing one final condition, which was why they had not yet entered the Domain Ancestor realm.
But a Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor like this would certainly once have had a resounding reputation, though identifying exactly who they were was very difficult.
After all, if enough years had passed and they had not come out to act for a very long time, who could possibly know who they were? The mysterious figure looked at the masked man and chuckled, “Your Excellency should be the Wind Mountain Lord of Black Wind Mountain, correct?”
The masked man, who was indeed the Wind Mountain Lord, said in surprise, “I did not expect you to know me. Could you be someone from the Heavenly Emperor Palace? No... the Heavenly Emperor Palace should not have a Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor like you. Besides, even Vast Sea Domain Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace might not necessarily know the true situation of our Black Wind Mountain.”
“I never said I came from the Heavenly Emperor Palace!”
the mysterious man sneered. “The Heavenly Emperor Palace is indeed very strong, but only because Vast Sea Domain Ancestor is strong. The foundation of the Heavenly Emperor Palace is still lacking. Before Vast Sea Domain Ancestor rose to power, the Heavenly Emperor Palace was only an ordinary Ninth-Heaven force, not even comparable to the foundation of your Black Wind Mountain.
Vast Sea Domain Ancestor was also too greedy. What he wanted to seize was far too great, and he overstepped himself, which was why several Domain Ancestors took action against him.
He believed that by throwing one-third of the domain realm fragments into the Dark Forbidden Domain and gambling once, he could carry out his plan.
But he had no idea that such powerful beings had already infiltrated the domain realm fragments. Wind Mountain Lord, you could originally have easily left the domain realm fragments. I suspect you dared venture deep into the Dark Forbidden Domain precisely because you also knew these fragments could lead to a new realm, didn’t you?”
“So you are not a Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace?”
Wind Mountain Lord smiled and said, “There is one thing you did say correctly. I did indeed know that the domain realm fragments could lead to a new realm, otherwise I would never have dared to risk bringing Wind Mountain into the Dark Forbidden Domain... You should know this as well, or you would not have said such a thing.
Might you happen to know the origin of that treasure that fused into the domain realm fragments?”
“I do not know!”
the mysterious man replied. “I only know that the treasure can search for realms in the Dark Forbidden Domain and evolve worlds. Once that evolving world becomes a Forbidden Realm, it will continuously devour an entire realm, thereby advancing into an unprecedentedly vast world.
The Divine Heaven Domain was far too strong. Vast Sea Domain Ancestor did not dare do such a thing inside the Divine Heaven Domain, because before he could finish his plan, some ancient Domain Ancestors would already have killed him.
That is why he chose to take a risk, searching for another realm in order to execute his plan.
But unfortunately, it seems quite a few people know of this plan. He is destined to busy himself for nothing!”
“Hahaha, how do you know he will busy himself for nothing?”
Wind Mountain Lord laughed. “The trump cards and hidden arrangements Vast Sea Domain Ancestor left behind are things neither you nor I fully understand.
And once the Forbidden Realm is formed and the Heavenly Emperor Palace locates it, if Vast Sea Domain Ancestor has not fallen, he will certainly come here.
At that point, it would be no problem for him to take control of this place.
After all, he is a mighty expert in the later stage of the Domain Ancestor realm.... not some newly advanced Domain Ancestor who has only just stepped into that level!”
The mysterious man did not deny it, but instead nodded. “What you say is also true. We indeed do not know Vast Sea Domain Ancestor’s hidden arrangements. But I know very well that your Black Wind Mountain also has its own plans in this matter. In fact, the news that Vast Sea Domain Ancestor obtained that treasure—wasn’t it your people who leaked it? After all, your Black Wind Mountain could not deal with Vast Sea Domain Ancestor alone, so you could only rely on other Domain Ancestors. Indeed, you likely know even more hidden secrets than I do.”
“We will not acknowledge any of that!”
Wind Mountain Lord flatly denied it.
“Hahaha, whether you acknowledge it or not does not matter. I have not come this time to be your enemy.”
the mysterious man said. “I want half of this Bug King’s blood and a portion of its body. A Bug King will not die from losing these things. ‘2.
2’ It will simply grow back. That request is not excessive, is it?”
“Not excessive!”
Wind Mountain Lord agreed.
At once, he directly cut away half of the Bug King’s body and handed it over to the mysterious man.
Then the mysterious man departed.
Watching the mysterious man vanish, Wind Mountain Lord could not help but frown. “Not from the Heavenly Emperor Palace... Could it be one of the Domain Ancestors’ people?”
Of course, it was also possible that this person really was a Half-Step Domain Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace and had deliberately spoken that way.
In short, the situation in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm had now grown more and more complicated.
....Far away, the mysterious man looked in the direction of Wind Mountain Lord and murmured, “Wind Mountain Lord is truly powerful. I practically used my full force, yet I only managed to break his defense without really injuring him. His strength is also infinitely close to the ultimate level of a Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
Moreover, is that really his true body?”
Rumor had it that Wind Mountain Lord was a Domain Ancestor, but from what he had seen today, that did not seem to be the case.
But what if this was merely Wind Mountain Lord’s avatar? “Wind Mountain Lord, we will meet again in the future!”
The mysterious man slipped into the void and vanished completely.

Chapter 1236 The Heavenly Emperor Palace’s Concerns!

Chapter 1236: The Heavenly Emperor Palace’s Concerns
！【Please Subscribe Fully】
Not long afterward, many Dao Ancestors discovered that the Bug King had disappeared.
Soon after, Black Wind Mountain sent Dao Ancestors to investigate and discovered that the Bug King had truly vanished. They then dispatched a large number of Dao Ancestors to charge into the Forbidden Insect Nest once again, killing off the remaining Forbidden Insects one by one, and the Forbidden Insect... was destroyed.
Once the Forbidden Insect Tree was destroyed, although the Forbidden Insect Nest had not yet shattered, it was no longer as sturdy as before.
Moreover, the Forbidden Insect Nest had lost its former breeding ability and could no longer give birth to new Forbidden Insects.
Unless, after the passage of a very long time, a new Forbidden Insect Tree was born again inside the Forbidden Insect Nest.
But the Xuanxu Ancient Realm would never allow such a thing to happen and would certainly station forces here.
Black Wind Mountain moved very quickly, transporting away everything of value inside the Forbidden Insect Nest at the first possible moment. They then made some modifications and turned it into a base.
The Heavenly Emperor Palace moved a little more slowly. After all, they had not known that the Bug King had disappeared. By the time the Dao Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace entered the Forbidden Insect Nest, the place was completely empty, with nothing left behind. Even the fragments of the Forbidden Insect Tree had vanished.
....Heavenly Emperor Palace 21.
Golden Crow Palace Master, Azure Dragon Palace Master, True Martial Palace Master, White Tiger Palace Master, and many other palace masters were holding a meeting, and the subject of the meeting was precisely the Bug King.
“Everyone, have you found any information about the Bug King?”
Golden Crow Palace Master asked.
“No trace!”
Azure Dragon Palace Master shook his head. “The Bug King just suddenly disappeared. Logically speaking, regardless of whether it continued chasing us or not, it should not have abandoned the Forbidden Insect Nest! But now the Bug King has truly vanished, and the Forbidden Insect Nest has already been transformed by Black Wind Mountain.
I think Black Wind Mountain must know what happened to the Bug King. Otherwise, Black Wind Mountain would not have dared to act so boldly!”
“Could it be that an expert from Black Wind Mountain killed the Bug King?”
White Tiger Palace Master guessed.
At the thought of this possibility, White Tiger Palace Master and the other palace masters all became worried.
After all, that Forbidden Bug King had been incomparably powerful. Even Golden Crow Palace Master had not been its match. It possessed the combat strength of the most powerful second-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor, in other words, the most powerful Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
For such a powerful Forbidden Bug King, even a third-step Half-Step Domain Ancestor—a Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor—would likely find it difficult to kill it. And if it had been given a little more time, that Forbidden Bug King could have raised its strength to the Unity Realm.
At that point, aside from a very few Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestors, only a Domain Ancestor could have killed it.
If Black Wind Mountain had truly killed that Forbidden Bug King, then that meant Black Wind Mountain possessed at least one Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
“It may not necessarily have been Black Wind Mountain that killed the King. There may be some other explanation!”
Golden Crow Palace Master hurriedly said.
He said this on the surface, but in truth he was deeply worried inside.
On the surface, he was the strongest in the Heavenly Emperor Palace.
But in truth, the Heavenly Emperor Palace also had several ancient palace masters who belonged to the same generation as Vast Sea Domain Ancestor.
At the beginning, Vast Sea Domain Ancestor had not been the master of the Heavenly Emperor Palace. He had risen step by step from weakness, advancing through the levels of Invincible Dao Ancestor, Half-Step Domain Ancestor, and finally Domain Ancestor.
Strictly speaking, Vast Sea Domain Ancestor should be regarded as the second Heavenly Emperor, while under the first-generation Heavenly Emperor there had also been many ancient and powerful palace masters, several of whom had once been stronger than him.
Only after Vast Sea Domain Ancestor took control of the Vast Sea Domain Realm did those ancient palace masters travel through the Divine Heaven Domain and the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Before the great war when the domain realm shattered arrived, those ancient palace masters also returned. Now, they too had arrived in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, but they still remained in slumber and would not be awakened unless absolutely necessary.
And all of them were at the level of Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestors—true Myriad Realm experts—and were not very far from the Unity Realm. One of them was even comparable to the most powerful Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestors.
Yet even that ancient palace master still could not kill the low-grade version of the Forbidden Bug King! If Black Wind Mountain truly had the power to eliminate the Forbidden Bug King, then that would be enough to prove that Black Wind Mountain’s strength had surpassed that of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, which was not a good thing.
The Heavenly Emperor Palace certainly had trump cards, but some of those trump cards could not be used lightly. Otherwise, the Heavenly Emperor Palace would lose its leading position and would no longer be able to intimidate the other forces.
These palace masters discussed the matter for a long time, yet still came up with no countermeasure. They could only investigate the matter as much as possible.
At the same time, they also needed to use the many treasures obtained from the Darkwing Roc Eagle to strengthen their own power and try their best to produce several more Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestors for the Heavenly Emperor Palace.
Elsewhere.
Ye Tian returned to the Human Realm in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm. Now that the matter of the Forbidden Insect Race had come to an end, although he did not know what had happened to the Forbidden Bug King, he did not care too much about it.
In any case, he no longer needed to enter the Dark Forbidden Domain to hunt Forbidden Insects, and could focus on steadily increasing his strength.
Ye Tian fused the three Forbidden talents he had copied from the Bug King one by one. Forbidden Talent: Dark Spear and Forbidden Talent: Purple Armor were not particularly precious to Ye Tian, because he already possessed Forbidden Talent: Dark Spear, and although he had not previously had Purple Armor, he had already copied a similar Forbidden talent from the Darkwing Roc Eagle.
But Forbidden Talent: Perception was much rarer. It was the first time he had copied a perception-type Forbidden talent.
Only after fusing it did Ye Tian realize just how powerful a perception Forbidden talent was.
For example, if someone possessed a stealth-type Forbidden talent, he could still sense that person’s existence by using the perception Forbidden talent.
He could even sense Ouyang Jiuer’s presence when she used Shadowless Godstep.
With a perception-type Forbidden talent, Ye Tian had now made up for this weakness of his. He no longer... had to fear being ambushed by others.
From this point on, Ye Tian focused on increasing his cultivation and comprehending the Endless Dao.
As time passed, before long Ye Tian’s cultivation had reached the absolute limit of a Supreme Dao Ancestor. His physical strength, Forbidden Dao Power, and soul power had all reached their peaks. If he did not enter the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm, then his cultivation would not be able to advance even half a step further.
In addition, Ye Tian’s Forbidden Dao Techniques had also basically entered a state of stagnation. Unless he once again went to comprehend the Eternal Origin Stone statue, there was no way to rapidly improve his attainments in Forbidden Dao Techniques, and progress would require a very long time.
Of course, this so-called stagnation was only compared to Ye Tian’s previous rate of progress. To others, and even to Half-Step Domain Ancestors, Ye Tian’s speed of improvement in Forbidden Dao Techniques was still incomparably fast, far surpassing the speed at which other Half-Step Domain Ancestors improved.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian occasionally entered Wind Mountain’s comprehension tower to study the Eternal Origin Stone statue. Ouyang returned to the Human Realm to cultivate in seclusion, while sometimes Ouyang went to guide and train the Dao Ancestors of the human race.
Thus, 550,000 years passed.

Over the course of more than five hundred thousand years, the changes in the human race had been enormous.
The human race did not lack geniuses, and with the time-flow advantage of the small Forbidden Void Realm, their growth rate had been exceptionally fast. A huge number of Dao Ancestors had been born, and gradually batches of Fifth-Heaven and Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestors had appeared. There had even emerged several Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors.
Of course, those few Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors were within the Nine Extremes Legion, but they were still members of the human race.
On this day.
Ye Tian summoned those six Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors and bestowed six Forbidden Blood Crystals upon them.
These six were all Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors who had advanced up from Invincible True Ancestors. Their potential was good, and they all possessed the potential to advance into Supreme Dao Ancestors. However, it was relatively difficult for them to grasp Dark Forbidden Power. If they relied on the path of supreme power to advance into Supreme Dao Ancestors, the time required would be rather long.
Therefore, Ye Tian granted them six Forbidden Blood Crystals, which could help them condense Dark Forbidden Power and thereby easily allow them to charge into the Supreme Dao Ancestor realm.
After obtaining the Forbidden Blood Crystals, these six Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors all returned to cultivate in seclusion.
They had already cultivated for vast ages within the small Forbidden Void Realm, and their cultivation had long since reached the ultimate limit of Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors. Moreover, they had no intention of accumulating for even longer. Once they refined the Forbidden Blood Crystals and grasped Dark Forbidden Power, and once their attainment in Dark Forbidden Power improved somewhat, they could begin trying to break through to the Supreme Dao Ancestor realm.
Therefore, the Nine Extremes Legion would very soon give birth to six Supreme Dao Ancestors.
In Black Wind Mountain, even among the Ten Kings who possessed Supreme Dao Ancestor legions, there were probably none like this. After all, those Supreme Dao Ancestors could not easily cultivate even a single Supreme Dao Ancestor. Perhaps in the legions under Invincible Dao Ancestors there might be one or two Supreme Dao Ancestors.
But for someone like Ye Tian, who could so easily cultivate six Supreme Dao Ancestors at once, that was practically unheard of.
Ye Tian was simply too wealthy. He was even willing to take out treasures like Forbidden Blood Crystals to cultivate his subordinates. If other Invincible Dao Ancestors obtained even a single one, they would be reluctant to use it on someone else and would try their best to use it themselves.
Not long afterward, those six Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors all broke through to the Supreme Dao Ancestor level.
Ye Tian had the Nine Extremes Legion divided into six great legions, with each Supreme Dao Ancestor taking command of one legion.
In addition, these six Supreme Dao Ancestors became the six Hall Masters of the human race, each ruling over one hall and managing the upper echelon of the human race.
With these six Supreme Dao Ancestors managing the human race, Ye Tian naturally had far fewer worries and could devote himself more wholeheartedly to cultivation.
Meanwhile, over these years he often went to comprehend the Eternal Origin Stone statue, and he possessed multiple Forbidden talents. Moreover, quite a few of those Forbidden talents were formed by stacking and merging the same kind of Forbidden talent, making them extremely powerful.
Because of that, his efficiency in comprehending the Forbidden Dao far surpassed that of everyone else.
It could even be said that even the Half-Step Domain Ancestors were far inferior to him in terms of comprehension efficiency.
Now, he had already cultivated one of his Forbidden Dao Techniques, Dark Extreme Dao Spear, to the major mastery realm, while his other Forbidden Dao Techniques had all reached the peak of minor mastery.
And according to what Ye Tian knew, many Half-Step Domain Ancestors only had Forbidden Dao Techniques at the entry level. Those who had reached the minor mastery level in a Forbidden Dao Technique could be counted on one’s fingers, while those Half-Step Domain Ancestors who had reached the major mastery level in a Forbidden Dao Technique seemed to be very, very few. Even Half-Step Domain Ancestors like Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor likely had not cultivated a single Forbidden Dao Technique to major mastery.
After all, these Half-Step Domain Ancestors did not possess Forbidden talents. For them, cultivating a Forbidden Dao Technique to major mastery was far too difficult. It was not something that could be accomplished just through enough time—this was a limitation of talent.
In addition, Ye Tian’s Endless Dao had also risen to nearly sixty percent, and was no longer too far from the ultimate limit of the Endless Dao.
And his Forbidden Dao was also far stronger than before, with quite a high level of attainment, though he had no idea how far he still was from the Myriad Realm. But the distance was certainly very great.
Based on Ye Tian’s own estimate, aside from the fact that his Endless Dao had not yet reached its limit and thus prevented him from advancing to the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm, in all other aspects he had already surpassed Invincible Dao Ancestors. His combat power had reached an inconceivable degree, likely comparable to invincible existences even among Invincible Dao Ancestors.
