Chapter 1238 The Stone Pupil Gate!

Chapter 1238: The Stone Pupil Gate
！
Palace Master Longying said, “Our Heavenly Emperor Palace possesses a supreme treasure called the Stone Pupil Gate. Once one enters the Stone Pupil Gate to cultivate, one hundred million years can pass inside while only an instant passes outside, and in total we can activate it for one hundred thousand instants.
The Stone Pupil Gate was refined using the eyeballs of the Forbidden creature Stone Pupil Beast, and originally there were seven stone pupils on the gate. Each time it is used, one stone pupil is consumed.
Back then, the first Heavenly Emperor used the Stone Pupil Gate, and the second Heavenly Emperor, Vast Sea Domain Ancestor, also used the Stone Pupil Gate.
In short, only those with great contributions are qualified to use the Stone Pupil Gate.
At present, there are only three stone pupils left on the Stone Pupil Gate, and ordinarily it must not be used lightly.
But now is an extraordinary time, so we are prepared to use the Stone Pupil Gate once!”
Stone Pupil Gate! The various palace masters were all incomparably shocked. They had never expected that the Heavenly Emperor Palace actually possessed such a treasure, and yet they had known nothing about it beforehand.
White Tiger Palace Master, however, was not surprised, because he knew of the Stone Pupil Gate. After all, he was the son of Vast Sea Domain Ancestor. Although he was only one among many offspring, he was also the most accomplished one, and so he knew many great secrets.
However, he had never seen the Stone Pupil Gate either, because the Stone Pupil Gate was simply too precious. It was one of the true trump cards of the Heavenly Emperor Palace. Aside from Vast Sea Domain Ancestor, no one else was allowed to enter the Stone Pupil Gate to cultivate.
Moreover, others could not enter the Stone Pupil Gate on their own either, because when entering the Stone Pupil Gate, one had to swear a life-bound oath that one was not entering it out of selfish motives. This was also to prevent any generation of Heavenly Emperor from abusing the Stone Pupil Gate and turning it into a discarded, useless object.
“Where is the Stone Pupil Gate?”
Azure Dragon Palace Master asked curiously.
The other palace masters also looked toward Palace Master Longying, waiting for his answer.
“There is no harm in telling you now!”
Palace Master Longying said, “The Stone Pupil Gate is not in the Heavenly Emperor Palace, because the time laws contained within the stone pupils on the Stone Pupil Gate are far too powerful, and ordinary formations simply cannot conceal the power of those stone pupil time laws.
If it were placed within the Heavenly Emperor Palace, it would be easily discovered by everyone. In that case, the Stone Pupil Gate would no longer remain a secret.
Therefore, the Stone Pupil Gate is hidden within a special spatiotemporal realm, and that spatiotemporal realm is fused together with the river of time and space of the Vast Sea Domain Realm.
Back then, when one-third of the Vast Sea Domain Realm was severed, the river of time and space was also cut apart.
Now, that Stone Pupil Spacetime Realm should have fused into the river of time and space of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, and it is constantly moving.
Without a special method, there is simply no way to find that spacetime realm!”
At this moment, Palace Master Leijie spoke, “Only the five of us palace masters know the secret art for locating the spacetime realm, and at least three palace masters must act together in order to determine the location of the spacetime realm. That is also why the five of us palace masters cannot lightly appear in the outside world, because once more than three of us fall, that spacetime realm would effectively disappear forever!”
But very soon, a problem arose for them—which one of them should enter the Stone Pupil Gate to cultivate? “I choose to give up. My potential is exhausted. Even if I were allowed to enter the Stone Pupil Gate to cultivate, I still would not be confident of reaching the Unity Realm!”
Palace Master Xuangui said.
After that, Palace Master Tiankong also chose to give up, because he likewise had no way of cultivating to the Unity Realm.
Although the Stone Pupil Gate could greatly accelerate cultivation speed and grant them countless years, if one lacked potential, then even with endless time it would still be very difficult to advance to the Unity Realm.
In theory, Half-Step Domain Ancestors could all attempt to reach the Domain Ancestor level, but that was only in theory.
If many Half-Step Domain Ancestors truly believed they could definitely advance to the Domain Ancestor level, then they would be far too foolish.
Many Half-Step Domain Ancestors have cultivated for extremely long ages.
So long that even their own will began to doubt themselves, their Dao hearts collapsed—such things are not unheard of.
Some Half-Step Domain Ancestors hid in desolate places and cultivated bitterly for countless hundreds of millions upon hundreds of millions of universes, only for their Dao hearts to collapse and for them to die.
Therefore, the vast majority of Half-Step Domain Ancestors had no hope of becoming Domain Ancestors.
“Palace Master Longying, you are the strongest, and you still have potential remaining. If you enter the Stone Pupil Gate, you should be able to reach the Unity Realm, perhaps even beyond the ordinary level!”
Palace Master Leijie suggested.
What followed was a vote—whether or not to let Palace Master Longying enter.
Palace Master Tianfa also wanted to enter, after all, this was a tremendous opportunity! But in the end, Palace Master Longying had the most supporters and won the chance to enter.
....Palace Master Longying, Palace Master Leijie, Palace Master Tianfa, Palace Master Xuangui, and Palace Master Tiankong—the five great palace masters—simultaneously cast a secret art to draw forth the spacetime realm from within the river of time and space. In this way, they could practically one hundred percent locate it.
Boom!!!! Time and space trembled, and a passage of time and space appeared.
In the perception of the many palace masters, a spacetime realm stood within the river of time and space.
Through that spacetime realm, they could even see a vast stone gate standing within it.
That stone gate was precisely the Stone Pupil Gate. On it were seven enormous stone pupils. Four of those pupils had already closed, leaving only three that still emitted Forbidden laws.
Palace Master Longying stepped into the spacetime passage, entered the spacetime realm, and then entered the Stone Pupil Gate.
Once Palace Master Longying had completely entered the Stone Pupil Gate, it closed, and one stone pupil slowly began to shut.
One instant! Two instants! Three instants!.... Time slowly passed. For the other palace masters, this short span of time was brief, yet with every instant that passed, Palace Master Longying had effectively bitterly cultivated for innumerable years within the Stone Pupil Gate.
Before they knew it, ten thousand instants had passed, and one stone pupil had completely closed, losing its law fluctuations and becoming an ordinary closed stone pupil.
Crack!!! The Stone Pupil Gate opened, and a figure radiating loneliness, indifference, and a violent aura stepped out.
“I’ve finally come out!”
Palace Master Longying sighed with emotion.
Cultivating alone within that dim space had been too lonely and too agonizing.
If he had not constantly been able to feel himself improving, there was no way he could have endured it.
But the final result was good! He had broken through. Both his Forbidden Dao and his physical body had reached the utmost perfect limit of the Myriad Realm, completing the unification of all things and achieving a complete transformation of his body. Moreover, his Forbidden Body had also been tempered to ninety-seven percent.
In addition, three of his Forbidden Dao Techniques had reached the major mastery realm, while all the others had reached the peak of minor mastery.
It could be said that he was now a true Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor, and not a weak one at that, but rather a relatively powerful Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
Even if he encountered the most top-tier Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestors, though he might not be able to defeat them, he would still be able to contend with them somewhat, and he would not be left completely powerless or be easily killed.
“Congratulations, Palace Master Longying!”
The various palace masters all offered their congratulations one after another.

Chapter 1239 The Crisis of the War God Tower!

Chapter 1239: The Crisis of the War God Tower
！
Palace Master Longying gave a slight nod, then dismissed the various palace masters.
In the time that followed, Palace Master Longying did not continue cultivating. He had cultivated for far too long, and his Dao heart had nearly developed problems, so he needed to relax properly.
Although Palace Master Longying had become a Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor, this matter did not cause any visible changes in the outside world. In fact, the outside world did not even know that the Heavenly Emperor Palace had someone called Palace Master Longying.
As time passed, more and more Forbidden treasures were born within the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, while no new small Forbidden Void Realms were born again. Only medium Forbidden Void Realms continued to appear one after another, seven or eight in total.
These Forbidden Void Realms were almost entirely divided up between the Heavenly Emperor Palace and Black Wind Mountain, while the other three major Ninth-Heaven forces no longer had the ability to seize any of them.
....As time flowed on, more and more Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors were born within the Xuanxu Ancient Realm.
In the past, it had been extremely, extremely difficult for a Dao Ancestor to condense Dark Forbidden Power. But now, there were many treasures that could allow Dao Ancestors to give birth to Dark Forbidden Power. For example, both Black Wind Mountain and the Heavenly Emperor Palace possessed quite a few such treasures, and even the three major Ninth-Heaven forces as well as some Eighth-Heaven forces had ways to cultivate a few Supreme Dao Ancestors.
In the past, the status of a Supreme Dao Ancestor had been incredibly high, almost like a ruler of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, but now it had become something commonplace.
Without the strength of an Invincible Dao Ancestor, one would not even dare act arrogantly anymore.
After all, more and more powerful beings kept appearing within the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, and even Half-Step Domain Ancestors seemed to emerge one after another. Any force without an Invincible Dao Ancestor in command or without a large number of Supreme Dao Ancestors might very well be destroyed at any moment.
And during this stretch of years, many forces that had only ordinary Dao Ancestors or Third- and Fourth-Heaven Dao Ancestors in command were wiped out one by one.
For example, if a Forbidden treasure land appeared near a certain force, that force might no longer exist by the next day.
On this day.
A Forbidden treasure land appeared near the territory of the War God Tower, and it was a large-scale Forbidden treasure land.
The value of a large Forbidden treasure land was far inferior to that of a Forbidden Void Realm, but it still attracted very, very many Dao Ancestors.
After all, a large Forbidden treasure land like this would at the very least produce more than ten Forbidden supreme treasures, as well as a huge number of Forbidden artifacts. No one was without need of Forbidden artifacts and Forbidden supreme treasures, and some Forbidden supreme treasures were of extremely high value, even being of enormous help to Invincible Dao Ancestors.
More importantly, this Forbidden treasure land was too close to the War God Tower.
Even if the people of the War God Tower wanted to withdraw at this moment, it was already too late, because other forces would suspect that the War God Tower had taken away some especially valuable Forbidden supreme treasures and would never simply let the War God Tower leave.
Of course, the main reason was still that the War God Tower was too weak.
Because the War God Tower had already been relatively weak before, it had gained virtually no benefits during the Forbidden Insect incident or from the Darkwing Roc Eagle, and it had not participated in the struggle for the Forbidden Void Realms, so its growth in strength had been relatively slow.
At present, the War God Tower only had a single Fifth-Heaven Dao Ancestor, several dozen Fourth-Heaven Dao Ancestors, and around three hundred-plus other Dao Ancestors. That was already many, many times stronger than it had once been.
But such strength was far too weak within the Xuanxu Ancient Realm and simply not worth mentioning. At best, it barely qualified as a Fifth-Heaven force.
At this moment.
A gloomy cloud hung over the War God Tower, for they had already sensed one powerful figure after another descending through the air, among them not only Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors but also Supreme Dao Ancestors.
“Tower Master, request protection from the Battle Heaven Sect!”
a Third-Heaven Dao Ancestor pleaded.
“It’s useless!”
The War God Tower Master said in despair, “The Battle Heaven Sect cannot protect us. Although we have submitted to the Battle Heaven Sect, the Battle Heaven Sect itself is only an Eighth-Heaven force and still has not given birth to a single Invincible Dao Ancestor.
If they tried to protect us, their losses would certainly be severe. They would not be so foolish!”
Just then.
A group of Dao Ancestors had already descended upon the War God Tower. This was a group of Sixth- and Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors. They were not in a hurry to enter the large Forbidden treasure land, but instead wanted to obtain benefits from the War God Tower first. They even wanted to capture some Dao Ancestors for later use in triggering great horrors.
There was no helping it—when one was weak, things were just like this, unable to determine one’s own fate.
“Everyone, our War God Tower truly has not entered that large Forbidden treasure land and has not obtained any treasures at all!”
the War God Tower Master hurriedly said.
In truth, the Dao Ancestors of the War God Tower had indeed entered that large Forbidden treasure land and had obtained quite a few Forbidden artifacts, but he had promptly ordered those Dao Ancestors back out.
But he absolutely did not dare tell these Dao Ancestors any of that.
“Hmph, we don’t know exactly when that large Forbidden treasure land was born. What if it had already appeared long ago, and you had already taken out all the good things?”
a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor said coldly.
Just as the War God Tower Master was about to explain, this group of Dao Ancestors attacked directly, unwilling to waste any words at all, because time was very important to them and there was no way they would waste it on the War God Tower.
Boom!!!! The strike of a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor slammed into the War God Tower’s protective grand formation. Yet this formation could only block the attacks of Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestors. Although it could also withstand a single strike from a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, it could only withstand one strike at most.
After that single blow, cracks spread across the War God Tower’s protective grand formation.
Then the other Dao Ancestors also attacked, instantly shattering the protective formation.
“I’ll fight you all to the death!”
The War God Tower Master burned all his flesh, blood, and soul, erupting with a full-force blow comparable to that of a Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor, and crashed toward that Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor.
0Yet all of it was futile.
That Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor blasted apart the War God Tower Master with just a single punch. The gap in strength between the two sides was simply too great. They were not on the same level at all.
The War God Tower Master had fallen! “Tower Master!”
One Dao Ancestor after another of the War God Tower, as well as the True Ancestors, cried out in despair.
Those Dao Ancestors did not immediately kill the people of the War God Tower. Instead, they planned to capture these Dao Ancestors. One could see them easily seize one Dao Ancestor after another and store them inside their inner worlds.
Among the many Dao Ancestors of the War God Tower, Dao Ancestor Yun Zi was considered one of the stronger ones. Because her fortune had been good and her potential very high, she was now already a Fourth-Heaven Dao Ancestor, the strongest Fourth-Heaven Dao Ancestor in the War God Tower, and in the future she had even been expected to take charge of the War God Tower.
But now she too was being targeted by a Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor. One could see the other party manifest a heaven-covering giant hand and grab toward her. That power was far beyond anything she had imagined. Even attacking with all her strength, she could not shake the opponent’s attack in the slightest.
“It’s over!”
Yun Zi Divine Maiden despaired.
But just at that moment, a spear pierced through the body of that Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor.
And within the void, one powerful Sixth- and Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor after another was pierced through by spear after spear.
In an instant, all the many Dao Ancestors who had come to invade the War God Tower were killed in seconds.
Whoosh! A figure appeared and came before Yun Zi Divine Maiden with a smile. “Yun Zi Divine Maiden, long time no see!”
Yun Zi Divine Maiden looked at that familiar face before her and said in shock, “Wanfa Dao Ancestor!”

Chapter 1240 The Great Terror Phantom That Attacks on Its Own!

Chapter 1240: The Great Terror Phantom That Attacks on Its Own
！
The Dao Ancestor who had suddenly appeared was none other than Ye Tian.
Ye Tian had led a group of Human Dao Ancestors here to this large forbidden treasure land to seize forbidden artifacts and forbidden supreme treasures, and just happened to sense that something had happened to the War God Tower, so he personally came over.
After all, he was at least acquainted with Divine Maiden Yun Zi. If he had not seen it, that would have been one thing, but now that he had, there was naturally no way he could ignore it....
。

Divine Maiden Yun Zi also left together with the Dao Ancestors of the War God Tower and did not take part in the struggle over the large forbidden treasure land.
After all, “Zero Four Seven”
in a place like a large forbidden treasure land, without the strength of a Sixth- or Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, one simply was not qualified to compete. In fact, even a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor had a high chance of falling there.
If she dared enter the large forbidden treasure land, the probability of her death was probably as high as ninety-nine percent.
As Divine Maiden Yun Zi flew through the air, she looked in the direction of the large forbidden treasure land and murmured inwardly, “Ye Tian, thank you!”
Ye Tian had saved her many times, yet she had nothing she could offer in return, and she felt deeply ashamed.
At the same time, she also sighed repeatedly.
Once upon a time, she had been a prodigy whose name stood alongside Ye Tian’s, yet now the gap between them had become so vast.
Back then, she could at least still see Ye Tian’s back, but now she could not even see his shadow anymore.
In Ye Tian’s eyes, even a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor who could casually kill the Tower Master of the War God Tower was merely an ant he could casually kill, which showed just how powerful Ye Tian had become.
Saving the people of the War God Tower was only a small interlude for Ye Tian. At this moment, he had already arrived at the large forbidden treasure land.
This large forbidden treasure land had the appearance of a water world. An endless ocean covered the entire forbidden treasure land, while scattered across the sea were isolated islands, each of which had given birth to many forbidden artifacts.
Thus, every single island was a target for the Dao Ancestors to fight over.
Ye Tian’s strength was incomparably great, so he easily gathered a large number of forbidden artifacts, and no one dared compete with him at all.
On a certain island within the large forbidden treasure land.
A forbidden supreme treasure had appeared, and the intense fluctuations of forbidden laws spread outward, drawing the attention of many Dao Ancestors, who all flew over at high speed.
Yet when they arrived, they discovered that things were not as they had imagined.
One Dao Ancestor corpse after another lay on the island, but there were no signs of battle at all, as though these Dao Ancestors had been erased by some invisible force.
This bizarre scene made many Dao Ancestors cautious, and they did not dare step onto the island lightly.
However, there were those who were not afraid of such a scene.
A Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor rushed onto the island, trying to seize that forbidden supreme treasure.
After all, forbidden supreme treasures were almost always the targets of Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors. As a mere Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, he had almost no chance of getting one under normal circumstances, and at the moment the Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors had not yet arrived—only Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors like them were here.
Therefore, if he could seize it first and then desperately flee, he had a very high chance of getting away alive.
In an instant, he arrived on the island and reached that forbidden supreme treasure.
This forbidden supreme treasure was a piece of black, round wood, three meters in diameter, and above the black wood there appeared a phantom image, seemingly that of a miniature roc.
This Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor knew that this forbidden supreme treasure would trigger a great terror, so he threw out a forbidden-bloodline creature from his inner world, trying to draw out the great terror.
When the forbidden-bloodline creature collided with the black wood, it disintegrated, and the great terror was triggered.
Yet what happened next was something this Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor had never anticipated.
The roc phantom stretched out one claw and directly grabbed at that Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor.
“How can this be....”
The Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor was dumbfounded.
Why would the great terror actively attack someone? Hadn’t it always only attacked whoever touched it?
Run! He wanted to flee, but under that illusory grab, his entire body seemed frozen solid, and he could not move in the slightest.
Whoosh! With one claw, this Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor’s body cracked apart, his soul collapsed, and he fell completely.
Outside the island.
Many Dao Ancestors sensed the death of that Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor and finally understood how the earlier Dao Ancestors had died—they had actually been directly erased by the great terror, and it had attacked on its own initiative.
This matter was far too strange! For a time, not a single Dao Ancestor dared step onto this island anymore.
Whoosh! A Supreme Dao Ancestor descended here, and when he saw that these Dao Ancestors had not entered the island, he was greatly puzzled... “What happened here? Why is no one entering the island to seize that forbidden supreme treasure?”
Supreme Dao Ancestor Xingluan asked.
“Dao Ancestor Xingluan, the great terror phantom drawn out by that forbidden supreme treasure actually attacks people directly. All the Dao Ancestors who entered the island were silently wiped out!”
A Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor explained.
“How is that possible!!!”
Xingluan Dao Ancestor found it hard to believe, but since everyone else said the same thing, he had no choice but to believe it.
At this moment, he was hesitating.
He was undoubtedly the strongest one here. If he managed to seize that forbidden supreme treasure, then it would definitely belong to him, and no one would be able to resist him.
But if he waited until other Supreme Dao Ancestors or Invincible Dao Ancestors arrived, then it would no longer be his.
Danger and opportunity coexisted! “I’m doing it!”
Xingluan Dao Ancestor gritted his teeth and decided.
Immediately, he made a sneak attack against some of the weaker Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors, binding them with streaks of starlight.
After all... these Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors were not Dao Ancestors from his own force, so killing them did not matter.
“Sorry!”
Xingluan Dao Ancestor thought to himself:。
Dozens of Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors were captured by Xingluan Dao Ancestor and brought onto the island.
Then Xingluan Dao Ancestor threw all these dozens of Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors toward that black wooden forbidden supreme treasure. At the same time, he also threw out a number of forbidden-bloodline creatures imprisoned in his inner world.
With so many Dao Ancestors and forbidden-bloodline creatures, he did not believe “2。
2” that they would not be enough to offset the great terror.
He believed that those Dao Ancestors had died earlier only because the great terror had been too powerful to offset, which had led to the great terror falling upon them and killing them.
“No!”
“Xingluan Dao Ancestor, may you die a miserable death!”
“If we die, Xingluan Dao Ancestor, you’ll die too!”
One Dao Ancestor after another cursed him with furious eyes.
Whoosh! The great terror was triggered. One Dao Ancestor after another had their bodies frozen and cracked apart, their souls instantly extinguished. Even those forbidden-bloodline creatures died in an instant.
Yet even so, the great terror still did not disappear.
Swish! An illusory claw struck toward Xingluan Dao Ancestor.
“Impossible!”
Xingluan Dao Ancestor completely panicked, unable to believe what was happening.
Pfft! The illusory claw ignored his defenses and his forbidden-weapon-grade defensive armor, passed directly through his body, and the light in his eyes gradually dimmed.

Chapter 1241 Jinsheng Dao Ancestor Severely Wounded!

Chapter 1241: Jinsheng Dao Ancestor Severely Wounded
！【Please Subscribe Fully】
Xingluan Dao Ancestor’s body stood motionless, and all signs of life completely dissipated.
Xingluan Dao Ancestor had fallen! Outside the isolated island, many Dao Ancestors were filled with fear.
What Xingluan Dao Ancestor had done earlier, ambushing so many Dao Ancestors, had indeed been despicable, but even with so many Dao Ancestors plus a whole pile of Forbidden bloodline creatures, they still had not been able to offset the Great Terror, and even Xingluan Dao Ancestor himself had been killed.
Xingluan Dao Ancestor had not been some mere Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, but an Eighth Heaven Supreme Dao Ancestor, and a rather powerful one at that! Even an ordinary Invincible Dao Ancestor would not dare claim they could kill such a powerful Supreme Dao Ancestor in a single strike; at the very least, it would take two moves to kill him.
Yet before the Great Terror, he had been killed in a single move, with absolutely no power to resist. Most likely, even if Xingluan Dao Ancestor had been several times stronger, the result would have been exactly the same.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!!! One Supreme Dao Ancestor after another, one Invincible Dao Ancestor after another, descended here, and the area outside the isolated island became lively.
Ye Tian also arrived here. One of the Human Dao Ancestors had informed him to come, because the situation here was simply too strange.
“Wanfa Dao Ancestor!”

Ye Tian asked.
Liuhuo Dao Ancestor said, “The power of the Great Terror triggered by this Forbidden supreme treasure is too terrifying. Whoever dares trigger it will die, and even Supreme Dao Ancestors cannot escape.
Under normal circumstances, the Great Terror only attacks the being that touches the Forbidden supreme treasure; it will not attack the surrounding people.
But this time it is different. Any Dao Ancestor who enters the range of the isolated island, even if they simply stand still, will be unable to escape as long as someone triggers the Great Terror.
Right now, no one dares enter the isolated island. Otherwise, if someone deliberately touches the Forbidden supreme treasure, everyone will die! Based on my understanding of Great Terror, the key reason is that the corresponding supreme treasure in the Dark Forbidden Domain is no ordinary thing, and the Forbidden creature guarding that treasure is unimaginably powerful. It can project a considerable portion of its power across countless regions of the Dark Forbidden Domain, and it can even attack autonomously.”
“A Forbidden creature capable of projecting a considerable amount of its power!”
Ye Tian also sensed just how troublesome the matter was.
Of course, if one was not interested in this Forbidden supreme treasure, then there would be no danger, because the power of the Great Terror could not extend beyond the isolated island.
But who would not want such a Forbidden supreme treasure! As time passed, more and more Invincible Dao Ancestors and Supreme Dao Ancestors gathered here, yet none of them dared casually trigger the Great Terror.
After all, one only had one life. Once one fell, no one could revive them.
“I’ll do it. I refuse to believe that a mere Great Terror can kill us Invincible Dao Ancestors!”
An Invincible Dao Ancestor suddenly spoke.
Everyone looked over and saw that it was the Invincible Dao Ancestor of Vajra City—Jinsheng Dao Ancestor! Back when Jinsheng Dao Ancestor was still a Supreme Dao Ancestor, he already had the title of invincible in the flesh. Although he was not as strong as Yan Ancestor or Xuanhu Dao Ancestor and the like, his strength was still quite formidable. Now that he had advanced to the Invincible Dao Ancestor level, his combat power was only average among Invincible Dao Ancestors, but his defensive power and survival ability were considered top-tier.
Therefore, he had great confidence in his own ability to preserve his life.
Others did not dare go in, but if he went in and withstood the Great Terror, then he could easily take away the Forbidden supreme treasure.
“Jinsheng Dao Ancestor truly has courage. Don’t worry, if you really do withstand the Great Terror, I will not compete with you for that Forbidden supreme treasure!”
An Invincible Dao Ancestor said.
One after another, more Invincible Dao Ancestors also declared that they would not seize the Forbidden supreme treasure, though still quite a number of Invincible Dao Ancestors gave no statement at all.
Jinsheng Dao Ancestor did not care too much. Even if some Invincible Dao Ancestors wanted to rob him, it would not be that easy for them to kill him.
He had complete confidence in his ability to escape.
Whoosh! Jinsheng Dao Ancestor stepped onto the isolated island and arrived before the piece of black wood, staring at the roc phantom with a solemn expression.
“Go!”
Jinsheng Dao Ancestor threw out one Forbidden bloodline creature after another, all of which he had captured earlier. After all, although Invincible Dao Ancestors could ignore the Great Terror of Forbidden artifacts, they still found it difficult to contend with the Great Terror of Forbidden supreme treasures, so they often captured Forbidden bloodline creatures as bait. Naturally, he had quite a few such creatures on him.
He threw out approximately several hundred Forbidden bloodline creatures to trigger the Great Terror power contained in that piece of black wood.
Boom!!!! The power of the Great Terror was triggered.
Puff puff puff!!! One Forbidden bloodline creature after another exploded and instantly fell dead. Then one claw of the illusory roc extended toward Jinsheng Dao Ancestor. The speed was too fast, and a suppressive force acted on Jinsheng Dao Ancestor, making it hard for him to move.
With a ripping sound! Jinsheng Dao Ancestor was struck by a terrifying force, which continuously destroyed his body and even injured his soul.
“Not good!”
Jinsheng Dao Ancestor was greatly alarmed. He knew clearly that if he did not flee now, there was no way he would survive.
At once, he used a life-saving treasure to forcibly break free from the restraint and escaped to the outside of the isolated island. The attack of the Great Terror did not continue pursuing him anymore.
Outside the isolated island.
Jinsheng Dao Ancestor’s so-called invincible fleshly body kept cracking and healing. He himself was coughing up blood continuously, his inner world was nearly collapsing, and his soul had also suffered grievous injury. His wounds could be described as extremely severe, and less than twenty percent of his combat power could now be brought into play.
Seeing this scene, many Invincible Dao Ancestors were shocked.
Jinsheng Dao Ancestor’s survival 07 ability and defensive ability were so powerful, yet he still ended up in such a miserable state. Wouldn’t ordinary Invincible Dao Ancestors be killed in a single strike? And if Jinsheng Dao Ancestor had not fled, he probably would have died as well.
From this, it could be seen that even top-tier Invincible Dao Ancestors could not contend with this kind of Great Terror. Only Half-Step Domain Ancestors could withstand such a Great Terror.
But this time, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors had not come, because a mere large Forbidden Void Realm was not enough to attract them.
There were simply too many opportunities in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm. No one knew how many opportunities the Half-Step Domain Ancestors had already obtained, and they were all using every bit of time to cultivate and increase their strength. Unless it was a truly great opportunity, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors were not too willing to come out.
Moreover, the Dao Ancestors present also did not want to inform the Half-Step Domain Ancestors, because if they did, then how would there still be any share left for them? “How about this: everyone gathers enough Forbidden bloodline creatures, then together we trigger the Great Terror. I refuse to believe that the power of the Great Terror is inexhaustible.
Once the power of the Great Terror is exhausted, everyone can then fairly compete for this Forbidden supreme treasure. How about it?”
Liuhuo Dao Ancestor proposed.
“Agreed, that’s a good method!”
“I agree too!”
“Agreed!”
Many Invincible Dao Ancestors immediately agreed, while only very few Supreme Dao Ancestors echoed them, because they did not dare. Their strength was too weak, and they did not dare take such a risk.

Chapter 1242 No Longer Hiding!

Chapter 1242: No Longer Hiding
！【Please Subscribe Fully】
“I agree as well!”
Ye Tian said.
He was not afraid of the Great Terror. In terms of survival ability, he was confident he was above Jinsheng Dao Ancestor. Since even Jinsheng Dao Ancestor had managed to escape, he naturally would have no problem at all.
And in terms of strength, he was even confident that he could battle somewhat against a weaker Half-Step Domain Ancestor....,.... so why would he fear some so-called Great Terror?
Next, these Dao Ancestors began searching this large forbidden treasure land for forbidden bloodline creatures. There were quite a few forbidden bloodline creatures here, and together with the forbidden bloodline creatures they had already suppressed earlier, they could gather a huge number of them.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!!! One Invincible Dao Ancestor after another, along with a few Supreme Dao Ancestors, sprang into action.
As for the other Dao Ancestors, they did not continue staying here, but instead went elsewhere to search for forbidden artifacts.
After all... they were not qualified to compete for this Forbidden supreme treasure. If they wasted time here, then the forbidden artifacts of this large forbidden treasure land would all be swept away by other Dao Ancestors, so naturally they had to leave and quickly go search for forbidden artifacts.
Time passed bit by bit.
Very soon, one Invincible Dao Ancestor after another arrived at this isolated island again, and Ye Tian had also returned.
Everyone was extremely nervous, because if anything unexpected happened, someone might very well fall here.
“Let’s begin!”
One Supreme Dao Ancestor after another, one Invincible Dao Ancestor after another, threw forbidden bloodline creatures toward that black-wood Forbidden supreme treasure.
Boom!!!! The Great Terror was triggered. Dense masses of forbidden bloodline creatures seemed to be frozen in place, and illusory claws swept across their bodies, quickly killing them all in seconds.
Then, one claw after another reached toward the Invincible Dao Ancestors and several Supreme Dao Ancestors.
Since it was attacking many Invincible Dao Ancestors at once, the power of each illusory claw was naturally not at its full strength.
The Dao Ancestors could not simply sit and wait for death, so they all erupted with their full power, trying to attack these illusory claws. Their power also slightly affected the strength of the illusory claws, so it was not as though it had no effect at all.
Yet these illusory claws still pierced through the bodies of one Dao Ancestor after another. Even Ye Tian was unable to avoid them and was struck by an illusory claw as well.
Boom!!!! A terrifying power invaded Ye Tian’s body, continuously destroying his flesh. Even his Forbidden Body seemed terribly weak before this force, and his body was being destroyed bit by bit, only for the damage to be offset and repaired in time by the power of Forbidden Origin.
Ye Tian suffered only light injuries! But the others were not so fortunate. One Invincible Dao Ancestor after another was seriously wounded, while three Supreme Dao Ancestors fell, and even one Invincible Dao Ancestor with poor life-preserving ability also fell.
Four people died in an instant! Then that illusory roc launched another attack on the crowd, and one illusory claw after another swept toward them.
This time, another person fell, and several Invincible Dao Ancestors were already gravely injured and no longer dared remain here, fleeing instantly.
“How can this be? Could it be that this Great Terror is endless?”
Many Invincible Dao Ancestors felt panic in their hearts.
If the Great Terror could not be neutralized, they simply did not dare go take the Forbidden supreme treasure—otherwise, whoever touched it would die.
But soon, the Invincible Dao Ancestors discovered that the power of the Great Terror had weakened greatly and was now much weaker than before.
Just like that, the Invincible Dao Ancestors forcibly resisted the power of the Great Terror, continuously weakening it until its power became smaller and smaller.
Before long, the power of the Great Terror could no longer pose a threat to the many Dao Ancestors.
Just as the many Invincible Dao Ancestors shifted their attention to that Forbidden supreme treasure and no longer focused on the Great Terror, a sudden change erupted.
Boom!!!!! A terrifying power spread out from the Forbidden supreme treasure, forming a special domain that enveloped the entire isolated island.
This domain contained unique Forbidden laws, seemingly some form of spatial laws, and in an instant it sealed off the entire island.
One Invincible Dao Ancestor tried to use some treasure of the escape type to flee, but it failed.
“Damn it, we can’t escape anymore!”
that Invincible Dao Ancestor said in despair.
Anyone could see that something had gone terribly wrong. Yet no matter how they tried to flee, it was useless. Even flying out by ordinary means did not work—the space where the isolated island was located seemed to have been stretched infinitely.
It was just like Sun Wukong being unable to escape the palm of Buddha’s hand: no matter how far one flew, it was still futile.
Within the domain, a gigantic creature appeared. It resembled an enlarged roc and looked somewhat similar to the Darkwing Roc Eagle that had once fallen in the Dark Forbidden Domain, though in reality it was not the same species.
This roc was pitch-black all over, possessed sixty-six claws, and its eyes shone golden.
At this moment, it was as if the roc’s true body had descended, and the terrifying aura of a Forbidden creature spread out, causing everyone’s hearts to tremble.
“How can this be? This is a Forbidden creature!”
The Invincible Dao Ancestors thought in fear.
“This is a projection!”
Liuhuo Dao Ancestor said bitterly, “It’s just that this Forbidden creature is far too powerful. Even across an immeasurably vast distance, the power of its projection is still comparable to that of a Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
Moreover, it should be extremely proficient in spatial laws, which is why it can project a wisp of consciousness here. This should be a Great Terror projection avatar containing a trace of consciousness!”
No one could imagine what kind of unimaginably powerful Forbidden creature it would take for a mere trace of a projection to possess the strength of a Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
“.
Let’s attack together. If we don’t kill it, we’re all going to die!”
an Invincible Dao Ancestor proposed.
Boom!!!! The roc creature attacked, leaving these Dao Ancestors no time to think.
In an instant, the two sides clashed.
Facing this roc projection creature with Half-Step Domain Ancestor combat power, the many Invincible Dao Ancestors were simply no match for it, and one after another they were heavily wounded and sent flying.
However, fortunately this was only a projection, and its defense was not very strong, so with the many Invincible Dao Ancestors unleashing their trump cards, they were still able to barely contend with the roc projection creature.
Yet the gap in strength between the two sides was simply too great, and casualties quickly appeared.
Aside from Ye Tian, the other several Supreme Dao Ancestors all fell one after another, and the weaker Invincible Dao Ancestors also quickly died as well.
Suddenly.
The roc projection creature swiped one claw toward the already heavily wounded Liuhuo Dao Ancestor. The void around “that Zhao” solidified, making it difficult for Liuhuo Dao Ancestor to break free, while the Forbidden defensive armor on his body had long since been shattered, and his life-saving treasures were almost all exhausted.
He might not be able to withstand this strike.
Just as the claw was about to descend, a spear suddenly blocked the roc projection creature, and a figure stood in front of Liuhuo Dao Ancestor.
This person was Ye Tian! “Many thanks, Wanfa Dao Ancestor!”
Liuhuo Dao Ancestor said gratefully.
Ye Tian said nothing and instead directly began fighting with this roc projection creature.
At this moment, he no longer needed to hide his strength.
If he could already battle a Half-Step Domain Ancestor, then that alone was enough to place him at the Half-Step Domain Ancestor level. And with Black Wind Mountain as his backing, what did he still need to fear? Boom!!!! Ye Tian and the roc projection creature fought continuously, and this level of battle power completely stunned everyone.

Chapter 1244 An 84% Forbidden Body! Plea..

Chapter 1244: An 84% Forbidden Body
！【Please Subscribe Fully】
The Extreme Dao inheritance was extremely complete. It could be said that as long as one’s talent was sufficient, one’s potential was sufficient, and one’s resources were sufficient, one could step into the Extreme Dao realm.
Other Invincible Dao Ancestors might not be able to cultivate to the Extreme Dao realm, but Ye Tian felt that it should not be a problem for him.
Moreover, that black piece of wood he had obtained this time was actually a spiritwood of the highest Forbidden supreme treasure grade, and one of the absolute top tier, capable of tempering the Forbidden Body. Even for a major-completion Forbidden Body, it still had a very powerful tempering effect.
Otherwise, Ye Tian had no idea how many years it would take for him to raise his Forbidden Body to the tenfold perfect great completion realm.
However, he was also very clear that if others did not possess his Copying Talent, then wanting to walk the path of the Extreme Dao would be far too difficult.
Even for his own loved ones, there was not much hope of walking the path of the Extreme Dao.
Therefore, for now he did not plan to tell his loved ones about the path of the Extreme Dao. Otherwise, if they insisted on taking that path and ended up achieving nothing, or even slowing down their growth, then that would be completely unnecessary.
If in the future Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and his wife Xiao Yue, among others, had hope of walking the path of the Extreme Dao, then he would pass the Extreme Dao inheritance on to them.
Ye Tian took out the black wood, shaved off a bit of wood dust, then ground it into powder. Only then could it be refined; otherwise, this black wood would be very difficult to refine.
Boom!!! The powder was refined by Ye Tian and transformed into an incomparably pure energy that continuously tempered Ye Tian’s Forbidden Body.
Originally, once Ye Tian’s Forbidden Body had reached 80%, progress had become very slow, and no matter how many Forbidden artifacts he used, he had no way to continue tempering his Forbidden Body.
But now, after refining this black powder, Ye Tian’s Forbidden Body began to improve again. The tempering effect was simply too good.
At this rate, it would not take long for Ye Tian’s Forbidden Body to reach 81%.
And his Forbidden Dao Power was also being continuously tempered, with an extremely good effect.
In addition, the Extreme Dao inheritance also contained secret arts specifically for refining the purity of Forbidden Dao Power.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian continuously tempered his Forbidden Body and cultivated the secret arts of the Extreme Dao inheritance, and time passed very quickly.
In the blink of an eye, it was... tens of thousands of years later.
At this time, Ye Tian’s Forbidden Body had already been tempered to 84%, while the black wood had only been consumed by one-thousandth, % in total.
From this, it was easy to see just how enormous the value of this black wood was. And this black wood was clearly the凝聚 formed projection of some supreme treasure from the Dark Forbidden Domain. For example, that Roc Ancestor possessed a similar treasure to the black wood, except one whose value exceeded this black wood by no one knew how many times.
“As the Forbidden Body is tempered further and further, it becomes increasingly difficult. This black wood probably won’t be enough to fully temper my Forbidden Body to the tenfold perfect level. In the future, I’ll have to seek out top-grade cultivation-type Forbidden supreme treasures before my Forbidden Body can reach tenfold perfect completion!”
Ye Tian murmured.
After that, Ye Tian frequently entered Wind Mountain to contemplate the Eternal Origin Stone statue, comprehending the Forbidden Dao and the Endless Dao, so that he could bring the Endless Dao to its limit as soon as possible and thereby step into the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm.
Only by stepping into the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm could he undergo another transformation and reach an extremely terrifying level, at which point he would no longer need to worry much about his own safety.
Heavenly Emperor Palace.
Golden Crow Palace Master and Azure Dragon Palace Master were discussing a major matter—a major matter aimed at Black Wind Mountain.
Previously, Black Wind Mountain had repeatedly seized opportunities from the Heavenly Emperor Palace, causing the Heavenly Emperor Palace no small amount of losses.
Now that Palace Master Longying had stepped into the Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor level, the Heavenly Emperor Palace no longer needed to fear Black Wind Mountain in either top-tier combat strength or overall foundation.
And this time, the subject they were discussing was Ye Tian.
Inside the large Forbidden treasure land, Ye Tian had fought a roc projection creature comparable to a Half-Step Domain Ancestor and displayed terrifying combat power.
Even if Ye Tian was still inferior to a true Half-Step Domain Ancestor, the actual gap was already not that great anymore.
A Supreme Dao Ancestor comparable to a Half-Step Domain Ancestor—what an utterly terrifying matter this was.
Golden Crow Palace Master and Azure Dragon Palace Master had never heard of such a thing even in the Divine Heaven Domain, and so they were extremely wary of Ye Tian.
“Wanfa Dao Ancestor must be killed. Otherwise, once he steps into the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm, it will become difficult to kill him!”
Golden Crow Palace Master proposed.
“Exactly!”
Azure Dragon Palace Master nodded. “His Dao is very powerful. Wanting to raise it to the ultimate level will probably be very difficult and will take an extremely long time, but we can no longer give.... him time.
Before, he was not especially strong, so we did not pay enough attention to him....
But now we must take him seriously. Otherwise, once he fully rises, he will pose a huge threat to our Heavenly Emperor Palace!”
Golden Crow Palace Master kept looking through the intelligence regarding Ye Tian, then said coldly, “Judging from the information, Wanfa Dao Ancestor is very likely the same person as Dark King, and Dark King is most likely... the former Nine Extremes Heavenly King.
Previously, you all said that Nine Extremes Heavenly King could not possibly have grown this fast, and believed Dark King was one of the ancient Ten Kings. But in truth, your intelligence was wrong! Since even Wanfa Dao Ancestor can grow this fast, then naturally Nine Extremes Heavenly King can as well!”
“But Dark King and Nine Extremes Heavenly King have appeared at the same time before, and Dark King didn’t seem like a clone!”
Azure Dragon Palace Master frowned.
0“What do you know? No one knows how many secrets of the Dark Forbidden Domain remain beyond our understanding. If there exists some special cloning talent, that would not be strange at all!”
Golden Crow Palace Master said. “We cannot track Dark King’s whereabouts, but Wanfa Dao Ancestor’s movements are very easy to track.
I propose that we immediately launch an assassination against Wanfa Dao Ancestor. Once Wanfa Dao Ancestor is killed, it will certainly cause enormous losses to Black Wind Mountain.
But we will only have one chance to strike. Once Wanfa Dao Ancestor notices something, then wanting to kill him afterward will become difficult!”
“Who should we send?”
Azure Dragon Palace Master hesitated.
“You go personally!”
Golden Crow Palace Master ordered. “Wanfa Dao Ancestor’s combat power is close to that of a weaker Half-Step Domain Ancestor. If the other palace masters go to assassinate Wanfa Dao Ancestor, they will also have difficulty killing him.
But you have the strength to kill weaker Half-Step Domain Ancestors, and if several other Half-Step Palace Masters join forces with you, then in a short amount of time you should be able to kill Wanfa Dao Ancestor.
As for me, I will be responsible for intercepting the Half-Step Domain Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain who come to rescue him.
If necessary, Palace Master Longying and the others will also take action.
If this time we can kill Wanfa Dao Ancestor and then kill several Half-Step Domain Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain as well, that would truly be perfect!”
“Then let’s proceed according to this plan!”
Azure Dragon Palace Master agreed.
However, the Heavenly Emperor Palace never found a suitable opportunity.
During these years, Ye Tian had always been cultivating either in Wind Mountain or in the Human Realm, and the Human Realm was a medium Forbidden Void Realm. Even Half-Step Domain Ancestors could not invade it, so there was no way to launch an attack. They could only slowly wait for an opportunity刀。

Chapter 1245 Breakthrough, Invincible Dao Ancestor! Plea..

Chapter 1245: Breakthrough, Invincible Dao Ancestor
！【Please Subscribe Fully】
On this day.
Ye Tian received a transmission message. It came from Ouyang Jiuer.
“The Heavenly Emperor Palace wants to kill me?”
Ye Tian was a little surprised.
Moreover, it was the Half-Step Domain Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace who were planning to assassinate him, and several of them were going to strike together. Once they acted, they would leave him no chance of survival.
“Where did Jiuer get this information?”
Ye Tian was very curious.
All along, Ouyang Jiuer seemed to understand the Heavenly Emperor Palace extremely well. She even appeared to know every one of its plans like the back of her hand.
Yet this time, the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s plan was clearly something only Half-Step Domain Ancestors should know, and Ouyang Jiuer still knew about it.
“Could it be that Jiuer has an intelligence contact at the Half-Step Domain Ancestor level inside the Heavenly Emperor Palace? Who could it be?”
Ye Tian was somewhat curious.
If his guess was right, then Ouyang Jiuer’s identity was definitely no ordinary one. Otherwise, a Half-Step Domain Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace would never have leaked such information “Zero Four Seven”
to her.
“Last time, I exposed my combat strength on the isolated island in the forbidden treasure land. The Heavenly Emperor Palace should already know that my battle power is only a step below that of a Half-Step Domain Ancestor. If they launch an ambush, they will definitely treat me as a true Half-Step Domain Ancestor. Once they attack, they will absolutely try to kill me!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Black Wind Mountain was powerful, but its Half-Step Domain Ancestors could not protect him at all times. And ordinary Half-Step Domain Ancestors were not powerful enough to protect him anyway. Only someone like Miaofa Dao Ancestor could barely manage it.
And in fact, Miaofa Dao Ancestor was not especially powerful either. She could only be considered half a Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor. If the Heavenly Emperor Palace sent out a true Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor, even Miaofa Dao Ancestor would not be able to protect him.
Therefore, he had to rely on himself. As long as he was strong enough, the Heavenly Emperor Palace would not dare to casually make a move against him.
“I must break through to the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm as quickly as possible!”
Ye Tian thought.
At present, his Endless Dao had already reached eighty-three percent. As long as he continued to focus all his effort on comprehending the Endless Dao, it would not be difficult for him to bring it to its limit.
“The people of the Heavenly Emperor Palace think that for me to rise to the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm would probably require a very long time. But what they do not know is that Black Wind Mountain possesses the Eternal Origin Stone statue, and I have always been able to comprehend it. On top of that, my talent is good enough. To advance to Invincible Dao Ancestor does not require endless ages! Hmph, once I step into the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm, if the Half-Step Domain Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace dare to ambush me, they will be the ones who suffer!”
Ye Tian murmured.
From then on, he spent most of his time inside the Wind Mountain comprehension tower for the Eternal Origin Stone statue.
He had many contribution points, and on top of that he possessed countless resources, enough to exchange for plenty more points, so he could spend a long time comprehending the Eternal Origin Stone statue.
Thus, year after year passed by.
The Heavenly Emperor Palace kept watching the situation of the human race, yet Ye Tian simply never came out, so they assumed he was in seclusion and suspected nothing. After all, it was perfectly normal for Dao Ancestors to enter secluded cultivation.
In addition, Ye Tian also had his family members cultivate in seclusion and do their best not to leave the Human Realm.
After all, Ye Tian was also afraid that the Heavenly Emperor Palace might target his loved ones and use them to lure him out.
So Ye Tian had his loved ones remain in seclusion as well. That way, it would be much safer.
Under Ye Tian’s all-out effort to improve his Endless Dao, his progress was extremely rapid. After all, he had temporarily given up cultivation in all other aspects and focused almost entirely on the Endless Dao, so roughly every ten thousand years he could raise his Endless Dao by one percent.
Thus, ten thousand years passed, then another ten thousand years.
After more than a hundred thousand years had passed, on this day Ye Tian finally comprehended the Endless Dao to its ultimate limit.
“At last, I can break through!”
Ye Tian murmured.
Boom!!!! The Endless Dao at its limit connected with the origin of the Chaos Great Dao. Ye Tian’s body, his Endless Dao at the ultimate limit, and the origin of the Chaos Great Dao seemed to merge into one, bringing about a tremendous transformation in his entire body.
Crack!!!! An invisible bottleneck was shattered, and boundless origin power surged into Ye Tian’s body, helping him continuously change the very essence of his flesh.
His Supreme Body was now transforming into the Ultimate Body, representing the very limit of a Dao Ancestor, far more powerful than the Supreme Body.
Moreover, the Dao Power, soul, and physical strength of an Invincible Dao Ancestor all far surpassed those of a Supreme Dao Ancestor. Only a few exceptionally rare Supreme Dao Ancestors could compare to weaker Invincible Dao Ancestors.
Under normal circumstances, an Invincible Dao Ancestor could easily kill a Supreme Dao Ancestor.
But Ye Tian had now broken through, and his aura was continuously rising. His physical strength, soul strength, and Forbidden Dao Power were all skyrocketing, as though he had broken through an entire major realm.
Because Ye Tian’s foundation was simply too deep, it seemed that even the power of Chaos Origin was not enough to complete his breakthrough in one go.
So Ye Tian took out an enormous amount of cultivation-type Forbidden artifacts, shattered them, turned them into Forbidden energy, and poured them into his inner world. He also mobilized Forbidden Origin Power to complete the transformation of his body... Just like that, time slowly passed.
One day! Two days! Three days!.... Ye Tian’s breakthrough took place in the Human Realm, so the outside world did not know. Even Black Wind Mountain did not know that he had broken through.
This breakthrough lasted a full six months, consuming countless resources from Ye Tian before the transformation was finally completed.
“My strength....”
Ye Tian slightly sensed it, and was immediately overjoyed.
He was now far, far stronger than before.... His whole being had undergone an entirely new qualitative transformation.
If the Ye Tian at the Supreme Dao Ancestor level had merely been comparable to a weaker Half-Step Domain Ancestor, then now his battle power probably already surpassed that of Azure Dragon Palace Master and might even be enough to rival Half-Step Domain Ancestors like Golden Crow Palace Master and Miaofa Dao Ancestor.
More importantly, he had only just broken through to Invincible Dao Ancestor, and he still had tremendous room for improvement.
Once he cultivated the Nine Extremes Dao Hall, stabilized his cultivation, improved his Forbidden Dao Power, soul strength, and physical strength, then further strengthened his Forbidden Body, and cultivated the Extreme Dao inheritance—
at that point, his strength would still increase by a considerable margin.
By then, even if his battle power still fell short of a Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor, the gap would not be very large.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian remained extremely low-key. He did not publicize his breakthrough, but instead honestly stabilized his realm and improved his cultivation and strength.
Thus, another ten thousand years passed.
And after ten thousand years of bitter cultivation, Ye Tian’s realm had long since stabilized “2。
2” and his cultivation had grown somewhat as well.
Moreover, because he had broken through to the Invincible Dao Ancestor realm, Ye Tian’s Forbidden Body had also improved. It had now been tempered to eighty-seven percent. If he kept working hard, it would not take too long before it could reach ninety percent tempering.
In addition, his Forbidden Dao Techniques had basically all advanced to the major mastery realm.
“It is time to go out and lure the Heavenly Emperor Palace into making its move!”
Ye Tian decided.
However, he was not going to send out his true body, but rather create a copy of his own body and send that copy out under his identity. That way, even if the copied body was killed, it would not affect him much.
This was the safest method. After all, he did not know whether the Heavenly Emperor Palace would go all out to kill him, and if that happened, then even battle power at the Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor level might not be fully reliable.
One only had one life, so naturally he had to be cautious.

This time, the deaths of Palace Master Tianlang and Palace Master Xingkong truly shocked the entire Heavenly Emperor Palace.
Many people found it impossible to imagine that two Half-Step Domain Ancestors had actually fallen at the hands of Wanfa Dao Ancestor. Quite a few Supreme Dao Ancestors and Invincible Dao Ancestors had dealt with Wanfa Dao Ancestor before, and they all admitted that Wanfa Dao Ancestor was indeed formidable.
But no matter how formidable, he should not have reached the level of killing two Half-Step Domain Ancestors, right? And this time, five Half-Step Domain Ancestors had joined forces to assassinate Wanfa Dao Ancestor—even Azure Dragon Palace Master had personally acted—yet they still were not his match.
Heavenly Emperor Palace main hall.
Palace Master Longying was in a very bad mood, and the other palace masters were equally displeased.
“Wanfa Dao Ancestor has already become fully established. It will be difficult to kill him now!”
Xuangui Palace Master spoke.
“Yes, Wanfa Dao Ancestor’s strength should be infinitely close to that of a Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor, and he knows multiple Forbidden Dao Techniques. More importantly, he only recently broke through to the Invincible Dao Ancestor level, so he still has considerable room for improvement.
Probably before long, he will truly possess the battle power of a Myriad Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor.
At that point, killing him will become far too difficult! Unless Palace Master Longying personally assassinates him, only then could he be easily killed!”
Palace Master Leijie said.
“Forget it. For now, do not target Wanfa Dao....
Our ultimate mission is still to promote the Xuanxu Ancient Realm into a Supreme Sacred Realm, or even a Forbidden Realm. Once the Forbidden Realm is successfully born, then we will be able to guide Haohai Domain Ancestor here.
At that time, what Wanfa Dao Ancestor, what Wind Mountain Lord—they will all be ants!”
Palace Master Longying said.
All the palace masters nodded one after another, fully agreeing with Palace Master Longying’s words.
They worshiped and respected Haohai Domain Ancestor immensely. Before Haohai Domain Ancestor, even the strongest Unity Realm Half-Step Domain Ancestor was merely an ant. What ability would they have to resist? Even if Wanfa Dao Ancestor were allowed to continue growing, could he really grow to the Domain Ancestor level? Difficult! Far too difficult! Therefore, they did not necessarily need to kill Wanfa Dao Ancestor right now.
Palace Master Longying then shifted the topic to how to develop and strengthen the Heavenly Emperor Palace, no longer discussing Wanfa Dao Ancestor Ye Tian.
....The Daoshan Realm Domain was vast, incomparably vast, and the Xuanxu Ancient Realm only occupied a small region of it, utterly unable to compare with the entire realm domain.
Because of this, the total number of living beings in the Daoshan Realm Domain was simply too great...., and there were also many remote regions.
On this day.
Somewhere within the Daoshan Realm Domain, a universe stood there.
Suddenly.
A figure appeared there and stared at this universe excitedly. “Hehe, I’ve found another universe without much of a background. Once I devour this universe, my strength can rise another tiny bit.
How many universes have I devoured by now again? Ah, I remember now—seems like more than the thirty-thousandth universe!”
The moment his voice fell, he opened his mouth and sucked, and this universe instantly turned into a tiny sphere that entered his mouth... Then the universe collapsed and transformed into boundless energy, which he devoured completely.
As for the countless living beings inside the universe, they also perished because of this! This person then left that region and went to look for the next universe. Occasionally, when he passed by some Chaotic Continents, he devoured them directly as well.
In short, he only devoured universes and Chaotic Continents.
He had already been doing this for many years.
Of course, he was not stupid. He would not devour those universes and Chaotic Continents that belonged to and were valued by major forces, because that would make him very easy to discover.
But nothing was absolute. No matter how careful he was, on this day something still went wrong.
Just as he was devouring a Chaotic Continent, a young man suddenly manifested a phantom figure from his body, which was clearly the imprint of an Invincible Dao Ancestor.
Evidently, this young man was some named disciple or similar figure under an Invincible Dao Ancestor.
“Who are you, to dare devour this Chaotic Continent? Don’t you know that this is a Chaotic Continent under our Myriad Domain Temple!”
that Invincible Dao Ancestor said coldly.
“Noisy!”
The mysterious man let out a cold snort, the phantom shattered, and that young man completely fell as well.
But soon, this mysterious figure left that place and vanished without a trace.
Myriad Domain Temple.
Half-Moon Dao Ancestor was extremely furious. He had discovered a promising seedling in the Daoshan Realm Domain, one whose talent was very high. Even in a barren place like a Chaotic Continent, that person had still been able to cultivate to the True Ancestor level in a short amount of time. “2。”
His potential was astonishingly high.
Half-Moon Dao Ancestor had planned that before long, he would guide the young man into the Xuanxu Ancient Realm. With proper nurturing, within one hundred thousand years it would be enough to raise him to the Invincible Dao Ancestor level, and there might even be a slight hope of impacting the Supreme True Ancestor level.
Yet now, his named disciple had fallen, and it had been because some mysterious person had devoured the Chaotic Continent he was on.
Under normal circumstances, powerful experts did not deliberately devour weaker living beings—aside from cases where collateral damage from battle was unavoidable.
But intentionally devouring an entire Chaotic Continent was equivalent to cutting off the source of future geniuses! This kind of behavior was basically forbidden by all the major powers, and once discovered, it would definitely be harshly punished.
“Which power’s Dao Ancestor did this exactly?”
Half-Moon Dao Ancestor dispatched a batch of Dao Ancestors to investigate, but the results of the investigation very quickly left everyone utterly astonished.
